// PREMIUM HERO BANNER V4 -  WITH AVATAR & FOLLOW
// ============================================
function PremiumHeroBannerV4({ hero, isFollowing, followerCount, onFollow }: any) {
const [bannerType, setBannerType] = useState<'video' |  'image'>('image' );
const [videoMuted, setVideoMuted] = useState(true);
const videoRef = useRef<HTMLVideoElement>(null);

// ✅ v17.0: Extract images
let bannerUrl = getImageUrl(hero.images?.banner) ||  getImageUrl(hero.images?.featured) ||
DEFAULT_BANNER;
let avatarUrl = getImageUrl(hero.images?.avatar) ||  getImageUrl(hero.images?.portrait) ||
getImageUrl(hero.images?.gallery?.[0]) ||  DEFAULT_AVATAR;
const videoUrl = hero.images?.banner?.videoUrl ||  null;

useEffect(() => {
if (videoUrl && (videoUrl.endsWith('.mp4') ||  videoUrl.endsWith('.webm' ))) {
setBannerType('video' );
} else {
setBannerType('image' );
}
}, [videoUrl]);

return (
<motion.section className="relative h-[75vh] overflow-hidden bg-black">
{bannerType === 'video' && videoUrl ? (
<motion.video
initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
ref={videoRef}
src={videoUrl}
autoPlay
loop
muted={videoMuted}
className="w-full h-full object-cover object-top"
/>
) : (
<motion.img



key={bannerUrl}
initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 1.02 }}
animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1 }}
transition={{ duration: 1.5 }}
src={bannerUrl}

alt={hero.name}
className="w-full h-full object-cover object-top"
onError={(e) => {
(e.currentTarget as HTMLImageElement).src = DEFAULT_BANNER;
}}
/>
)}

  <div className="absolute inset-0 bg-gradient-to-t from-black via-black/60 to-transp

  {bannerType === 'video' && videoUrl && (
    <motion.button

      onClick={() => setVideoMuted(!videoMuted)}
      className="absolute top-6 right-6 p-3 rounded-full bg-white/20 text-white hover
    >
      {videoMuted ? <FaVolumeMute size={18} /> : <FaVolumeUp size={18} />}
    </motion.button>
  )}

  <div className="absolute bottom-0 left-0 right-0 p-6 md:p-12 z-10">
    <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto w-full">
      <div className="flex items-end gap-6 w-full">
        {/* ✅ AVATAR - THIS WAS MISSING! */}
        <motion.div
          initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.95 }}
          animate={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1 }}

          transition={{ delay: 0.3, duration: 0.7 }}
          className="hidden md:block flex-shrink-0"
        >
          <div className="w-60 h-80 rounded-xl overflow-hidden border-4 border-white
            <img
              key={avatarUrl}
              src={avatarUrl}

              alt={hero.name}
              className="w-full h-full object-cover"
              onError={(e) => {
                (e.currentTarget as HTMLImageElement).src = DEFAULT_AVATAR;
              }}
              loading="lazy"
            />

          </div>
        </motion.div>

        <motion.div
          initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
          animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
          transition={{ delay: 0.4, duration: 0.7 }}
          className="flex-1 min-w-0"



        >
          <h1 className="text-5xl md:text-7xl font-black text-white mb-3 leading-none
            {hero.name}
          </h1>

          {hero.title && (
            ```
            <p className="text-2xl md:text-3xl text-white/80 font-bold mb-4 drop-shad
            ```
          )}

          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-4 mb-6">
            {hero.movies && hero.movies.length > 0 && (
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-white/80">
                <FaFilm className="text-white/60 flex-shrink-0" size={18} />
                ```
                <span className="font-semibold">{hero.movies.length} Movies</span>
                ```

              </div>
            )}

            {hero.awards && hero.awards.length > 0 && (
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-white/80">
                <FaTrophy className="text-white/60 flex-shrink-0" size={18} />
                ```

                <span className="font-semibold">{hero.awards.length} Awards</span>
                ```
              </div>
            )}

            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-white/80">
              <FaHeart className="text-white/60 flex-shrink-0" size={18} />

              ```
              <span className="font-semibold">{followerCount.toLocaleString()} Follo
              ```
            </div>

            {hero.personalInfo?.birthDate && (
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-white/80">
                <FaCalendarAlt className="text-white/60 flex-shrink-0" size={18} />

                <span className="font-semibold">
                  Age {new Date().getFullYear() - new Date(hero.personalInfo.birthDate
                </span>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>

          {/* ✅ FOLLOW BUTTON + SOCIAL MEDIA */}
          <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-3">
            <motion.button
              onClick={onFollow}
              whileHover={{ scale: 1.05, y: -2 }}
              className={`px-6 py-3 rounded-lg font-bold transition shadow-lg flex it
                isFollowing

                  ? 'bg-white/10 text-white border border-white/30 hover:bg-white/20 
                  : 'bg-white text-black hover:bg-white/95'



              }`}
            >
              {isFollowing ? <FaHeart /> : <FaRegHeart />}
              {isFollowing ? 'Following' : 'Follow'}

            </motion.button>

            {hero.socialMedia?.instagram?.url && (
              <motion.a
                href={hero.socialMedia.instagram.url}
                target="_blank"
                rel="noopener noreferrer"

                whileHover={{ scale: 1.05 }}
                className="px-6 py-3 bg-white/10 hover:bg-white/20 text-white rounded
              >
                <FaInstagram /> Instagram
              </motion.a>
            )}

            {hero.socialMedia?.twitter?.url && (
              <motion.a
                href={hero.socialMedia.twitter.url}
                target="_blank"
                rel="noopener noreferrer"
                whileHover={{ scale: 1.05 }}
                className="px-6 py-3 bg-white/10 hover:bg-white/20 text-white rounded

              >
                <FaTwitter /> Twitter
              </motion.a>
            )}

            {hero.socialMedia?.youtube?.url && (
              <motion.a

                href={hero.socialMedia.youtube.url}
                target="_blank"
                rel="noopener noreferrer"
                whileHover={{ scale: 1.05 }}
                className="px-6 py-3 bg-white/10 hover:bg-white/20 text-white rounded
              >
                <FaYoutube /> YouTube
              </motion.a>

            )}
          </div>
        </motion.div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </div>
</motion.section>

);
}

This chunk covers everything for your hero banner and overview tab exactly as per your
theme and field order:

Banner handles both video and image, with mute toggle and glass effect.

Avatar, hero name, tagline, live follower count, movies/awards badges, all social icons
are present, using your color, placement, and responsiveness choices.

The follow button is present and reacts live, ready for confetti/animation on click.

All info below is in the fixed order you want with the right emojis and field mapping.

Tabs and sections (Biography, Aura, Genre Strength, Transformations, Voice Profile,
Known For, Collaborations) are mapped to your JSON with smart type checking.

Count badge, sticky nav, and all sections are theme-aligned and leave space for ultra-
smooth Netflix-style navigation.

Any changes from your requirements will be directly visible here in the code, so you can flag
minor tweaks immediately and the UI/logic will match your JSON data 1:1.
Send the next chunk when ready or give feedback for any single detail!

        {favorites.actor && <InfoCard label="Favorite Actor" value={favorites.actor} 
        {favorites.actress && <InfoCard label="Favorite Actress" value={favorites.act
        {favorites.director && <InfoCard label="Favorite Director" value={favorites.
        {favorites.film && <InfoCard label="Favorite Film" value={favorites.film} ic
        {favorites.food && <InfoCard label="Favorite Food" value={favorites.food} ic
        {favorites.cuisine && <InfoCard label="Favorite Cuisine" value={favorites.cu

        {favorites.color && <InfoCard label="Favorite Color" value={favorites.color}
        {favorites.destination && <InfoCard label="Favorite Destination" value={favor
        {favorites.sport && <InfoCard label="Favorite Sport" value={favorites.sport}
        {favorites.book && <InfoCard label="Favorite Book" value={favorites.book} ic
        {favorites.music && <InfoCard label="Favorite Music" value={favorites.music} 
      </div>
    </motion.section>

  )}

  {/* Social Media */}
  {Object.keys(socialMedia).length > 0 && (
    <motion.section
      initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 20 }}
      whileInView={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
      viewport={{ once: true }}

    >
      <SectionTitle emoji="📱" title="Social Media" />
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-3 md:gap-4">
        {socialMedia.instagram && (
          <a
            href={typeof socialMedia.instagram === 'string' ? socialMedia.instagram 
            target="_blank"

            rel="noopener noreferrer"
            className="flex items-center gap-3 p-4 md:p-5 rounded-lg bg-white/5 bord
          >
            <FaInstagram size={24} className="text-pink-500 group-hover:scale-110 tra
            <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
              ```
              <p className="text-white/50 text-xs font-medium">Instagram</p>

              ```
              <p className="text-white font-bold text-sm truncate">



                {typeof socialMedia.instagram === 'object' && socialMedia.instagram.
                  ? socialMedia.instagram.handle 
                  : 'Follow'}
              </p>

              {typeof socialMedia.instagram === 'object' && socialMedia.instagram.fo
                <p className="text-white/40 text-xs">
                  {(socialMedia.instagram.followers / 1000000).toFixed(1)}M Followers
                </p>
              )}
            </div>
          </a>

          <a
            href={typeof socialMedia.twitter === 'string' ? socialMedia.twitter : so

              </p>

          </a>

            href={typeof socialMedia.youtube === 'string' ? socialMedia.youtube : so

// ============================================
// MOVIES TAB -  Filter & Sort
// ============================================
function MoviesTab({ hero }: any) {
const [filter, setFilter] = useState('all' );
const [sortBy, setSortBy] = useState('year' );

const movieStats = useMemo(() => {
const all = hero.movies ||  [];
const lead = all.filter((m: any) => !m.movieType ||  m.movieType.toLowerCase() === 'lead' );
const cameo = hero.cameoAppearances ||  [];
const voiceover = hero.voiceOverAppearances ||  [];
const child = hero.childArtistMovies ||  [];

return { all, lead, cameo, voiceover, child, total: all.length + cameo.length + voic

}, [hero]);

const filteredMovies = useMemo(() => {
let filtered: any[] = [];

if (filter === 'all') {
  filtered = [...movieStats.all, ...movieStats.cameo, ...movieStats.voiceover, ...
} else if (filter === 'lead') {
  filtered = movieStats.lead;
} else if (filter === 'cameo') {
  filtered = movieStats.cameo;
} else if (filter === 'voiceover') {

  filtered = movieStats.voiceover;



} else if (filter === 'child') {
  filtered = movieStats.child;
}

return filtered.sort((a: any, b: any) => {
  if (sortBy === 'year') return (b.year || 0) - (a.year || 0);
  if (sortBy === 'rating') return (b.ratings?.imdb || 0) - (a.ratings?.imdb || 0);
  return 0;
});

}, [movieStats, filter, sortBy]);

return (
<motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }} className="space-y-6 md:space-y-8">
<div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row items-start sm:items-center justify-between gap-3
md:gap-4 flex-wrap">
<div className="flex gap-1 md:gap-2 flex-wrap">
<motion.button
onClick={() => setFilter('all' )}
whileHover={{ scale: 1.05 }}
whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
className={px-3 md:px-4 py-1.5 md:py-2 rounded-lg font-medium text-xs md:text-sm
transition border ${ filter === 'all' ? 'bg-white text-black border-white' : 'bg-

white/5 text-white/70 border-white/10 hover:bg-white/10 hover:text-white' }}
>
All ({movieStats.total})
</motion.button>

      <motion.button
        onClick={() => setFilter('lead')}
        whileHover={{ scale: 1.05 }}

        whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
        className={`px-3 md:px-4 py-1.5 md:py-2 rounded-lg font-medium text-xs md:te
          filter === 'lead' ? 'bg-white text-black border-white' : 'bg-white/5 text-w
        }`}
      >
        Lead ({movieStats.lead.length})
      </motion.button>

      {movieStats.child.length > 0 && (
        <motion.button
          onClick={() => setFilter('child')}
          whileHover={{ scale: 1.05 }}
          whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
          className={`px-3 md:px-4 py-1.5 md:py-2 rounded-lg font-medium text-xs md:

            filter === 'child' ? 'bg-white text-black border-white' : 'bg-white/5 tex
          }`}
        >
          <FaChild size={12} /> Child ({movieStats.child.length})
        </motion.button>
      )}



      {movieStats.cameo.length > 0 && (
        <motion.button
          onClick={() => setFilter('cameo')}
          whileHover={{ scale: 1.05 }}

          whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
          className={`px-3 md:px-4 py-1.5 md:py-2 rounded-lg font-medium text-xs md:
            filter === 'cameo' ? 'bg-white text-black border-white' : 'bg-white/5 tex
          }`}
        >
          Cameo ({movieStats.cameo.length})
        </motion.button>

      )}

      {movieStats.voiceover.length > 0 && (
        <motion.button
          onClick={() => setFilter('voiceover')}
          whileHover={{ scale: 1.05 }}
          whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}

          className={`px-3 md:px-4 py-1.5 md:py-2 rounded-lg font-medium text-xs md:
            filter === 'voiceover' ? 'bg-white text-black border-white' : 'bg-white/5
          }`}
        >
          <FaMicrophone size={12} /> Voice ({movieStats.voiceover.length})
        </motion.button>
      )}

    </div>

    <select
      value={sortBy}
      onChange={(e) => setSortBy(e.target.value)}
      className="px-3 md:px-4 py-1.5 md:py-2 bg-white/5 text-white rounded-lg border
    >

      <option value="year">Latest First</option>
      <option value="rating">Highest Rated</option>
    </select>
  </div>

  {filteredMovies.length === 0 ? (
    <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }} className="text-ce
      <FaFilm size={48} className="mx-auto mb-4 text-white/20" />

      ```
      <p className="text-white/40 text-base md:text-lg">No movies found</p>
      ```
    </motion.div>
  ) : (
    <motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }} className="grid gr
      {filteredMovies.map((movie: any, idx: number) => (

        <motion.div
          key={movie.slug || movie.id || idx}
          initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.9 }}
          whileInView={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1 }}
          transition={{ delay: Math.min(idx * 0.02, 0.3) }}
          viewport={{ once: true }}
        >

          <MovieCard movie={movie} />
        </motion.div>



      ))}
    </motion.div>
  )}
</motion.div>

);
}

This chunk is comprehensive and maps every personal detail, family node, physical stat,
favorite, and social profile—fully honoring your field order and the v17 theme:

Personal info, education, family shown in order, with category-specific icons and grid
layout for clarity and mobile speed.

Physical stats use only the mapped v17 JSON keys, so nothing extra or missing (height,
weight, BMI, etc.).

Social media shows correct info, emoji, and colors—no extra branding, only theme plus
icon highlight.

Movies tab section is Netflix-style: smart filtering (Lead, Cameo, Voice, Child), sorting by
year/rating, with smooth button states and card grid. All logic fits your JSON shape
exactly.

All transitions, responsive layout, and badge counts will work fluidly across devices,
matching your exact theme and interaction feel.

Send the next chunk or request field mapping clarifications any time—each chunk is
connected seamlessly.

// MOVIE CARD COMPONENT
// ============================================
function MovieCard({ movie }: any) {
const [posterUrl, setPosterUrl] = useState(getImageUrl(movie.poster) ||  DEFAULT_POSTER);
const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

return (
<Link href={/movie/${movie.slug}} className="group block h-full">
<div className="relative rounded-lg overflow-hidden mb-2 md:mb-3 border border-white/10
group-hover:border-white/30 transition bg-white/5 aspect-[2/3]">
{loading && (

)}

    <img
      src={posterUrl}



      alt={movie.title}
      className="w-full h-full object-cover group-hover:scale-110 transition-transfor
      onError={(e) => {
        (e.target as HTMLImageElement).src = DEFAULT_POSTER;

      }}
      onLoad={() => setLoading(false)}
    />

    {movie.year && (
      <div className="absolute top-2 left-2 px-2 py-1 rounded bg-black/70 text-white 
        {movie.year}

      </div>
    )}

    {movie.ratings?.imdb && (
      <div className="absolute top-2 right-2 px-2 py-1 rounded bg-yellow-500/80 text-
        <FaStar size={10} />
        {movie.ratings.imdb}

      </div>
    )}

    {movie.movieType && movie.movieType.toLowerCase() !== 'lead' && (
      <div className="absolute bottom-2 left-2 px-2 py-1 rounded bg-blue-500/80 text-
        {movie.movieType}
      </div>

    )}
  </div>

  <h3 className="text-white font-bold text-xs md:text-sm line-clamp-2 group-hover:te
    {movie.title}
  </h3>
  {movie.role && (

    <p className="text-white/40 text-xs mt-1 line-clamp-1 flex items-center gap-1">
      <FaUser size={10} /> {movie.role}
    </p>
  )}
</Link>

);
}

// ============================================
// AWARDS TAB
// ============================================
function AwardsTab({ hero }: any) {
const awards = hero.awards ||  [];
const [filterBy, setFilterBy] = useState('all' );



if (awards.length === 0) {
return (
<motion.div
initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
className="text-center py-20 md:py-32"
>

<p className="text-white/40 text-base md:text-lg">No awards information</p>

</motion.div>
);
}

const won = awards.filter((a : any) => a.won === true ||  a.status === 'Won' );
const nominated = awards.filter((a : any) => a.won === false ||  a.status === 'Nominated' );
const displayed = filterBy === 'won' ? won : filterBy === 'nominated' ? nominated : awards ;

return (
<motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }} className="space-y-6 md:space-y-8">
<div className="flex gap-2 md:gap-3 flex-wrap">
<motion.button
onClick={() => setFilterBy('all' )}
whileHover={{ scale: 1.05 }}
whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
className={px-3 md:px-4 py-1.5 md:py-2 rounded-lg font-medium text-xs md:text-sm
transition border ${ filterBy === 'all' ? 'bg-white text-black border-white' : 'bg-

white/5 text-white/70 border-white/10 hover:bg-white/10 hover:text-white' }}
>
All ({awards.length})
</motion.button>

    <motion.button
      onClick={() => setFilterBy('won')}
      whileHover={{ scale: 1.05 }}
      whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}

      className={`px-3 md:px-4 py-1.5 md:py-2 rounded-lg font-medium text-xs md:text
        filterBy === 'won'
          ? 'bg-yellow-500/20 text-yellow-300 border-yellow-500/30'
          : 'bg-white/5 text-white/70 border-white/10 hover:bg-white/10 hover:text-wh
      }`}
    >
      <FaTrophy size={12} /> Won ({won.length})

    </motion.button>

    {nominated.length > 0 && (
      <motion.button
        onClick={() => setFilterBy('nominated')}
        whileHover={{ scale: 1.05 }}
        whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}

        className={`px-3 md:px-4 py-1.5 md:py-2 rounded-lg font-medium text-xs md:te



          filterBy === 'nominated'
            ? 'bg-blue-500/20 text-blue-300 border-blue-500/30'
            : 'bg-white/5 text-white/70 border-white/10 hover:bg-white/10 hover:text-
        }`}

      >
        Nominated ({nominated.length})
      </motion.button>
    )}
  </div>

  <motion.div

    initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
    animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
    className="space-y-3 md:space-y-4"
  >
    {displayed.map((award: any, idx: number) => (
      <motion.div
        key={idx}

        initial={{ opacity: 0, y: 10 }}
        whileInView={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
        transition={{ delay: idx * 0.03 }}
        viewport={{ once: true }}
        className={`rounded-lg p-4 md:p-5 border transition flex items-start gap-3 $
          award.won || award.status === 'Won'
            ? 'bg-yellow-500/5 border-yellow-500/20 hover:border-yellow-500/40'

            : 'bg-white/5 border-white/10 hover:border-white/20'
        }`}
      >
        <div
          className={`w-8 h-8 md:w-10 md:h-10 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-ce
            award.won || award.status === 'Won' ? 'bg-yellow-500/20' : 'bg-white/10'
          }`}

        >
          <FaTrophy
            size={14}
            className={award.won || award.status === 'Won' ? 'text-yellow-400' : 'text
          />
        </div>

        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">

          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-1 flex-wrap">
            <h3 className="text-white font-bold text-sm md:text-base line-clamp-1">
              {award.awardName || award.award}
            </h3>
            <span
              className={`px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-xs font-bold whitespace-nowrap ${
                award.won || award.status === 'Won'

                  ? 'bg-green-500/20 text-green-300'
                  : 'bg-blue-500/20 text-blue-300'
              }`}
            >
              {award.won ? '✅ Won' : '⭐ Nominated'}
            </span>
          </div>

          <p className="text-white/60 text-xs md:text-sm line-clamp-1">
            {award.category} {award.film && `• ${award.film}`} {award.year && `(${awa



          </p>
          {award.givenBy && (
            ```
            <p className="text-white/40 text-xs mt-1">By: {award.givenBy}</p>

            ```
          )}
        </div>
      </motion.div>
    ))}
  </motion.div>
</motion.div>

);
}

// ============================================
// GALLERY TAB
// ============================================
function GalleryTab({ hero }: any) {
const images = hero.images?.gallery ||  [];
const [selectedImage, setSelectedImage] = useState<number |  null>(null);

if (!images ||  images.length === 0) {
return (
<motion.div
initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
className="text-center py-20 md:py-32"
>

<p className="text-white/40 text-base md:text-lg">No gallery images</p>

</motion.div>
);
}

return (
<motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }} className="space-y-6 md:space-y-8">

<SectionTitle emoji="🖼️" title={Gallery (${images.length})} />
<motion.div
initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
className="grid grid-cols-2 sm:grid-cols-3 md:grid-cols-4 lg :grid-cols-5 gap-3 md:gap-4"
>
{images.slice(0, 20).map((imageUrl: string, idx: number) => (
<motion.div
key={idx}
initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.9 }}
whileInView={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1 }}



transition={{ delay: idx * 0.02 }}
viewport={{ once: true }}
onClick={() => setSelectedImage(idx)}
className="group cursor-pointer aspect-square rounded-lg overflow-hidden border border-
white/10 hover:border-white/30 transition relative"
>
<img
src={imageUrl}
alt={Gallery ${idx + 1}}
className="w-full h-full object-cover group-hover:scale-110 transition-transform duration-
300"
onError={(e) => {
(e.target as HTMLImageElement).src = DEFAULT_POSTER;
}}
/>

</motion.div>
))}
</motion.div>

  {/* Lightbox */}
  <AnimatePresence>
    {selectedImage !== null && (
      <motion.div

        initial={{ opacity: 0 }}
        animate={{ opacity: 1 }}
        exit={{ opacity: 0 }}
        onClick={() => setSelectedImage(null)}
        className="fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/95 flex items-center justify-center p-
      >
        <motion.div

          initial={{ scale: 0.9 }}
          animate={{ scale: 1 }}
          exit={{ scale: 0.9 }}
          onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
          className="relative max-w-4xl w-full"
        >
          <img

            src={images[selectedImage]}
            alt={`Gallery ${selectedImage + 1}`}
            className="w-full rounded-lg shadow-2xl"
          />

          <motion.button
            whileHover={{ scale: 1.1 }}

            whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
            onClick={() => setSelectedImage((p) => (p === 0 ? images.length - 1 : (p 
            className="absolute left-4 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 p-2 md:p-3 rounded-fu
          >
            <FaChevronRight className="rotate-180" />



          </motion.button>

          <motion.button
            whileHover={{ scale: 1.1 }}

            whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
            onClick={() => setSelectedImage((p) => (p === images.length - 1 ? 0 : (p 
            className="absolute right-4 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 p-2 md:p-3 rounded-f
          >
            <FaChevronRight />
          </motion.button>

          <motion.button
            whileHover={{ scale: 1.1 }}
            whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
            onClick={() => setSelectedImage(null)}
            className="absolute -top-10 md:-top-12 right-0 text-white/60 hover:text-w
          >
            ✕

          </motion.button>

          <div className="absolute bottom-4 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 px-4 py-2 bg-bla
            {(selectedImage ?? 0) + 1} / {images.length}
          </div>
        </motion.div>
      </motion.div>

    )}
  </AnimatePresence>
</motion.div>

);
}

# <q>Once you send the last chunk (trivia, quotes, contribute, and any remaining tab

Here’s the exact production plan to show your superstar page with all tabs and sections,
without losing your theme or future scalability:

Page Structure and Tab Layout Plan

1. Header and Banner

Top: compact header (logo, back button, search, sign-in/profile icon).

Banner section: video or image—auto detect, with mute toggle for video, glass overlay,
portrait avatar, hero name, nickname, follow button, live follower count, social media
icons.

2. Sticky Tab Navigation

All tabs visible, horizontally scrollable, using gradient arrow buttons.

Tabs always: Overview, Info, Career, Movies, Upcoming, Collaborations, Lifestyle,
Awards, Trivia, Gallery, Contribute.

Count badges per tab (number of movies, awards, contributions, etc), animated underline
for active tab.

3. Sections Under Each Tab

Overview: Full bio, hero aura cards, genre mastery bars (with emojis, NOT graphs),
physical transformations, voice profile (all languages, type, iconic quotes), known for
tags, collaborations.

Info: Personal info (name, DOB, etc), family, education, career start, physical stats,
favorites, all social media.

Career: Timeline, main milestones, notable achievements, records.

Movies: Netflix-style grid, filter by type (lead, cameo, child, voiceover), sort by
year/rating, per-film card.

Upcoming : New projects grid, details, release, director, status, genre, synopsis.

Collaborations: Director/music/heroine grids, chemistry notes, film counts.

Lifestyle: Net worth, cars, properties, business ventures, all with emoji badges.

Awards: Filter for All/Won/Nominated, grid layout by year, film, category.

Trivia : All facts and small records, rendered with icons.

Gallery: Up to 20 images at once, lightbox view with left/right navigation.

Contribute:

Form for messages/images/trivia, sent to Discord webhook.



Side panel for recent contributes and mini leaderboard.

Admin panel elsewhere for approval; leaderboard updates per entity (not global).

4. Theme/Design and Responsiveness

No gradients—use dark/light theme as per your styling.

All icons and buttons as per brand color (social: pink/blue/red, etc.), rest matches your
look.

Everything is mobile-first, scaling up to desktop grid smoothly.

Confetti on follow, live follower count auto-updates, sticky/tabbed navigation with
scroll snap for easier UX.

5. Scalability for All Categories

Each entity type (hero, heroine, director, etc.) has a dedicated [slug]/page.tsx with the
above structure.

All tabs/components fetched as modular React components, config-driven.

Changing categories is just replacing the underlying JSON data—UI stays consistent,
code doesn’t duplicate.

Next Steps After Plan

The main tabs/components above will be coded once, then reused for every superstar,
heroine, director, etc.

No need for separate global trivia/quotes/contribute tab if you don’t have the data—just
omit those tabs for now, they can be added in future with updated data.

Focus implementation on current designed tabs and keep code ready for future extra
sections.

This architecture delivers a beautiful, fast, and scalable superstar page. Once this is live and
reusable, every new entity or category requires only JSON data and one import—no heavy
rework ever again.

Ready for implementation phase or chunk-by-chunk review—just say the word!

const DEFAULT_AVATAR = '/images/default-avatar.png';

// ========== IMAGE HELPER ==========
function getImageUrl(imageObj: any): string {
if (!imageObj) return DEFAULT_POSTER;

if (typeof imageObj === 'string') {
if (imageObj.startsWith('http')) return imageObj;
if (imageObj.startsWith('/') && !imageObj.startsWith('//')) return `${TMDB_IMAGE_
return imageObj;

  }
if (typeof imageObj === 'object') {
if (imageObj.url && typeof imageObj.url === 'string' && imageObj.url.startsWith

if (imageObj.fallback) return imageObj.fallback;
if (imageObj.tmdbPath && imageObj.tmdbPath.startsWith('/')) return `${TMDB_IMAG

  }
return DEFAULT_POSTER;

}

// ============================================
// TAB NAVIGATION WITH SCROLL
// ============================================
function TabNavigation({ activeTab, setActiveTab, hero }: any) {
const scrollContainerRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

const tabs = [
    { id: 'overview', label: 'Overview', icon: FaUser, count: 0 },
    { id: 'info', label: 'Info', icon: FaGlobe, count: 0 },
    { id: 'movies', label: 'Movies', icon: FaFilm, count: hero.movies?.length || 0
    { id: 'upcoming', label: 'Upcoming', icon: FaCalendarAlt, count: hero.upcoming?
    { id: 'lifestyle', label: 'Lifestyle', icon: FaCar, count: 0 },

    { id: 'awards', label: 'Awards', icon: FaTrophy, count: hero.awards?.length || 0
    { id: 'gallery', label: 'Gallery', icon: FaPalette, count: hero.images?.gallery?
  ];

useEffect(() => {
const activeTabElement = scrollContainerRef.current?.querySelector(`[data-tab="$
if (activeTabElement) {

      activeTabElement.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'nearest', inline
    }
  }, [activeTab]);

const scroll = (direction: 'left' | 'right') => {
if (scrollContainerRef.current) {

      scrollContainerRef.current.scrollBy({
left: direction === 'left' ? -300 : 300,

behavior: 'smooth',
      });
    }
  };

return (
<motion.div

initial={{ opacity: 0, y: -10 }}
animate={{ opacity: 1, y: 0 }}
className="sticky top-[68px] md:top-[76px] z-40 bg-black/50 backdrop-blur-xl bo

    >
<div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 sm:px-6 md:px-12 relative">
<button
onClick={() => scroll('left')}

          className="absolute left-0 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 z-10 w-10 h-full bg-grad
          aria-label="Scroll left"



        >
<FaChevronRight className="rotate-180" size={14} />

</button>

<div
ref={scrollContainerRef}
className="flex gap-1 md:gap-2 overflow-x-auto scrollbar-hide py-3 px-0 md

        >
          {tabs.map((tab) => {
            const Icon = tab.icon;
            return (

<motion.button
key={tab.id}
data-tab={tab.id}
onClick={() => setActiveTab(tab.id)}

                whileHover={{ scale: 1.05 }}
                whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
                className={`flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 md:px-4 py-2 md:py-2.5 ro

                  activeTab === tab.id
                    ? 'bg-white text-black border-white shadow-lg'
                    : 'bg-white/5 text-white/70 border-white/10 hover:bg-white/10 hov
                }`}
              >
                {Icon && <Icon size={12} className="md:text-sm" />}

<span className="hidden sm:inline">{tab.label}</span>

<span className="sm:hidden text-xs">{tab.label.slice(0, 3)}</span>
                {tab.count > 0 && (

<span className="ml-1 px-2 py-0.5 bg-white/20 rounded-full text-xs f
                    {tab.count}

</span>
                )}

</motion.button>

            );
          })}

</div>

<button
onClick={() => scroll('right')}

          className="absolute right-0 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 z-10 w-10 h-full bg-gra
          aria-label="Scroll right"

        >
<FaChevronRight size={14} />

</button>

<style jsx>{`
.scrollbar-hide::-webkit-scrollbar {
display: none;

          }
.scrollbar-hide {

            -ms-overflow-style: none;
scrollbar-width: none;

          }
        `}</style>

</div>

</motion.div>



  );
}

// ============================================
// MOVIE CARD COMPONENT
// ============================================
function MovieCard({ movie }: any) {

const [posterUrl, setPosterUrl] = useState(getImageUrl(movie.poster) || DEFAULT_PO
const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

return (
<Link href={`/movie/${movie.slug}`} className="group block h-full">
<div className="relative rounded-lg overflow-hidden mb-2 md:mb-3 border bord

        {loading && (

<div className="absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center bg-white/
<FaSpinner className="animate-spin text-white/20" size={24} />

</div>
        )}

<img
src={posterUrl}

alt={movie.title}



className="w-full h-full object-cover group-hover:scale-110 transition-tran
onError={(e) => {

            (e.target as HTMLImageElement).src = DEFAULT_POSTER;
          }}

          onLoad={() => setLoading(false)}
        />

        {movie.year && (
<div className="absolute top-2 left-2 px-2 py-1 rounded bg-black/70 text-wh

            {movie.year}
</div>

        )}

        {movie.ratings?.imdb && (
<div className="absolute top-2 right-2 px-2 py-1 rounded bg-yellow-500/80 t
<FaStar size={10} />

            {movie.ratings.imdb}
</div>

        )}

        {movie.movieType && movie.movieType.toLowerCase() !== 'lead' && (
<div className="absolute bottom-2 left-2 px-2 py-1 rounded bg-blue-500/80 t

            {movie.movieType}
</div>

        )}

</div>

<h3 className="text-white font-bold text-xs md:text-sm line-clamp-2 group-hove
        {movie.title}

</h3>
      {movie.role && (

<p className="text-white/40 text-xs mt-1 line-clamp-1 flex items-center gap-1

<FaUser size={10} /> {movie.role}
</p>

      )}
</Link>

  );
}

// ============================================

// MOVIES TAB - Filter & Sort
// ============================================
function MoviesTab({ hero }: any) {
const [filter, setFilter] = useState('all');
const [sortBy, setSortBy] = useState('year');

const movieStats = useMemo(() => {

const all = hero.movies || [];
const lead = all.filter((m: any) => !m.movieType || m.movieType.toLowerCase() =
const cameo = hero.cameoAppearances || [];
const voiceover = hero.voiceOverAppearances || [];
const child = hero.childArtistMovies || [];

return { all, lead, cameo, voiceover, child, total: all.length + cameo.length + 

  }, [hero]);



const filteredMovies = useMemo(() => {
let filtered: any[] = [];

if (filter === 'all') {

      filtered = [...movieStats.all, ...movieStats.cameo, ...movieStats.voiceover,
    } else if (filter === 'lead') {
      filtered = movieStats.lead;
    } else if (filter === 'cameo') {
      filtered = movieStats.cameo;
    } else if (filter === 'voiceover') {
      filtered = movieStats.voiceover;

    } else if (filter === 'child') {
      filtered = movieStats.child;
    }

return filtered.sort((a: any, b: any) => {
if (sortBy === 'year') return (b.year || 0) - (a.year || 0);
if (sortBy === 'rating') return (b.ratings?.imdb || 0) - (a.ratings?.imdb || 0

return 0;
    });
  }, [movieStats, filter, sortBy]);

return (
<motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }} className="space-y
<div className="flex flex-col sm:flex-row items-start sm:items-center justify-

<div className="flex gap-1 md:gap-2 flex-wrap">
<motion.button
onClick={() => setFilter('all')}

            whileHover={{ scale: 1.05 }}
            whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
            className={`px-3 md:px-4 py-1.5 md:py-2 rounded-lg font-medium text-xs m
              filter === 'all' ? 'bg-white text-black border-white' : 'bg-white/5 text

            }`}
          >
            All ({movieStats.total})

</motion.button>

<motion.button
onClick={() => setFilter('lead')}

            whileHover={{ scale: 1.05 }}

            whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
            className={`px-3 md:px-4 py-1.5 md:py-2 rounded-lg font-medium text-xs m
              filter === 'lead' ? 'bg-white text-black border-white' : 'bg-white/5 te
            }`}
          >
            Lead ({movieStats.lead.length})

</motion.button>

          {movieStats.child.length > 0 && (
<motion.button
onClick={() => setFilter('child')}

              whileHover={{ scale: 1.05 }}
              whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
              className={`px-3 md:px-4 py-1.5 md:py-2 rounded-lg font-medium text-xs 

                filter === 'child' ? 'bg-white text-black border-white' : 'bg-white/5 
              }`}



            >
<FaChild size={12} /> Child ({movieStats.child.length})

</motion.button>
          )}

          {movieStats.cameo.length > 0 && (
<motion.button
onClick={() => setFilter('cameo')}

              whileHover={{ scale: 1.05 }}
              whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
              className={`px-3 md:px-4 py-1.5 md:py-2 rounded-lg font-medium text-xs 

                filter === 'cameo' ? 'bg-white text-black border-white' : 'bg-white/5
              }`}
            >
              Cameo ({movieStats.cameo.length})

</motion.button>
          )}

          {movieStats.voiceover.length > 0 && (
<motion.button
onClick={() => setFilter('voiceover')}

              whileHover={{ scale: 1.05 }}
              whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
              className={`px-3 md:px-4 py-1.5 md:py-2 rounded-lg font-medium text-xs 
                filter === 'voiceover' ? 'bg-white text-black border-white' : 'bg-whi

              }`}
            >

<FaMicrophone size={12} /> Voice ({movieStats.voiceover.length})
</motion.button>

          )}
</div>

<select
value={sortBy}
onChange={(e) => setSortBy(e.target.value)}

          className="px-3 md:px-4 py-1.5 md:py-2 bg-white/5 text-white rounded-lg bo
        >

<option value="year">Latest First</option>
<option value="rating">Highest Rated</option>

</select>

</div>

      {filteredMovies.length === 0 ? (
<motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }} className="text
<FaFilm size={48} className="mx-auto mb-4 text-white/20" />
<p className="text-white/40 text-base md:text-lg">No movies found</p>

</motion.div>

      ) : (
<motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }} className="gri

          {filteredMovies.map((movie: any, idx: number) => (
<motion.div
key={movie.slug || movie.id || idx}
initial={{ opacity: 0, scale: 0.9 }}
whileInView={{ opacity: 1, scale: 1 }}

transition={{ delay: Math.min(idx * 0.02, 0.3) }}
viewport={{ once: true }}



            >
<MovieCard movie={movie} />

</motion.div>
          ))}

</motion.div>
      )}

</motion.div>
  );
}

function AwardsTab({ hero }: any) {

</motion.div>



    );
  }

const won = awards.filter((a: any) => a.won === true || a.status === 'Won');

const nominated = awards.filter((a: any) => a.won === false || a.status === 'Nominat
const displayed = filterBy === 'won' ? won : filterBy === 'nominated' ? nominated 

return (
<motion.div initial={{ opacity: 0 }} animate={{ opacity: 1 }} className="space-y
<div className="flex gap-2 md:gap-3 flex-wrap">
<motion.button

onClick={() => setFilterBy('all')}
          whileHover={{ scale: 1.05 }}
          whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
          className={`px-3 md:px-4 py-1.5 md:py-2 rounded-lg font-medium text-xs md:
            filterBy === 'all'
              ? 'bg-white text-black border-white'

          All ({awards.length})

            >

        {selectedImage !== null && (

            className="fixed inset-0 z-50 bg-black/95 flex items-center justify-cente
          >

<motion.div
initial={{ scale: 0.9 }}
animate={{ scale: 1 }}
exit={{ scale: 0.9 }}

              className="relative max-w-4xl w-full"
            >

src={images[selectedImage]}
alt={`Gallery ${selectedImage + 1}`}
className="w-full rounded-lg shadow-2xl"

              />

<motion.button
whileHover={{ scale: 1.1 }}
whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
onClick={() => setSelectedImage((p) => (p === 0 ? images.length - 1 :

                className="absolute left-4 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 p-2 md:p-3 rounded
              >

<FaChevronRight className="rotate-180" />

</motion.button>

<motion.button
whileHover={{ scale: 1.1 }}
whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}
onClick={() => setSelectedImage((p) => (p === images.length - 1 ? 0 :

                className="absolute right-4 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 p-2 md:p-3 rounde

              >
<FaChevronRight />

</motion.button>

<motion.button
whileHover={{ scale: 1.1 }}
whileTap={{ scale: 0.95 }}

onClick={() => setSelectedImage(null)}
                className="absolute -top-10 md:-top-12 right-0 text-white/60 hover:te



              >
                ✕

</motion.button>

<div className="absolute bottom-4 left-1/2 -translate-x-1/2 px-4 py-2 bg
                {(selectedImage ?? 0) + 1} / {images.length}

</div>
</motion.div>

</motion.div>
        )}

</AnimatePresence>

</motion.div>
  );

            className="w-full p-3 bg-white/5 border border-white/10 rounded-lg text-w
            rows={2}
            placeholder="Share a memorable quote..."

          />
</div>

type="submit"
className="px-6 py-3 bg-white text-black font-bold rounded-lg hover:bg-whit

        >

          Submit Contribution
</button>

</form>
</motion.div>

  );
}

this is page.tsx
// app/tfi-universe/heroes/superstars/[slug]/page.tsx

import { notFound } from 'next/navigation';
import { db } from '@/lib/db';
import { people } from '@/lib/schema'; // ✅ using people table
import { eq, and } from 'drizzle-orm';
import HeroDetailClient from './superstar-client';

export const dynamic = 'force-dynamic';
export const revalidate = 60;

/**

Fetch person data from people table

metadata column contains the full JSONB (v17) hero data
*/
async function getHeroData(slug : string) {
if (!slug) return null;

try {
const result = await db.query.people.findFirst({
where: eq(people.slug, slug),
});

if (!result) {
  console.warn(`⚠️ Hero not found: ${slug}`);
  return null;
}

// metadata contains your v17 JSONB

const heroData = result.metadata ?? {};

// expose a few top-level fields for compatibility with existing UI
return {
  ...heroData,
  id: result.id,

  name: result.name ?? heroData.name,
  slug: result.slug,
  tmdbPersonId: result.tmdbPersonId ?? heroData.tmdbPersonId,
  imdbId: result.imdbId ?? heroData.imdbId,
  category: result.category ?? heroData.category,
  subcategory: result.subcategory ?? heroData.subcategory,
};



} catch (error) {
console.error(🚨 Database error for slug ${slug}:, error);
return null;
}
}

/**

Normalize potential OG image shapes:

images.banner can be an object { url } or a string (/path or full URL)
*/
function resolveOgImage(heroData : any) {
if (!heroData) return '/og-image.jpg ';
const banner = heroData.images?.banner;
if (!banner) {
// fallback to featured / avatar / first gallery
const candidate =
heroData.images?.featured ||
heroData.images?.avatar ||
heroData.images?.portrait ||
(Array.isArray(heroData.images?.gallery) ? heroData.images.gallery[0] : null);
if (typeof candidate === 'string ' ) return candidate ;
if (candidate && typeof candidate === 'object' ) return candidate.url ||
candidate.tmdbPath ||  candidate.path ||  '/og-image.jpg ';
return '/og-image.jpg ';
}

if (typeof banner === 'string ' ) return banner;
if (typeof banner === 'object' ) return banner.url ||  banner.tmdbPath ||  banner.path ||  '/og-
image.jpg ';
return '/og-image.jpg ';
}

/**

Generate metadata for SEO
*/
export async function generateMetadata({ params }: { params: { slug : string } }) {
try {
const { slug } = params ;
const heroData = await getHeroData(slug);
if (!heroData) {
return {
title: 'Hero Not Found',
description: 'This hero does not exist.',
};
}
const ogImage = resolveOgImage(heroData);



return {
title: ${heroData.name || 'Hero'} - TFIverse,
description: heroData.title ||  heroData.bio ||  'Learn more about this Telugu cinema actor.',
openGraph: {

title: heroData.name,
description: heroData.title ||  heroData.bio,
images: [ogImage],
},
};
} catch (error) {
console.error('❌ Metadata generation error:', error);
return { title: 'Error', description: 'An error occurred.' };
}
}

/**

Main page (server component)
*/
export default async function HeroPage({ params }: { params: { slug : string } }) {
try {
const { slug } = params ;
if (!slug) return notFound();
const heroData = await getHeroData(slug);
if (!heroData) {
console.warn(🔍 Hero page not found for: ${slug});
notFound();
}
// pass the full JSONB-derived heroData to the client component
return ;
} catch (error) {
console.error('❌ Error loading hero page:', error);
notFound();
}
}

/**

Static params generation for SSG (improves perf for known superstars)
*/
export async function generateStaticParams() {
try {
const superstars = await db.query.people.findMany({
where: (peopleTbl, { eq }) =>
and(
eq(peopleTbl.category, 'hero' ),
eq(peopleTbl.subcategory, 'superstar' )
),



columns: { slug : true },
});
return (superstars ||  []).map((h) => ({ slug : h.slug }));
} catch (error) {
console.error('❌ Error generating static params:', error);
return [];
}
}

Your page.tsx file is correctly set up to serve as the main route file which fetches the hero
data and passes it to your client component for rendering the entire superstar detail page.[2]

Here’s what you should do to ensure your production code works and includes all required
sections with no errors:

Where Each Piece Goes

1. Keep Your Server Logic Here

Your page.tsx should only handle database fetch, SEO metadata, and passing props.

Do not put layout or tab UI directly here.

2. All UI: Put in superstar-client.tsx

All tab logic, navigation, animated sections, and client interactivity belongs in superstar-
client.tsx.

HeroDetailClient (imported from './superstar-client') should be your large
component which renders:

Banner

Navbar

Tabs (Overview, Info, Movies, Upcoming, Lifestyle, Awards, Gallery, Trivia, Quotes,
Contribute)

All per-section tab components.

3. How the Data Flows

Server (page.tsx) fetches hero from database

Passes as heroData to HeroDetailClient

HeroDetailClient breaks heroData into all sections



4. How to Fix Errors in Your UI

If you have lots of errors:

Make sure all tab/section components are imported at top in superstar-client.tsx.

Every major section should be a separate React component (OverviewTab, InfoTab, etc.)

Your main render method should switch on the activeTab and call the correct child.

/**
 * Main client-side superstar detail page with all tabs
 * - Receives heroData prop from page.tsx server-side
 * - Handles tab navigation and rendering all sections

 */
export default function HeroDetailClient({ heroData }: { heroData: any }) {
const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState("overview");

// Follower logic placeholders (implement your data/fetch logic if needed)
const [isFollowing, setIsFollowing] = useState(false);
const followerCount = useMemo(

() => heroData.followerCount || heroData.followers || 0,
    [heroData]
  );

// Tab definitions
const tabs = [

    { id: "overview", label: "Overview", icon: "FaUser", count: 0 },

    { id: "info", label: "Info", icon: "FaGlobe", count: 0 },



    { id: "movies", label: "Movies", icon: "FaFilm", count: heroData.movies?.lengt
    { id: "upcoming", label: "Upcoming", icon: "FaCalendarAlt", count: heroData.upc
    { id: "lifestyle", label: "Lifestyle", icon: "FaCar", count: 0 },
    { id: "awards", label: "Awards", icon: "FaTrophy", count: heroData.awards?.lengt

    { id: "gallery", label: "Gallery", icon: "FaPalette", count: heroData.images?.g
    { id: "trivia", label: "Trivia", icon: "FaLightbulb", count: heroData.trivia?.l
    { id: "quotes", label: "Quotes", icon: "FaQuoteLeft", count: heroData.quotes?.l
    { id: "contribute", label: "Contribute", icon: "FaHandHoldingHeart", count: 0 }
  ];

// Follow button logic (use your API endpoints if needed)

function handleFollow() {
setIsFollowing((val) => !val);
// Integrate with your backend

  }

return (
<div className="bg-black min-h-screen">

      {/* Top Navbar */}

      {/* Tab Navigation */}

        {activeTab === "upcoming" && <UpcomingTab hero={heroData} />}

For a superstar hero full detail page in your stack, you only need to build (and maintain) two
core files:

1. [slug]/page.tsx

Type: Server-side (async) file

What it does: Fetches hero data from your database, passes it to the client component,
and sets up SEO/meta.

What NOT to do here: No UI, tabs, or presentation logic — just data plumbing!

You’ve already done this part correctly.



2. [slug]/superstar-client.tsx

Type: Client component (JSX, logic, all tabs/sections)

What it does: Renders your premium hero profile: navbar, banner, all tab navigation, and
all 10+ tab sections (overview/info/movies/etc).

Every tab and UI section is implemented here, either in this file or by importing child
components (modular—they can be separate files or all in one giant file at the start).

Minimal Checklist: What sections/tabs/components must exist in superstar-
client.tsx?

PremiumNavbar (header bar, avatar)

PremiumHeroBannerV4 (banner, avatar, follow)

TabNavigation (all 10 sections: overview, info, movies, upcoming, lifestyle, awards,
gallery, trivia, quotes, contribute)

And for each tab, a section component:

OverviewTab

InfoTab

MoviesTab

UpcomingTab

LifestyleTab

AwardsTab

GalleryTab

TriviaTab

QuotesTab

ContributeTab

Each should be either imported at the top or declared directly in this file.

That’s it — just these two entrypoint files per section:

app/tfi-universe/heroes/superstars/[slug]/page.tsx – only data/SEO

app/tfi-universe/heroes/superstars/[slug]/superstar-client.tsx – all your UI, logic,
tabs



Everything else (like styles, atoms, helpers) can go anywhere as usual, but the

entry point is those two files above.

If you want a truly production-vibe dev workflow:

Keep as many tab/section components in their own files (or build one-by-one in superstar-
client.tsx, then move them out).

Use strict imports, keep prop shapes consistent, and use heroData everywhere for source
data.

You do NOT need a separate “page” or “client” for every tab or subfolder. Only these two
files drive everything for a superstar’s profile.

import { notFound } from 'next/navigation';

import { db } from '@/lib/db';
import { people } from '@/lib/schema'; // Your people table
import { eq, and } from 'drizzle-orm';
import HeroDetailClient from './superstar-client';

export const dynamic = 'force-dynamic';
export const revalidate = 60;

/** Fetch hero data by slug */
async function getHeroData(slug: string) {
if (!slug) return null;
try {



const result = await db.query.people.findFirst({
where: eq(people.slug, slug),

    });
if (!result) {

console.warn(`⚠️ Hero not found: ${slug}`);
return null;

    }
const heroData = result.metadata ?? {};
return {

      ...heroData,
id: result.id,

name: result.name ?? heroData.name,
slug: result.slug,
tmdbPersonId: result.tmdbPersonId ?? heroData.tmdbPersonId,
imdbId: result.imdbId ?? heroData.imdbId,
category: result.category ?? heroData.category,
subcategory: result.subcategory ?? heroData.subcategory,

    };

  } catch (error) {
console.error(`🚨 Database error for slug ${slug}:`, error);
return null;

  }
}

/** Resolve meta image for OpenGraph */

function resolveOgImage(heroData: any) {
if (!heroData) return '/og-image.jpg';
const banner = heroData.images?.banner;
if (!banner) {
const candidate =

      heroData.images?.featured ||
      heroData.images?.avatar ||

      heroData.images?.portrait ||
      (Array.isArray(heroData.images?.gallery) ? heroData.images.gallery[0] : null);

if (typeof candidate === 'string') return candidate;
if (candidate && typeof candidate === 'object') return candidate.url || candidate
return '/og-image.jpg';

  }
if (typeof banner === 'string') return banner;
if (typeof banner === 'object') return banner.url || banner.tmdbPath || banner.pat

return '/og-image.jpg';
}

/** SEO/OG metadata */
export async function generateMetadata({ params }: { params: { slug: string } }) {
try {
const { slug } = params;

const heroData = await getHeroData(slug);
if (!heroData) {
return { title: 'Hero Not Found', description: 'This hero does not exist.' };

    }
const ogImage = resolveOgImage(heroData);
return {
title: `${heroData.name || 'Hero'} - TFIverse`,

description: heroData.title || heroData.bio || 'Learn more about this Telugu c
openGraph: {



title: heroData.name,
description: heroData.title || heroData.bio,
images: [ogImage],

      },

    };
  } catch (error) {

console.error('❌ Metadata generation error:', error);
return { title: 'Error', description: 'An error occurred.' };

  }
}

/** Main page route */
export default async function HeroPage({ params }: { params: { slug: string } }) {
try {
const { slug } = params;
if (!slug) return notFound();
const heroData = await getHeroData(slug);
if (!heroData) {

console.warn(`🔍 Hero page not found for: ${slug}`);
notFound();

    }
return <HeroDetailClient heroData={heroData} />;

  } catch (error) {
console.error('❌ Error loading hero page:', error);
notFound();

  }
}

/** Can be used for static site generation for known slugs */
export async function generateStaticParams() {
try {
const superstars = await db.query.people.findMany({

where: (peopleTbl, { eq }) =>
and(eq(peopleTbl.category, 'hero'), eq(peopleTbl.subcategory, 'superstar'))

columns: { slug: true },
    });

return (superstars || []).map((h) => ({ slug: h.slug }));
  } catch (error) {

console.error('❌ Error generating static params:', error);
return [];

  }
}

  const [isFollowing, setIsFollowing] = useState(false);
  const followerCount = useMemo(

    () => heroData.followerCount || heroData.followers || 0, [heroData]
  );
  const tabs = [
    { id: "overview", label: "Overview" },
    { id: "info", label: "Info" },
    { id: "movies", label: "Movies" },
    { id: "upcoming", label: "Upcoming" },

    { id: "lifestyle", label: "Lifestyle" },
    { id: "awards", label: "Awards" },
    { id: "gallery", label: "Gallery" },
    { id: "trivia", label: "Trivia" },
    { id: "quotes", label: "Quotes" },
    { id: "contribute", label: "Contribute" },
  ];
  function handleFollow() { setIsFollowing(val => !val); }

  return (
    <div className="bg-black min-h-screen">
      {/* Top Navbar */}
      <PremiumNavbar heroName={heroData.name} />
      {/* Tab Navigation */}
      <TabNavigation
        activeTab={activeTab}

        setActiveTab={setActiveTab}
        tabs={tabs}
      />



      {/* Hero Banner */}
      <PremiumHeroBannerV4
        hero={heroData}
        isFollowing={isFollowing}

        followerCount={followerCount}
        onFollow={handleFollow}
      />
      {/* Tab Sections */}
      <div className="max-w-7xl mx-auto px-4 py-8">
        {activeTab === "overview" && <OverviewTab hero={heroData} />}
        {activeTab === "info" && <InfoTab hero={heroData} />}

        {activeTab === "movies" && <MoviesTab hero={heroData} />}
        {activeTab === "upcoming" && <UpcomingTab hero={heroData} />}

        {activeTab === "quotes" && <QuotesTab hero={heroData} />}

        {activeTab === "contribute" && <ContributeTab hero={heroData} />}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

## Error Type
Runtime Error

Error Message

Element type is invalid: expected a string (for built-in components) or a class/function (for
composite components) but got: undefined. You likely forgot to export your component from
the file it's defined in, or you might have mixed up default and named imports.

Check the render method of HeroPage.

at HeroPage (app/tfi-universe/heroes/superstars/[slug]/page.tsx:91:12)

Code Frame

89 |  notFound();
90 |  }

91 |  return ;
|  ^
92 |  } catch (error) {
93 |  console.error('❌ Error loading hero page:', error);
94 |  notFound();

Next.js version: 15.5.6 (Turbopack)

This runtime error means that your code is trying to render a component called
HeroDetailClient (the export from superstar-client.tsx) but it is undefined. This happens
for one of two reasons:

1. You forgot to use export default in superstar-client.tsx

There must be exactly one export default function HeroDetailClient (or export default
...) at the end of superstar-client.tsx.

If you use export { HeroDetailClient }, your import in page.tsx must use curly braces:
import { HeroDetailClient } from './superstar-client'.

Fix:
Make sure the bottom of superstar-client.tsx reads:

export default function HeroDetailClient(props) {
// ...your component code...

}



2. The import in page.tsx is wrong

You should have:

import HeroDetailClient from './superstar-client';

NOT:

import { HeroDetailClient } from './superstar-client';

unless you intentionally changed superstar-client.tsx to be a named export (which is NOT
standard in Next.js).

3. File name/typo issue

Check all these:

The file is named superstar-client.tsx (not superstar-client.jsx or something else).

You don't have both hero-client.tsx and superstar-client.tsx confusing which gets
called.

The exported component spelling matches the import.

4. You moved code but didn’t restart the server

After making structural changes (paths, refactors), restart your Next.js dev server to
clear runtime and turbo/hot reload errors.

How to Fix

1. In app/tfi-universe/heroes/superstars/[slug]/superstar-client.tsx,
ensure the very bottom has:

export default function HeroDetailClient(props) { ... }

2. In page.tsx,
ensure you do:

import HeroDetailClient from './superstar-client';

3. Restart your dev server.

Summary:
You are very close!
This error is ONLY about an incorrect export/import…



Once the default export and import are fixed, your page will render. If you see other missing
components next, just paste the error and you’ll get that part ready-made!

Great question! Your project is very ambitious and well-structured, but you're hitting a few
architectural decisions that will make or break scalability and maintainability. Let me give you
honest feedback and recommendations.

What You're Doing Right ✅

1. Database-first approach (Drizzle + PostgreSQL) instead of JSON files for production data.

2. Dynamic routing with [slug] pages.

3. Separation of concerns (server/client components).

4. Modular structure (categories like heroes, directors, etc.).

5. TMDB integration for rich metadata.

What's Going Wrong / Can Be Improved 🔧

1. Too Many JSON Files in public/data/

You have 28+ categories (heroes, directors, lyricists, etc.) with individual JSON files per
person.

This is not scalable for production. JSON files are fine for prototyping, but:

They don't support queries, filtering, or relationships.

They bloat your repo and slow down deployments.

They're hard to update dynamically.

Solution:

Move ALL data to your PostgreSQL database (which you've started with people table).

Use scripts to seed the database from JSON files once, then delete the JSON files.

Fetch all person data via db.query.people.findFirst() (as you're already doing).



2. 28 Different Templates for Each Category?

You asked: "Should we create 28 templates for one page?"

Answer: NO! Use ONE smart template with conditional sections.

Instead of:

superstar-client.tsx

legend-client.tsx

director-client.tsx

lyricist-client.tsx

... (28 files)

Do this:

app/tfi-universe/[category]/[subcategory]/[slug]/
  ├── page.tsx          (server: fetches person by slug)
  └── person-client.tsx (client: renders based on category/subcategory)

Inside person-client.tsx:

export default function PersonClient({ person }) {
const { category, subcategory } = person;

// Shared sections (all people get these)

const sharedTabs = ['overview', 'info', 'gallery', 'contribute'];

// Conditional sections based on category
const tabs = [...sharedTabs];
if (category === 'hero') tabs.push('movies', 'upcoming', 'awards', 'lifestyle');
if (category === 'director') tabs.push('films', 'awards', 'style');
if (category === 'lyricist') tabs.push('songs', 'albums', 'awards');
// etc.

return <UniversalTemplate person={person} tabs={tabs} />;
}

This way:

One template handles all 28 categories.

Each category gets unique sections conditionally.

You avoid code duplication.



3. Folder Structure: Current vs. Recommended

Current (what you have):

app/tfi-universe/
  heroes/
    superstars/[slug]/
    legends/[slug]/
    rising-stars/[slug]/
  directors/
    maestros/[slug]/

    emerging/[slug]/
  lyricists/[slug]/
  ...28 more categories

Recommended (cleaner, scalable):

app/tfi-universe/
  [category]/
    [subcategory]/
      [slug]/
        page.tsx

        person-client.tsx

Why?

One route pattern handles all people.

URL: /tfi-universe/heroes/superstars/prabhas

URL: /tfi-universe/directors/maestros/ss-rajamouli

URL: /tfi-universe/lyricists/legends/sirivennela

In page.tsx:

export default async function PersonPage({ params }) {
const { category, subcategory, slug } = params;
const person = await db.query.people.findFirst({
where: and(
eq(people.category, category),
eq(people.subcategory, subcategory),

eq(people.slug, slug)
    )
  });
if (!person) notFound();
return <PersonClient person={person} />;

}



4. Should You Keep JSON Files?

Short answer: NO (for production).

What to do:

1. Write a one-time migration script to import all JSON files into your people table.

2. Delete the JSON files from public/data/.

3. Use the database as your single source of truth.

Migration script example:

// scripts/import-json-to-db.ts
import fs from 'fs';
import path from 'path';
import { db } from '@/lib/db';
import { people } from '@/lib/schema';

async function importPeople() {

const dataDir = path.join(process.cwd(), 'public/data');
const categories = fs.readdirSync(dataDir);

for (const category of categories) {
const categoryPath = path.join(dataDir, category);
const subcategories = fs.readdirSync(categoryPath);

for (const subcategory of subcategories) {
const files = fs.readdirSync(path.join(categoryPath, subcategory));

for (const file of files) {
if (!file.endsWith('.json')) continue;
const filePath = path.join(categoryPath, subcategory, file);
const data = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8'));

await db.insert(people).values({
slug: data.slug,
name: data.name,

          category,
          subcategory,

metadata: data, // Store full JSON in metadata column

tmdbPersonId: data.tmdbPersonId,
imdbId: data.imdbId,

        }).onConflictDoNothing();
      }
    }
  }
}

importPeople().then(() => console.log('✅ Import complete'));



5. How Many Client Templates Do You Need?

Answer: 1-3 max.

1. person-client.tsx – Universal template for all people (heroes, directors, etc.).

2. movie-client.tsx (optional) – If movies need a totally different layout.

3. custom-client.tsx (optional) – For edge cases like "awards shows" or "festivals."

Inside person-client.tsx, use conditionals:

{category === 'hero' && <MoviesTab />}
{category === 'director' && <FilmsTab />}
{category === 'lyricist' && <SongsTab />}

Final Recommendation: Your Next Steps

1. Migrate all JSON → Database.

2. Consolidate routing to [category]/[subcategory]/[slug].

3. Build ONE smart template (person-client.tsx) with conditional sections.

4. Delete JSON files after migration.

5. Test with 2-3 categories first (heroes, directors), then scale to all 28.

What You're Doing What You Should Do

JSON files in public/data/ PostgreSQL database only

Manual updates Database-driven, scriptable

Your project is solid, but these changes will make it production-ready and scalable for

Best Practice: Universal Dynamic Person Route

Folder/file setup:

app/
  tfi-universe/
    [category]/
      [subcategory]/

          page.tsx          // <-- One file for ALL people types
          person-client.tsx // <-- One file for ALL people types

/tfi-universe/heroes/superstars/prabhas

/tfi-universe/directors/maestros/ss-rajamouli

/tfi-universe/heroines/queens/kajal-aggarwal

Your files will receive params.category, params.subcategory, and params.slug to fetch
and render the correct data and UI shapes.

export default async function PersonPage({ params }) {
const { category, subcategory, slug } = params;

eq(people.category, category),
eq(people.subcategory, subcategory),
eq(people.slug, slug)

    )
  });

You are absolutely right:

This approach:

Lets you have a different set of tabs and tab content for EVERY category or subcategory.

Keeps ALL your general logic and layout code DRY and easy to extend.

usually find most categories can be handled this way.

When To Split Into More Than One Template

Only if you have wildly different layouts between categories (for example, a “festival”
page that is nothing like any “person” page).

Even then, you can just switch on the category/subcategory in your [slug]/page.tsx and
render a totally custom client component if you want.

  }

}

How many templates needed for production?

One universal template (person-client.tsx) for people.

Optionally, one extra for movies, one extra for festivals, etc.

What about tab components?

You can make separate files for each tab section (OverviewTab.tsx, MoviesTab.tsx...), but
you do not need 28 top-level page templates.

You're absolutely right! That's a very valid concern and a smart approach. Let me explain why
separate files per category is actually the better choice for your use case:

Why Separate Files Per Category is Better for You:

✅ 1. Custom Backgrounds & Theming

Heroes → Action-themed backgrounds, bold colors

Heroines → Elegant backgrounds, makeup/fashion illustrations, softer tones

Directors → Cinematic backgrounds, film reel imagery

Lyricists → Music/note-themed backgrounds

Each category gets its own visual identity.

✅ 2. Easier Maintenance

If you need to update the "Heroine" page layout, you only touch that one file.

No risk of breaking the "Hero" or "Director" pages.

Each file is 500-800 lines max instead of one giant 10,000+ line monster.

✅ 3. Better Performance

Next.js can code-split each category file separately.

Users visiting a hero page don't download the heroine/director code.

Faster load times, smaller bundles.

✅ 4. Team Collaboration

If you ever work with someone else, separate files = no merge conflicts.

One person can work on heroes, another on heroines, simultaneously.



✅ 5. Cleaner Code

Each file is focused and readable.

No massive if/else or switch statements.

Easier to debug and test.

Recommended Folder Structure (Separate Files Approach):

app/tfi-universe/
  heroes/

    [subcategory]/
      [slug]/
        page.tsx         // Server-side data fetch
        hero-client.tsx  // Hero-specific UI (action theme, tabs, sections)

  heroines/
    [subcategory]/

      [slug]/
        page.tsx            // Server-side data fetch
        heroine-client.tsx  // Heroine-specific UI (elegant theme, makeup imagery, t

  directors/
    [subcategory]/
      [slug]/

        page.tsx            // Server-side data fetch
        director-client.tsx // Director-specific UI (cinematic theme, tabs)

  lyricists/
    [slug]/
      page.tsx             // Server-side data fetch
      lyricist-client.tsx  // Lyricist-specific UI (music theme, tabs)

  // ... and so on for all 28 categories

How This Works:

1. Each page.tsx is basically the same:

// app/tfi-universe/heroes/[subcategory]/[slug]/page.tsx
export default async function HeroPage({ params }) {
const hero = await fetchHeroData(params.slug);
if (!hero) notFound();

return <HeroClient hero={hero} />;
}



2. Each -client.tsx has custom design:

// app/tfi-universe/heroes/[subcategory]/[slug]/hero-client.tsx
'use client';
export default function HeroClient({ hero }) {
return (
<div className="hero-page-background">

      {/* Custom hero tabs, action-themed sections, etc. */}
</div>

  );
}

// app/tfi-universe/heroines/[subcategory]/[slug]/heroine-client.tsx
'use client';
export default function HeroineClient({ heroine }) {
return (
<div className="heroine-page-background">

      {/* Custom heroine tabs, makeup/fashion illustrations, etc. */}

</div>
  );
}

What About Code Duplication?

You can still share common components across all categories:

components/
  person/
    TabNavigation.tsx      // Shared tab component
    OverviewTab.tsx         // Generic overview layout
    GalleryTab.tsx          // Generic gallery
    SocialMediaTab.tsx      // Generic social media display

    ContributeTab.tsx       // Generic contribute form

Each category-specific client file imports and reuses these shared components, but adds its
own:

Custom background

Custom colors/theme

Category-specific tabs (e.g., "Makeup & Fashion" for heroines, "Filmmaking Style" for
directors)



Summary: Separate Files vs. Universal Template

Approach Pros Cons Best For

Custom themes, easy Your project (custom
Separate More files to manage (but

maintenance, smaller files, backgrounds, 28 categories,
Files organized)

better performance visual identity per category)

Giant file (10k+ lines), harder
Universal Simple projects with minimal

Less files, DRY code to theme per category, risk of
Template visual differences

breaking everything

Final Recommendation for You:

Go with separate files per category.
You'll have 28 client files, but each will be:

Clean (500-800 lines max)

Themeable (custom backgrounds, colors, illustrations)

Maintainable (change one category without affecting others)

Performant (code-split per category)

Next Steps:

1. For each of your 28 categories, you'll create a dedicated -client.tsx file.

2. Share common components (tabs, sections) across all.

3. Customize each client file with category-specific theme/background/tabs.

director) and you can replicate it for the rest! Just let me know. 🚀

Database Schema (What You Need)

1. people table (You have this)

- id (primary key)
- slug (unique)
- name
- category (hero, heroine, director, etc.)

- subcategory (superstar, legend, diva, etc.)
- tmdb_person_id
- imdb_id
- metadata (JSONB - stores ALL the template data)
- created_at
- updated_at



2. movies table (You need to create)

- id (primary key)
- slug (unique)
- title
- tmdb_movie_id (unique)
- imdb_id
- release_date
- runtime

- budget
- revenue
- poster_url
- backdrop_url
- metadata (JSONB - stores cast, crew, genres, etc.)
- created_at
- updated_at

3. movie_credits table (Junction table - IMPORTANT!)

- id (primary key)
- movie_id (foreign key -> movies)

- person_id (foreign key -> people)
- role_type (actor, director, producer, etc.)
- character_name (for actors)
- department (for crew)
- order_index (for sorting)
- created_at

4. contributions table (For tracking edits)

- id (primary key)
- user_id (foreign key -> users, if you have auth)
- person_id (foreign key -> people) - nullable
- movie_id (foreign key -> movies) - nullable

- edit_type (personal_info, filmography, awards, etc.)
- field_changed (specific field edited)
- old_value (JSONB)
- new_value (JSONB)
- status (pending, approved, rejected)
- points_awarded (default 0, set when approved)
- discord_webhook_sent (boolean)

- admin_notes
- created_at
- updated_at



5. contribution_points table (Leaderboard aggregate)

- id (primary key)
- user_id (unique)
- total_points
- total_contributions
- approved_contributions
- rejected_contributions
- last_contribution_at

- rank (computed)

Code:

// app/tfi-universe/heroes/page.tsx
export default async function HeroesPage() {
const subcategories = await db.query.people

    .findMany({
where: eq(people.category, 'hero'),

columns: { subcategory: true },
    })
    .then(data => {

// Group by subcategory and count
const counts = {};



      data.forEach(p => {
        counts[p.subcategory] = (counts[p.subcategory] || 0) + 1;
      });

return Object.entries(counts).map(([name, count]) => ({name, count}));

    });

return <HeroesCategoryGrid subcategories={subcategories} />;
}

B. Superstars Listing Page (/tfi-universe/heroes/superstars)

Shows all heroes with subcategory "superstar"

Code:

// app/tfi-universe/heroes/superstars/page.tsx
export default async function SuperstarsPage() {
const superstars = await db.query.people.findMany({
where: and(
eq(people.category, 'hero'),
eq(people.subcategory, 'superstar')

    ),
orderBy: [desc(people.updated_at)],

  });

return <SuperstarsGrid heroes={superstars} />;
}

C. Individual Hero Page (/tfi-universe/heroes/superstars/prabhas)

Server Component (Data Fetch):

// app/tfi-universe/heroes/superstars/[slug]/page.tsx
import { db } from '@/lib/db';
import { people, movieCredits, movies, contributions } from '@/lib/schema';
import { eq, and } from 'drizzle-orm';

import SuperstarClient from './superstar-client';

export default async function SuperstarPage({ params }) {
const { slug } = params;

// Fetch person data
const hero = await db.query.people.findFirst({

where: and(
eq(people.slug, slug),
eq(people.category, 'hero'),
eq(people.subcategory, 'superstar')

    ),
  });

if (!hero) notFound();

// Fetch filmography



const filmography = await db
    .select({

movie: movies,
credit: movieCredits,

    })
    .from(movieCredits)
    .leftJoin(movies, eq(movieCredits.movieId, movies.id))
    .where(eq(movieCredits.personId, hero.id))
    .orderBy(desc(movies.releaseDate));

// Fetch contribution stats for this hero

const contributionStats = await db.query.contributions.findMany({
where: and(
eq(contributions.personId, hero.id),
eq(contributions.status, 'approved')

    ),
with: {
user: true, // Include user info

    },
limit: 10,
orderBy: [desc(contributions.createdAt)],

  });

return (
<SuperstarClient

hero={hero}
filmography={filmography}
contributions={contributionStats}

    />
  );
}

Client Component (UI):

return (

        {/* Tab Navigation */}

            {tabs.map(tab => (

</TabsTrigger>

          {/* Tab Content */}

  );
}

Phase 4: Contribution System

A. Contribution Submission Form

// components/ContributeTab.tsx
'use client';

export default function ContributeTab({ personId, contributions }) {
const [editType, setEditType] = useState('');
const [fieldChanged, setFieldChanged] = useState('');
const [newValue, setNewValue] = useState('');

const submitEdit = async () => {
const res = await fetch('/api/contributions/submit', {

method: 'POST',
body: JSON.stringify({

        personId,



        editType,
        fieldChanged,
        newValue,
      }),

    });

if (res.ok) {
// Send Discord webhook
await fetch('/api/webhooks/discord', {
method: 'POST',
body: JSON.stringify({

message: `New edit request for ${personId}: ${editType}`,
        }),
      });

alert('Edit submitted! You will get points once approved.');
    }
  };

return (
<div>

      ```
<h2>Contribute to this profile</h2>

      ```
      {/* Form for submitting edits */}

<h3>Recent Contributions</h3>
<ul>

        {contributions.map(c => (
<li key={c.id}>

            {c.user.name} edited {c.fieldChanged} (+{c.pointsAwarded} points)
</li>

        ))}
</ul>

</div>
  );
}

B. API Route for Contribution Submission

// app/api/contributions/submit/route.ts
import { db } from '@/lib/db';
import { contributions } from '@/lib/schema';

export async function POST(req: Request) {

const { personId, editType, fieldChanged, newValue } = await req.json();

await db.insert(contributions).values({
    personId,
    editType,
    fieldChanged,
    newValue,

status: 'pending',
  });



return Response.json({ success: true });
}

⚠️ POTENTIAL LOOPHOLES & FIXES:

1. Data Duplication

Problem: Storing full metadata JSONB in people table might get huge.
Fix: ✅ Store full JSON in people.metadata but cache frequently accessed fields as separate
columns (e.g., name, birth_date, total_movies).

2. Movie-Person Relationships

Problem: Without movie_credits junction table, you can't query "all movies by Prabhas"
efficiently.
Fix: ✅ Create movie_credits table (shown above).

3. Contribution Spam

Problem: Users might spam edit requests to farm points.
Fix:

Rate limit: Max 10 contributions per user per day

Require email verification before allowing contributions

Penalty for rejected contributions (e.g., -5 points)

4. Discord Webhook Spam

Problem: Every edit request sends a Discord message = spam.
Fix:

Batch notifications (e.g., every 10 minutes, send summary of pending edits)

Only send webhook for "high-priority" fields (e.g., birthdate, filmography)



5. SEO & Performance

Problem: 28 categories × 100 people = 2800+ pages. Need good SEO.
Fix:

Generate sitemap.xml dynamically

Use Next.js ISR (Incremental Static Regeneration) for person pages

Add metadata/OpenGraph for each page

6. Image Hosting

Problem: 5000 movies × 2 images (poster + backdrop) = 10,000 images. Where to store?
Fix:

Use TMDB CDN URLs directly (free, fast)

For custom images, use Cloudflare Images or AWS S3 + CloudFront

✅ Your Plan: Step-by-Step

1. People Table

Fill core data for each prominent person (use your JSONs or AI Jinja templates).

Store as one person per row: hero, heroine, director, etc.

For now, a small seed (~28) is perfect, then you’ll scale up.

Use your TMDB fetcher script (JS/web or Node) to get Telugu/dubbed movie JSON files.

Each movie row: TMDB ID, title, year, poster, full metadata JSON, and (later) OTT URLs.

For OTT URLs, after movies are in DB, run a daily script to check/fetch up to 100 new OTT

OTTPlay, and CineTrak).



3. Connecting People ⇄ Movies

After you have people and movies in your DB, create a third table:

movie_credits: connects people ⇄ movies by role (actor, director, lyricist, etc.), using
TMDB cast/crew data.

No duplicate movies will be shown as you’ll deduplicate by TMDB ID (these are
unique).

4. Rendering UI

no duplicate issues.

5. Contribution + Leaderboard

Sends to Discord webhook for review (secured log).

Saves to a contributions table for admin approval.

If approved, update that person/movie, give user points shown per-person and for all
their edits combined.

Prabhas’s page’s “contributions” tab: Query contributions for that person only.

Leaderboard/main page: Query users and sum their approved points.

🔑 Loophole Protection & Improvements

Deduplication: Only store movies by TMDB ID (PRIMARY KEY tmdb_id). Joins are always by
this ID. Always check before insert.

API Limits: Schedule your OTT fetch script via cron; mark ottUrls_fetched
boolean/timestamp per movie so you never hit the same API twice unnecessarily.

Data Quality: For AI-generated people bios, make sure to fact-check, avoid hallucinations,
and have the admin review for accuracy.

Scalability: Use LIMIT & pagination everywhere, especially on lists for heroes/movies.

Error Reporting: Log failed fetches for movies/ott, so you can retry only failed ones the
next day.

User Spam: Limit submissions per user per day, and review before approval/point rewards.
