⚡️ Example: Deduplication and Linking (Pseudo-Code)

// On fetch, before inserting a movie:
if (!db.movies.find(mv => mv.tmdb_id === movie.tmdb_id)) {

    db.movies.insert(movie);
}

// When displaying filmography for a person:
const person = db.people.find(p => p.slug === "prabhas");
const credits = db.movie_credits.filter(c => c.person_id === person.id);
const filmography = credits.map(c => db.movies.find(m => m.id === c.movie_id));

🚨 Loopholes & Pitfalls to Avoid

Duplicate import: Always upsert (update/insert) by TMDB ID/key.

Dangling credits: If a TMDB cast/crew person isn’t in your DB yet, create stub profiles for
later enrichment.

OTT API Rate-Limits: If the daily cap is hit, schedule next batch for tomorrow, always
keep a “done” flag per movie.

User-edit spam: Only award points on admin approval, not instantly.

Don't trust API bios for people!: Always curate, as they can have errors, especially for
Indian film personalities.

1. Data Model & Database

A. People Table

One row per person (category, subcategory, metadata JSON, etc.).

Store only unique (no duplicate slugs).

Fetch 5,000+ from TMDB. Store unique by TMDB ID, with name, year, poster, and full

Join table connecting people ⇄ movies (person_id, movie_id, role_type, character,

Save every user edit as a contribution: who, where, what they changed.

Store available OTT URLs with each movie row.

For each new movie:

For any TMDB person not in your DB, create a stub (to be later filled with core data).

Never duplicate movie credits (person_id + movie_id + role_type keys).

Daily script (scheduled job) fetches 100 URLs not yet fetched, using APIs such as
JustWatch, OTTPlay, or similar (with backups for rate limits).

🎯 RECOMMENDED ORDER (STEP-BY-STEP)

3. Updates ott_urls JSONB column and sets ott_fetched = true

4. Logs errors for failed fetches

Schedule this script to run daily via cron job or Vercel Cron

Why last? OTT URLs are nice-to-have but not required for MVP. Users can still browse

BASE_URL: 'https://api.themoviedb.org/3',

TEST_MOVIES: [1403735, 579974, 811941, 78581, 360133]

};

function log(msg, type='info') {
const el = document.getElementById('console');
const ts = new Date().toLocaleTimeString();
const prefix = `[${ts}] `;
const wrap = document.createElement('div');

  wrap.textContent = prefix + msg;
  el.appendChild(wrap);

  el.scrollTop = el.scrollHeight;
}

function updateStats() {
document.getElementById('stat-movies').textContent = STATE.moviesList.length;
document.getElementById('stat-fetched').textContent = STATE.fetchedMovies.length;
document.getElementById('stat-pages').textContent = STATE.currentPage;

if (STATE.startTime) {
const seconds = Math.floor((Date.now()-STATE.startTime)/1000);
document.getElementById('stat-time').textContent = seconds > 60 ? (Math.floor(se

  }
}

function setBar(id, pct, text) {

const el = document.getElementById(id);
  el.style.width = pct + '%';



  el.textContent = text || Math.floor(pct)+'%';
}
async function sleep(ms){ return new Promise(r=>setTimeout(r,ms)); }

/* ================ API HELPER ================ */
async function fetchWithRetry(url, attempts = CONFIG.RETRY_ATTEMPTS) {
for (let i=0;i<attempts;i++){
try {
const res = await fetch(url);
if (!res.ok) throw new Error('HTTP '+res.status);
return await res.json();

    } catch (err) {
log(`Retry ${i+1}/${attempts} for ${url} — ${err.message}`, 'warn');
if (i === attempts-1) throw err;
await sleep(CONFIG.RETRY_DELAY*(i+1));

    }
  }
}

/* ===== PURE TMDB FETCH (NO ROLE CATEGORY, NO DATA CHANGE) ===== */
async function getMovieDetailsOriginal(movieId) {
const key = document.getElementById('api-key').value.trim();
const url = `${CONFIG.BASE_URL}/movie/${movieId}?api_key=${key}&append_to_response
const data = await fetchWithRetry(url);
// Don't mutate, don't sort, just return JSON as-is

return data;
}

async function runFetchingPhase() {

}

Here’s a clear production-ready plan for your database tables, linking logic, and OTT URL
providers—using your pure TMDB JSON files (like the one you shared) and your current
people table with TMDB person IDs.

1. Database Tables & Columns to Create

a) movies

Column Type Notes

id SERIAL Primary key (internal)

tmdb_id INTEGER Unique TMDB movie id

imdb_id VARCHAR For external links

title VARCHAR TMDB or original title

year INTEGER Extract from release_date

slug VARCHAR for URLs

metadata JSONB Full TMDB JSON

poster_url VARCHAR From TMDB

backdrop_url VARCHAR From TMDB

ott_urls JSONB Fetched from below

ott_fetched BOOLEAN Has OTT been fetched?

created_at TIMESTAMP

updated_at TIMESTAMP

Primary Key: tmdb_id (unique—no duplicates)

Store full movie JSON with all cast/crew data in metadata so you have everything for
queries.

b) people
You already have this, linked by tmdb_person_id column.
No changes needed ; just keep TMDB person IDs.

c) movie_credits

Column Type Notes

id SERIAL Primary key

movie_id INTEGER FK to movies.id

person_id INTEGER FK to people.id

tmdb_person_id INTEGER TMDB actor/crew id (same as people table)

role_type VARCHAR ‘cast’ or ‘crew’



Column Type Notes

character VARCHAR Only if cast

job VARCHAR Only if crew

department VARCHAR Only if crew

order_index INTEGER If exists

You will parse the credits.cast and credits.crew arrays in your movie JSON to populate
this table.

Connect by TMDB id: Use the tmdb_person_id to ensure a perfect join between people
and credits.

2. Query Logic

A) Prabhas Page – Filmography Tab

On /heroes/superstars/prabhas, use Prabhas’s TMDB person ID
(people.tmdb_person_id).

Query movie_credits for all rows with tmdb_person_id = Prabhas’s TMDB ID.

Join to movies to get each movie (details/poster/year/metadata).

Result: Filmography tab shows all unique movies Prabhas acted in.

B) Movies Page – No Duplicates

List all movies from the movies table (one per tmdb_id).

No duplicate movies ever because of your unique constraint.

3. OTT URLs — Providers, How to Fetch, Daily Limits

A) Main APIs in India
All can use TMDB IDs or IMDb IDs for lookups:

JustWatch (https://www.justwatch.com/in)

Pros: Biggest, covers Netflix, Prime, Hotstar, SonyLIV, Zee5, SunNXT, etc.

API is unofficial—use at own risk, or web scrape if you work privately.

Usage is practically unlimited for small projects, but for big scale, limit to ~100 req/day for
safety.

OTTPlay (https://ottplay.com)

Pros: High Indian catalog, covers many Telugu movies.

API available for partners, typically requires signup/negotiation.

B) Other Options



Yidio (Global, not all Telugu)

ReelGood (good API, India coverage varies)

JustWatch (Global API): Can use with country code "IN".

C) Daily Fetching Limits

JustWatch (Unofficial/Private): No hard API key, but use 100 requests/day to avoid
block/ban.

OTTPlay: For official API, depends on your contract after signup.

What To Do:

Start with JustWatch’s unofficial API/web scrape for “IN” (check with their TOS if for public
use).

Set script to fetch/refresh 100 movies per day.

Store each movie’s OTT platforms/URLs as JSON in ott_urls, set ott_fetched = true.

4. Linking Movies and People in DB

When importing a movie's JSON:

For each entry in credits.cast and credits.crew, check if their TMDB ID exists in
people.

If not, create a stub people row with only tmdb_person_id and name.

Create a movie_credits row for every cast/crew—tie to person via tmdb_person_id.

NEXT STEPS Checklist

1. Create/verify tables:movies (unique by tmdb_id), movie_credits.

2. Import movie JSONs: Fill movies, then explode credits.cast/credits.crew into
movie_credits.

3. Querying : Use joins by tmdb_person_id for people ⇄ movies.

4. OTT urls: Register on JustWatch (no key needed for scraping), plan for 100/day, store in
ott_urls JSON.

5. Result: Filmography per person, browse all movies, OTT links per movie, no duplicates!

If you want any code (Node/Postgres/Drizzle schema, or ETL script for credits): just say "give
code", and specify which script you want first! [27] [28]

You are correct—the TMDB movie ID is always under "id" in the JSON (not "tmdb_id").
When designing your DB and scripts, always extract the TMDB movie ID from the id key in
the JSON file, like this:

{
"homepage": "",
"id": 579974, // TMDB movie ID (use this value for your tmdb_id column)

"imdb_id": "tt8178634",
  ...
}

For your movies table, tmdb_id will be set using that "id" field from the JSON.

For your people table, same logic—use the person’s "id" TMDB field as tmdb_person_id.

OTT URLs: Free API Options, Registration, and Daily Limits

A) JustWatch

Official API: Not public. Most projects use their unofficial API or web scrape.

Unofficial API:

Request:

GET https://apis.justwatch.com/content/titles/movie/{tmdb_id}/locale/en_IN

You do not need to register or use an API key for basic access, but you must be careful
not to spam—set your script to max 100/day.

Limit: Unofficial; use <100 requests per day for safety.



B) OTTPlay

API access only for business partners (not public for devs).

Loads more Telugu content than many, but you must negotiate access by contacting their
support or business team.

Usage: Request business access via email or their contact form.

Limit: As per contract.

C) Other Sources

ReelGood (US, some India): Not as good India coverage.

Yidio: US/UK focus.

RECOMMENDATION:

Start with JustWatch: It's free, doesn’t need a key for scraping/basic API calls, and has the
widest coverage for India OTT platforms like Netflix, Prime, Hotstar, Zee5, SunNXT,
SonyLIV, Eros, and others.

Limit to 100 movies/day (respectful, safe).

If you want more than 100/day or require advanced data/guaranteed availability, reach
out to OTTPlay or JustWatch for a commercial agreement.

Sample Table Recap:

Table Field Source Key Usage

movies tmdb_id JSON "id" Primary, unique movie link

movies imdb_id JSON "imdb_id" For external links/OTT lookups

movies ott_urls From OTT API Store all OTT URLs as JSON

people tmdb_person_id JSON "id" For joining credits/person to movies

In your code/scripts:

Always assign movie.tmdb_id = json.id

For all OTT API scripts, fetch using either tmdb_id or imdb_id as supported.

movie ID, like for tmdb id 579974:

JustWatch Unofficial API OTT Lookup Example

API Endpoint (India locale):

https://apis.justwatch.com/content/titles/movie/579974/locale/en_IN

Replace 579974 with any TMDB movie ID.

Locale en_IN is for India. For Telugu focus, this is best.

How to Use:

Just make a GET request to that URL.

Parse the result JSON for streaming providers (Netflix, Prime, Hotstar, etc.), their URLs,
and other details.

No API Key Needed

The endpoint is public/unofficial—no registration or API key required.

Still, limit to 100 requests per day to avoid bans and be respectful.

Example Usage:

fetch('https://apis.justwatch.com/content/titles/movie/579974/locale/en_IN')
  .then(res => res.json())
  .then(data => {

// Parse for streaming offers

console.log(data);
  });

This gives you the OTT platforms and their URLs for Telugu, Indian movies by TMDB movie
ID!

Here’s exactly where and how to use the JustWatch OTT API URL in your workflow:

1. When to Use the API

After you have imported the movie data from TMDB to your database

(ott_fetched = false)

2. How to Call the API

For each movie (example: TMDB ID 579974), make a GET request:

https://apis.justwatch.com/content/titles/movie/579974/locale/en_IN

No headers, key, or auth needed.

3. Where to Use It in Your Workflow

A) In Your OTT Fetcher Script

(Backend Node.js script or cron job)

Each night (or on-demand), iterate over 100 movies missing OTT info.

For each movie, call the URL above, get JSON back.

B) In Your Database Update Step

Parse the returned JSON for .offers array; this contains all the streaming platforms and
links.

Save these URLs and metadata (provider, link, type) into your movie’s ott_urls column.

Mark the movie’s ott_fetched = true so you don’t hit the same movie again.

4. Sample Node.js Code Block (for backend/ETL)

const fetch = require('node-fetch');

// Function that takes tmdb_id and returns OTT URLs array
async function fetchOttUrls(tmdb_id) {
const baseUrl = `https://apis.justwatch.com/content/titles/movie/${tmdb_id}/locale
const data = await fetch(baseUrl).then(res => res.json());



// Offers is usually an array of provider data
if (!data.offers) return [];
return data.offers.map(o => ({
provider: o.provider_id,

name: o.provider_name,
url: o.urls && o.urls.standard_web,
type: o.monetization_type // e.g. 'flatrate', 'rent', 'buy'

  }));
}

// Usage example:

const movieId = 579974;
const ottOffers = await fetchOttUrls(movieId);
console.log(ottOffers);

In production: Store ottOffers as JSONB in the movie’s row in your DB.

5. Where to Trigger This Code

Daily cron job (recommended): Check DB for 100 movies where ott_fetched = false, run
the code above, update each movie.

Edit page/OTT refresh button (optional): On your dashboard, allow admins to refresh OTT
URLs for any movie.

Bulk import: As part of movie data enrichment pipeline after TMDB movie data is loaded.

Summary

API URL is only used in your backend/data enrichment, never exposed on frontend.

Fetch, parse, and save OTT streaming info as part of your DB.

Daily limit: 100 movies to stay within best-practices for unofficial API.

B) What to Extract from TMDB Movie JSON

From each movie JSON file (like rrr-579974.json), extract:

Field JSON Key Use

tmdb_id id Unique movie identifier

imdb_id imdb_id For external links/OTT lookup

title title Display name

original_title original_title Telugu original name

slug Generate from title + id URL-friendly

year Extract from release_date Filtering

runtime runtime Display

poster_path poster_path Image URL

backdrop_path backdrop_path Hero image



Field JSON Key Use

overview overview Synopsis

tagline tagline Short description

status status Released/Upcoming

release_date release_date Sort/filter

vote_average vote_average Rating

vote_count vote_count Rating count

popularity popularity Sorting

budget budget Stats

revenue revenue Stats

metadata entire JSON Store everything for future use

C) Import Script (Node.js)

// scripts/import-movies.js
import fs from 'fs';
import path from 'path';

import { db } from './db'; // Your Drizzle setup
import { movies } from './schema';

const moviesDir = './tmdb-movies'; // Your downloaded JSON files folder

async function importMovies() {
const files = fs.readdirSync(moviesDir).filter(f => f.endsWith('.json'));

for (const file of files) {
const data = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(path.join(moviesDir, file), 'utf8'));

const slug = `${data.title || data.original_title}-${data.id}`
      .toLowerCase()
      .replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, '-')

      .replace(/^-+|-+$/g, '');

const year = data.release_date ? new Date(data.release_date).getFullYear() : null

await db.insert(movies).values({
tmdb_id: data.id,
imdb_id: data.imdb_id,

title: data.title,
original_title: data.original_title,

      slug,
      year,

runtime: data.runtime,
poster_path: data.poster_path,
backdrop_path: data.backdrop_path,
overview: data.overview,

tagline: data.tagline,



status: data.status,
release_date: data.release_date,
vote_average: data.vote_average,
vote_count: data.vote_count,

popularity: data.popularity,
budget: data.budget,
revenue: data.revenue,
metadata: data // Store full JSON

    }).onConflictDoUpdate({
target: movies.tmdb_id,
set: { updated_at: new Date() }

    });

console.log(`✓ Imported: ${data.title} (${data.id})`);
  }
}

importMovies();

Phase 2: Movie Credits (Link People ⇄ Movies)

A) Create movie_credits Table

CREATE TABLE movie_credits (
  id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
  movie_id INTEGER REFERENCES movies(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  person_id INTEGER REFERENCES people(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  tmdb_person_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
  role_type VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL, -- 'cast' or 'crew'

character VARCHAR(500), -- Only for cast
  job VARCHAR(100), -- Only for crew
  department VARCHAR(100), -- Only for crew
  order_index INTEGER,
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE INDEX idx_credits_movie ON movie_credits(movie_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_credits_person ON movie_credits(person_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_credits_tmdb_person ON movie_credits(tmdb_person_id);

B) Import Credits from Movie JSON

// Add to import-movies.js after movie insert

// Process cast
if (data.credits?.cast) {
for (const castMember of data.credits.cast) {
// Find person in your people table by tmdb_person_id

const person = await db.select().from(people)
      .where(eq(people.tmdb_person_id, castMember.id))
      .limit(1);



// If person doesn't exist, create stub
let personId;
if (person.length === 0) {

const [newPerson] = await db.insert(people).values({
tmdb_person_id: castMember.id,
name: castMember.name,
slug: castMember.name.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-'),
category: 'actor', // Default
metadata: castMember

      }).returning({ id: people.id });

      personId = newPerson.id;
    } else {
      personId = person[0].id;
    }

// Insert credit
await db.insert(movieCredits).values({

movie_id: movieRow.id,
person_id: personId,
tmdb_person_id: castMember.id,
role_type: 'cast',
character: castMember.character,
order_index: castMember.order

    });

  }
}

// Process crew (same logic for crew)
if (data.credits?.crew) {

// Same as above, but with role_type='crew', job, department

  }
}

Phase 3: OTT URLs (Streaming Links)

A) What's Missing : Full Movie URLs

TMDB does NOT provide full movie streaming URLs

JustWatch API provides OTT platform info (Netflix, Prime, Hotstar, etc.)

But NOT direct video URLs (those are proprietary to platforms)

B) What You CAN Get from JustWatch

{
"provider_id": 8,
"provider_name": "Netflix",
"monetization_type": "flatrate",
"presentation_type": "hd",
"urls": {



"standard_web": "https://www.netflix.com/title/81280459"
}

}

This gives you the platform landing page (where users can watch)

NOT the direct video stream URL (those require user login)

C) OTT Fetcher Script

// scripts/fetch-ott-urls.js
import fetch from 'node-fetch';
import { db } from './db';
import { movies } from './schema';

async function fetchOttUrls() {
// Get 100 movies without OTT data
const moviesToFetch = await db.select()

    .from(movies)
    .where(eq(movies.ott_fetched, false))
    .limit(100);

for (const movie of moviesToFetch) {
try {
const url = `https://apis.justwatch.com/content/titles/movie/${movie.tmdb_id}/
const response = await fetch(url);
const data = await response.json();

const ottUrls = data.offers?.map(o => ({

provider: o.provider_name,
provider_id: o.provider_id,
type: o.monetization_type,
url: o.urls?.standard_web

      })) || [];

await db.update(movies)

        .set({
ott_urls: ottUrls,
ott_fetched: true,
updated_at: new Date()

        })
        .where(eq(movies.id, movie.id));

console.log(`✓ Fetched OTT for: ${movie.title}`);
await new Promise(r => setTimeout(r, 1000)); // Rate limit

    } catch (err) {
console.error(`✗ Error for ${movie.title}:`, err.message);

    }
  }
}

fetchOttUrls();

CREATE TABLE awards (
  id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,

  entity_type VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL, -- 'movie' or 'person'
  entity_id INTEGER NOT NULL,
  award_name VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
  category VARCHAR(200),
year INTEGER,

  status VARCHAR(20), -- 'won', 'nominated'
  source VARCHAR(50), -- 'user_contribution', 'wikipedia', 'manual'

  verified BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  added_by INTEGER, -- user_id
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE INDEX idx_awards_entity ON awards(entity_type, entity_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_awards_year ON awards(year);

NO, you do NOT add manually! The import script does it automatically for all 5000 movies! Let
me explain clearly:

🤖 AUTOMATED URL CONVERSION (Zero Manual Work)

How It Works:

The import script reads each JSON file and automatically adds the base URL prefix to every
path. You write the logic ONCE, and it processes all 5000 movies.

Step-by-Step Process:

Step 1: Import Script Reads JSON

Script opens rrr-579974.json

Finds: "poster_path": "/u0XUBNQWlOvrh0Gd97ARGpIkL0.jpg"



Step 2: Script Adds Base URL (Automatic)

Script checks: Is there a poster_path?

If yes: Combine base URL + path

Result: https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/original/u0XUBNQWlOvrh0Gd97ARGpIkL0.jpg

Step 3: Save to Database

Store the FULL URL in poster_path column

Repeat for all images/videos

✅ The Logic (Pseudo-Code Explanation):

For each movie JSON file:
  1. Read the file
  2. Extract poster_path value (example: "/abc123.jpg")
  3. If poster_path exists:
     - Full URL = "https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/original" + poster_path

     - Save: "https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/original/abc123.jpg"
  4. Extract backdrop_path
  5. If backdrop_path exists:
     - Full URL = "https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/original" + backdrop_path
     - Save: "https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/original/xyz789.jpg"
  6. Extract videos array
  7. For each video:

     - If site is "YouTube":
       - Full URL = "https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=" + video.key
       - Save: "https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=FYt_srWx_V8"
  8. Save movie to database

Repeat for next file
```

---

### **Real Example (What Happens):**

**Input (from JSON):**
``````json

{
  "poster_path": "/u0XUBNQWlOvrh0Gd97ARGpIkL0.jpg",
  "backdrop_path": "/i0Y0wP8H6SRgjr6QmuwbtQbS24D.jpg",
  "videos": {
    "results": [
      {
        "key": "FYt_srWx_V8",

        "site": "YouTube"
      }
    ]
  }
}
```



**Output (saved to database):**
```json```
{

  "poster_url": "https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/original/u0XUBNQWlOvrh0Gd97ARGpIkL0.jpg
  "backdrop_url": "https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/original/i0Y0wP8H6SRgjr6QmuwbtQbS24D
  "trailer_url": "https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=FYt_srWx_V8"
}
```

---

### **For Multiple Images/Videos:**

TMDB gives you arrays of images and videos. The script loops through each one:

**Images Array Example:**
``````json

"images": {
  "posters": [
    {"file_path": "/poster1.jpg"},
    {"file_path": "/poster2.jpg"},
    {"file_path": "/poster3.jpg"}
  ]
}

```

**Script Processing:**

Loop through each poster:

1. poster1: https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/original/poster1.jpg

2. poster2: https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/original/poster2.jpg

3. poster3: https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/original/poster3.jpg

Save array to metadata JSON column

## **📋 Complete Workflow Continued:**

### **Step 5: Link Cast/Crew to Movies**

- Parse `credits.cast` array from movie JSON
- For each cast member:
  - Check if person exists in `people` table (by tmdb_person_id)
  - If NO: Create new person record (stub with basic info)
  - If YES: Use existing person_id

  - Insert row into `movie_credits` table linking movie ↔ person

- Parse `credits.crew` array
- Same process as cast



**Result:** 
- Every movie is linked to all its actors/crew
- Prabhas page shows all his movies via `movie_credits` join
- Movie page shows all cast/crew via reverse join

---

### **Step 6: Fetch OTT URLs (Automated Daily)**

- Daily cron job runs OTT fetcher script
- Selects 100 movies where `ott_fetched = false`

- For each movie:
  - Call JustWatch API with tmdb_id
  - Get OTT platforms (Netflix, Prime, etc.)
  - Store in `ott_urls` JSONB column
  - Mark `ott_fetched = true`
- Next day: Process next 100 movies
- After ~2 months: All movies have OTT data

---

### **Step 7: User Edit System (Phase 2)**

**Frontend Edit Button:**
- User visits Prabhas page

- Sees "Edit" button (if logged in)
- Clicks edit → Opens edit form

**What Users Can Edit:**
- Add missing biography details
- Submit new photos/posters
- Add missing cast/crew

- Submit YouTube trailer links
- Add OTT platform links
- Submit awards

**Contribution Flow:**
1. User submits edit
2. Goes to `contributions` table (status: pending)
3. Admin reviews in dashboard

4. Admin approves → Updates `movies` or `people` table
5. Admin rejects → Marks as rejected with reason

**Prevents Bad Data:**
- All edits must be approved first
- Prevents spam/vandalism
- Maintains quality

---

### **Step 8: Admin Dashboard**

**Features:**
- View pending contributions

- Approve/reject edits
- Manually add missing data



- See import progress
- Monitor OTT fetch status
- Check for duplicate movies (auto-prevented by unique constraint)

***

## **🎯 WHERE TO HANDLE URL CONVERSION**

### **Option 1: Change TMDB Fetcher (❌ NOT RECOMMENDED)**
- Fetcher saves files with partial paths

- You would have to modify fetcher to add full URLs
- Problem: You already downloaded 5 movies with partial paths
- You'd have to re-download everything

### **Option 2: Convert URLs During Database Import (✅ BEST OPTION)**
- Keep fetcher script as-is (already done)
- JSON files have partial paths (already downloaded)

- **Import script** reads JSON and converts paths to full URLs
- Saves full URLs to database
- When displaying on website, use full URLs from database

***

## **✅ CORRECT APPROACH (What We'll Do):**

### **Flow:**

1. **TMDB Fetcher** (already done)
   - Downloads JSON with partial paths: `/u0XUBNQWlOvrh0Gd97ARGpIkL0.jpg`

2. **Import Script** (next step)

   - Reads JSON file
   - Adds base URL: `https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/original/u0XUBNQWlOvrh0Gd97ARGpIkL0
   - Saves to database

3. **Website Pages** (later)
   - Reads full URL from database
   - Displays image directly

***

## **📋 STEP 2: Create Movies Table in Database**

**Do this now in Drizzle Studio:**

1. Open Drizzle Studio

2. Go to SQL Console
3. Run this SQL:

```sql```
CREATE TABLE movies (
  id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
  tmdb_id INTEGER UNIQUE NOT NULL,

  imdb_id VARCHAR(20),
  title VARCHAR(500) NOT NULL,



  original_title VARCHAR(500),
  slug VARCHAR(500) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
  tagline VARCHAR(500),
  overview TEXT,

  release_date DATE,
  year INTEGER,
  runtime INTEGER,
  budget BIGINT,
  revenue BIGINT,
  vote_average DECIMAL(3,1),
  vote_count INTEGER,

  popularity DECIMAL(10,2),
  poster_url VARCHAR(500),
  backdrop_url VARCHAR(500),
  trailer_url VARCHAR(500),
  status VARCHAR(50),
  metadata JSONB NOT NULL,
  ott_urls JSONB,

  ott_fetched BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW()
);

CREATE INDEX idx_movies_tmdb_id ON movies(tmdb_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_movies_slug ON movies(slug);

CREATE INDEX idx_movies_year ON movies(year);

4. Click "Execute"

5. Check that movies table appears in your database

✅ CHECKPOINT:

Once you create the table, reply:

// lib/schema.ts -  v17 CLEAN (OLD TABLES REMOVED)

import { sql } from 'drizzle-orm';
import {
pgTable, serial, text, timestamp, boolean, integer, varchar, jsonb,
uuid, index, unique, primaryKey
} from 'drizzle-orm/pg-core';
import { relations } from 'drizzle-orm';
import type { AdapterAccountType } from 'next-auth/adapters';



// ============================================================================
// AUTH SYSTEM -  NEXTAUTH CORE TABLES (UUID)
// ============================================================================

export const users = pgTable('user', {
id: uuid('id' ).primaryKey().defaultRandom(),
name: text('name' ),
email: text('email' ).notNull().unique(),
emailVerified: timestamp('emailVerified', { mode: 'date' }),
image: text('image' ),
password: text('password' ),
createdAt: timestamp('createdAt', { mode: 'date' }).defaultNow(),
});

export const accounts = pgTable(
'account',
{

userId: uuid('userId' ).notNull().references(() => users.id, { onDelete: 'cascade' }),
type: text('type' ).$type<AdapterAccountType>().notNull(),
provider: text('provider' ).notNull(),
providerAccountId: text('providerAccountId' ).notNull(),
refresh_token: text('refresh_token' ),
access_token: text('access_token' ),
expires_at: integer('expires_at' ),
token_type: text('token_type' ),
scope: text('scope' ),
id_token: text('id_token' ),
session_state: text('session_state' ),
},
(account) => ({
compoundKey: primaryKey({
columns: [account.provider, account.providerAccountId],
}),
})
);

export const sessions = pgTable('session', {
sessionToken: text('sessionToken' ).primaryKey(),

userId: uuid('userId' ).notNull().references(() => users.id, { onDelete: 'cascade' }),
expires: timestamp('expires', { mode: 'date' }).notNull(),
});

export const verificationTokens = pgTable(
'verificationToken',
{
identifier: text('identifier' ).notNull(),
token: text('token' ).notNull(),



expires: timestamp('expires', { mode: 'date' }).notNull(),
},
(vt) => ({
compoundKey: primaryKey({ columns: [vt.identifier, vt.token] }),
})
);

export const passwordResetTokens = pgTable('password_reset_token', {
id: uuid('id' ).primaryKey().defaultRandom(),
email: text('email' ).notNull(),
token: text('token' ).notNull().unique(),
expires: timestamp('expires', { mode: 'date' }).notNull(),
createdAt: timestamp('createdAt', { mode: 'date' }).defaultNow(),
});

// ============================================================================
// PROFILE SYSTEM (UUID-BASED)
// ============================================================================

export const userProfiles = pgTable('user_profile', {
id: uuid('id' ).primaryKey().defaultRandom(),

userId: uuid('userId' ).notNull().references(() => users.id, { onDelete: 'cascade' }).unique(),
username: text('username' ).notNull().unique(),
bio: text('bio' ),
location: text('location' ),
website: text('website' ),
coverImage: text('coverImage' ),
totalReviews: integer('totalReviews' ).default(0),
totalWatchlist: integer('totalWatchlist' ).default(0),
totalFollowers: integer('totalFollowers' ).default(0),
statusEmoji: text('status_emoji' ),
themeColor: text('theme_color' ).default('#3b82f6'),
totalFollowing : integer('totalFollowing ' ).default(0),
badges: jsonb('badges' ).

type<string[]>().default([]),
favoriteHeroSlug : text('favorite_hero_slug ' ),
favoriteMovieSlug : text('favorite_movie_slug ' ),
showFollowers: boolean('showFollowers' ).default(true),
showFollowing : boolean('showFollowing ' ).default(true),
showWatchlist: boolean('showWatchlist' ).default(true),
showWatched: boolean('showWatched' ).default(true),
showReviews: boolean('showReviews' ).default(true),
showTierLists: boolean('showTierLists' ).default(true),
showMemes: boolean('showMemes' ).default(true),
isOnline: boolean('isOnline' ).default(false),



lastSeen: timestamp('lastSeen', { mode: 'date' }),
});

export const userFollows = pgTable('user_follows', {
id: uuid('id' ).primaryKey().defaultRandom(),

followerId: uuid('followerId' ).notNull().references(() => users.id, { onDelete: 'cascade' }),

followingId: uuid('followingId' ).notNull().references(() => users.id, { onDelete: 'cascade' }),
createdAt: timestamp('createdAt', { mode: 'date' }).defaultNow(),
});

export const profileViews = pgTable('profile_views', {
id: uuid('id' ).primaryKey().defaultRandom(),

viewerId: uuid('viewer_id' ).references(() => users.id),

profileId: uuid('profile_id' ).notNull().references(() => users.id, { onDelete: 'cascade' }),
viewedAt: timestamp('viewed_at' ).defaultNow(),
});

// ============================================================================
// PEOPLE TABLE -  ALL PEOPLE (HEROES, DIRECTORS, SINGERS, ETC.)
// ============================================================================

export const people = pgTable(
'people',
{
// Primary Key (string like 'prabhas', 'ss-rajamouli' )
id: varchar('id', { length: 100 }).primaryKey(),

// Basic Info
name: varchar('name', { length: 255 }).notNull(),
slug: varchar('slug', { length: 255 }).notNull().unique(),

// External IDs
tmdbPersonId: integer('tmdb_person_id'),
imdbId: varchar('imdb_id', { length: 50 }),

// Category System (from metadata)
category: varchar('category', { length: 100 }).notNull(), // 'hero', 'heroine', 'dir
subcategory: varchar('subcategory', { length: 100 }),     // 'superstar', 'diva', 'hi

// Full JSON Data
metadata: jsonb('metadata').notNull(), // Complete JSON file stored here

// Timestamps
createdAt: timestamp('created_at').default(sql`CURRENT_TIMESTAMP`).notNull(),
updatedAt: timestamp('updated_at').default(sql`CURRENT_TIMESTAMP`).notNull(),

},
(table) => ({
slugIdx: index('idx_people_slug ' ).on(table.slug),
categoryIdx: index('idx_people_category' ).on(table.category),



subcategoryIdx: index('idx_people_subcategory' ).on(table.subcategory),
tmdbIdx: index('idx_people_tmdb' ).on(table.tmdbPersonId),
catSubcatIdx: index('idx_people_cat_subcat' ).on(table.category, table.subcategory),
})
);

// ============================================================================
// PEOPLE FOLLOWS
// ============================================================================

export const peopleFollows = pgTable('people_follows', {
id: uuid('id' ).primaryKey().defaultRandom(),

userId: uuid('user_id' ).notNull().references(() => users.id, { onDelete: 'cascade' }),

personId: varchar('person_id', { length: 100 }).notNull().references(() => people.id, { onDelete:
'cascade' }),
createdAt: timestamp('created_at' ).notNull().defaultNow(),
}, (table) => ({
userPersonIdx: unique('user_person_follow_unique' ).on(table.userId, table.personId),
}));

});

export const usersRelations = relations(users, ({ one, many }) => ({

}));

export const peopleRelations = relations(people, ({ many }) => ({
followers: many(peopleFollows),
}));

export const peopleFollowsRelations = relations(peopleFollows, ({ one }) => ({
user: one(users, {
fields: [peopleFollows.userId],

references: [users.id],
}),
person: one(people, {
fields: [peopleFollows.personId],

references: [people.id],
}),
}));

// ============================================================================
// MOVIES TABLE - ALL TELUGU MOVIES FROM TMDB
// ============================================================================

export const movies = pgTable(
  'movies',
  {

    // Primary Key (auto-increment)
    id: serial('id').primaryKey(),

    // TMDB IDs (for uniqueness and external references)
    tmdbId: integer('tmdb_id').notNull().unique(),
    imdbId: varchar('imdb_id', { length: 20 }),

    // Basic Info
    title: varchar('title', { length: 500 }).notNull(),
    originalTitle: varchar('original_title', { length: 500 }),
    slug: varchar('slug', { length: 500 }).notNull().unique(),
    tagline: varchar('tagline', { length: 500 }),
    overview: text('overview'),

    // Release Info
    releaseDate: timestamp('release_date', { mode: 'date' }),
    year: integer('year'),
    runtime: integer('runtime'), // in minutes
    status: varchar('status', { length: 50 }), // 'Released', 'Post Production', etc.

    // Financial Data

    budget: integer('budget'),
    revenue: integer('revenue'),

    // Ratings
    voteAverage: integer('vote_average'), // TMDB rating (0-100)
    voteCount: integer('vote_count'),
    popularity: integer('popularity'),

    // Media URLs (full URLs stored here)
    posterUrl: varchar('poster_url', { length: 500 }),



    backdropUrl: varchar('backdrop_url', { length: 500 }),
    trailerUrl: varchar('trailer_url', { length: 500 }),

    // Full JSON Data (backup/reference)

    metadata: jsonb('metadata').notNull(),

    // OTT Platform Data (from JustWatch API)
    ottUrls: jsonb('ott_urls'),
    ottFetched: boolean('ott_fetched').default(false),

    // Timestamps

    createdAt: timestamp('created_at').default(sql`CURRENT_TIMESTAMP`).notNull(),
    updatedAt: timestamp('updated_at').default(sql`CURRENT_TIMESTAMP`).notNull(),
  },
  (table) => ({
    tmdbIdIdx: index('idx_movies_tmdb_id').on(table.tmdbId),
    slugIdx: index('idx_movies_slug').on(table.slug),
    yearIdx: index('idx_movies_year').on(table.year),

    releaseIdx: index('idx_movies_release_date').on(table.releaseDate),
  })
);

// ============================================================================
// MOVIE CREDITS - LINKS MOVIES ↔ PEOPLE (CAST & CREW)

// ============================================================================

export const movieCredits = pgTable(
  'movie_credits',
  {
    // Primary Key
    id: serial('id').primaryKey(),

    // Foreign Keys
    movieId: integer('movie_id').notNull().references(() => movies.id, { onDelete: 
    personId: varchar('person_id', { length: 100 }).notNull().references(() => peopl

    // TMDB Person ID (for matching when person doesn't exist yet)
    tmdbPersonId: integer('tmdb_person_id').notNull(),

    // Role Type
    roleType: varchar('role_type', { length: 10 }).notNull(), // 'cast' or 'crew'

    // Cast-specific fields
    character: varchar('character', { length: 500 }), // Character name (for cast)
    orderIndex: integer('order_index'), // Display order (for cast)

    // Crew-specific fields
    job: varchar('job', { length: 100 }), // 'Director', 'Producer', etc.
    department: varchar('department', { length: 100 }), // 'Directing', 'Writing', e

    // Timestamp
    createdAt: timestamp('created_at').default(sql`CURRENT_TIMESTAMP`).notNull(),
  },

  (table) => ({
    movieIdx: index('idx_credits_movie').on(table.movieId),



    personIdx: index('idx_credits_person').on(table.personId),
    tmdbPersonIdx: index('idx_credits_tmdb_person').on(table.tmdbPersonId),
    roleIdx: index('idx_credits_role').on(table.roleType),
  })

);

// ============================================================================
// RELATIONS FOR MOVIES
// ============================================================================

export const moviesRelations = relations(movies, ({ many }) => ({
  credits: many(movieCredits),
}));

export const movieCreditsRelations = relations(movieCredits, ({ one }) => ({
  movie: one(movies, {
    fields: [movieCredits.movieId],

    references: [movies.id],
  }),
  person: one(people, {
    fields: [movieCredits.personId],
    references: [people.id],
  }),
}));

// ============================================================================
// TYPE EXPORTS FOR MOVIES
// ============================================================================

export type Movie = typeof movies.$inferSelect;

export type NewMovie = typeof movies.$inferInsert;
export type MovieCredit = typeof movieCredits.$inferSelect;
export type NewMovieCredit = typeof movieCredits.$inferInsert;

## **📝 STEP 3: Create Import Script**

Create a new file: `scripts/import-movies.ts`

import { db } from '@/lib/db';
import { movies, movieCredits, people } from '@/lib/schema';
import { eq } from 'drizzle-orm';
import fs from 'fs';
import path from 'path';

// TMDB Image Base URLs

const TMDB_IMAGE_BASE = 'https://image.tmdb.org/t/p/original';

const YOUTUBE_BASE = 'https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=';

// Folder containing your downloaded JSON files
const MOVIES_FOLDER = './test-movies'; // Change this to your folder path

interface TMDBMovie {
id: number;
imdb_id?: string ;
title: string ;
original_title?: string ;
tagline?: string ;



overview?: string ;
release_date?: string ;
runtime?: number;
budget?: number;
revenue?: number;
vote_average?: number;
vote_count?: number;
popularity?: number;
poster_path?: string ;
backdrop_path?: string ;
status?: string ;
videos?: {
results: Array<{
key: string ;
site: string ;
type: string ;
official?: boolean;
}>;
};
credits?: {
cast: Array<{
id: number;
name: string ;
character?: string ;
order?: number;
profile_path?: string ;
}>;
crew: Array<{
id: number;
name: string ;
job?: string ;
department?: string ;
}>;
};
}

function generateSlug(title: string, id: number): string {
return ${title}-${id}
.toLowerCase()
.replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, '-')
.replace(/^-+|-+$/g, ' ' );
}

function getFullImageUrl(path?: string): string |  null {
return path ? ${TMDB_IMAGE_BASE}${path} : null;
}



function getTrailerUrl(videos?: TMDBMovie['videos']): string |  null {
if (!videos?.results) return null;

// Find official trailer
const trailer = videos.results.find(
v => v.site === 'YouTube' && v.type === 'Trailer' && v.official
) ||  videos.results.find(
v => v.site === 'YouTube' && v.type === 'Trailer'
);

return trailer ? ${YOUTUBE_BASE}${trailer.key} : null;
}

async function importMovie(movieData : TMDBMovie) {
console.log(\n🎬 Processing: ${movieData.title} (${movieData.id}));

// Check if already exists
const existing = await db
.select()
.from(movies)

.where(eq(movies.tmdbId, movieData.id))

.limit(1);

if (existing.length > 0) {
console.log( ⏭️Already exists, skipping...);
return existing ;
}

// Generate slug

const slug = generateSlug(movieData.title, movieData.id);

// Extract year from release_date
const year = movieData.release_date
? parseInt(movieData.release_date.split('-'))
: null;

// Convert URLs
const posterUrl = getFullImageUrl(movieData.poster_path);
const backdropUrl = getFullImageUrl(movieData.backdrop_path);
const trailerUrl = getTrailerUrl(movieData.videos);

// Insert movie
const [movie] = await db.insert(movies).values({

tmdbId: movieData.id,
imdbId: movieData.imdb_id,
title: movieData.title,
originalTitle: movieData.original_title,
slug,
tagline: movieData.tagline,



overview: movieData.overview,
releaseDate: movieData.release_date ? new Date(movieData.release_date) : null,
year,
runtime: movieData.runtime,
budget: movieData.budget,
revenue: movieData.revenue,
voteAverage: movieData.vote_average,
voteCount: movieData.vote_count,
popularity: movieData.popularity,
posterUrl,
backdropUrl,
trailerUrl,
status: movieData.status,
metadata : movieData as any,
ottFetched: false,
}).returning();

console.log( ✅ Movie imported (ID: ${movie.id}));
console.log( 📸 Poster: ${posterUrl ? '✓' : '✗'});
console.log( 🎞️Backdrop: ${backdropUrl ? '✓' : '✗'});
console.log( 🎥 Trailer: ${trailerUrl ? '✓' : '✗'});

// Import cast
if (movieData.credits?.cast) {
let castCount = 0;
for (const castMember of movieData.credits.cast.slice(0, 20)) { // Top 20 cast
try {
// Check if person exists
const existingPerson = await db
.select()
.from(people)

.where(eq(people.tmdbPersonId, castMember.id))

.limit(1);

    let personId: string;

    if (existingPerson.length === 0) {
      // Create stub person

      const personSlug = castMember.name.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-');
      personId = personSlug;

      await db.insert(people).values({
        id: personId,
        name: castMember.name,
        slug: personSlug,

        tmdbPersonId: castMember.id,
        category: 'actor',
        metadata: {
          name: castMember.name,



          tmdb_person_id: castMember.id,
          profile_path: castMember.profile_path,
        },
      }).onConflictDoNothing();

    } else {
      personId = existingPerson.id;
    }

    // Insert credit
    await db.insert(movieCredits).values({
      movieId: movie.id,

      personId,
      tmdbPersonId: castMember.id,
      roleType: 'cast',
      character: castMember.character,
      orderIndex: castMember.order,
    });

    castCount++;
  } catch (err) {
    console.log(`   ⚠️  Cast error: ${castMember.name}`);
  }
}
console.log(`   👥 Cast imported: ${castCount}`);

}

// Import crew
if (movieData.credits?.crew) {
const directors = movieData.credits.crew.filter(c => c.job === 'Director' );
let crewCount = 0;

for (const crewMember of directors) {
  try {

    const existingPerson = await db
      .select()
      .from(people)
      .where(eq(people.tmdbPersonId, crewMember.id))
      .limit(1);

    let personId: string;

    if (existingPerson.length === 0) {
      const personSlug = crewMember.name.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-');
      personId = personSlug;

      await db.insert(people).values({
        id: personId,

        name: crewMember.name,
        slug: personSlug,
        tmdbPersonId: crewMember.id,
        category: 'director',
        metadata: {
          name: crewMember.name,



          tmdb_person_id: crewMember.id,
        },
      }).onConflictDoNothing();
    } else {

      personId = existingPerson.id;
    }

    await db.insert(movieCredits).values({
      movieId: movie.id,
      personId,
      tmdbPersonId: crewMember.id,

      roleType: 'crew',
      job: crewMember.job,
      department: crewMember.department,
    });

    crewCount++;
  } catch (err) {

    console.log(`   ⚠️  Crew error: ${crewMember.name}`);
  }
}
console.log(`   🎬 Crew imported: ${crewCount}`);

}

return movie ;
}

async function main() {
console.log('🚀 Starting movie import...\n' );
console.log(📁 Reading from: ${MOVIES_FOLDER}\n);

// Read all JSON files
const files = fs.readdirSync(MOVIES_FOLDER).filter(f => f.endsWith('.json' ));

console.log(📊 Found ${files.length} movies to import\n);

let successCount = 0;
let skipCount = 0;
let errorCount = 0;

for (const file of files) {
try {
const filePath = path.join(MOVIES_FOLDER, file);
const data = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf8'));

  const result = await importMovie(data);

  if (result) {
    successCount++;

  } else {
    skipCount++;
  }



} catch (err: any) {
  console.log(`❌ Error importing ${file}: ${err.message}`);
  errorCount++;
}

}

console.log('\n' + '='.repeat(50));
console.log('📊 IMPORT SUMMARY ' );
console.log('='.repeat(50));
console.log(✅ Successfully imported: ${successCount});
console.log(⏭️Skipped (duplicates): ${skipCount});
console.log(❌ Errors: ${errorCount});
console.log('='.repeat(50));
}

main()
.then(() => {
console.log('\n✨ Import complete!');
process.exit(0);
})
.catch((err) => {
console.error('💥 Fatal error:', err);
process.exit(1);
});

The issue is that the dotenv import is loading .env.local, but the lib/db.ts file is trying to
access process.env.DATABASE_URL before dotenv loads it, because the import happens at
module load time.

Fix: Use direct DATABASE_URL instead

Update your scripts/import-movies.ts first 10 lines to this:

// Load environment variables FIRST before any other imports
import { config } from 'dotenv';
config({ path: '.env.local' });

// Set DATABASE_URL explicitly if needed
process.env.DATABASE_URL = process.env.DATABASE_URL || 'postgresql://tfiverse:newpas

import { db } from '@/lib/db';
import { movies, movieCredits, people } from '@/lib/schema';
import { eq } from 'drizzle-orm';
import fs from 'fs';

import path from 'path';
```

This ensures `DATABASE_URL` is set **before** importing `lib/db.ts`.

**Try running it now:**

``````bash
npx tsx scripts/import-movies.ts
```

It should work! 🚀

Perfect! I found the issue. Looking at the JSON data:

**The problem:** The schema expects `voteAverage` and `popularity` as **integers**, 
- `"vote_average": 7` (integer in this case, but can be 7.5)
- `"popularity": 1.2055` (decimal)

import 'dotenv/config '; // ← ADD THIS FIRST LINE!
import * as fs from 'fs';

import postgres from 'postgres';

// Database connection
const connectionString = process.env.DATABASE_URL!;
const client = postgres(connectionString);
const db = drizzle(client);

// Base path to JSON files
const DATA_PATH = path.join(process.cwd(), 'public', 'data' );

// All categories with their folder structure
const CATEGORIES = [
{ folder: 'art-directors', mainCategory: 'art-director' },
{ folder: 'character-artists', mainCategory: 'character-artist' },
{ folder: 'choreographers', mainCategory: 'choreographer' },
{ folder: 'cinematographers', mainCategory: 'cinematographer' },
{ folder: 'comedians', mainCategory: 'comedian' },
{ folder: 'costume-designers', mainCategory: 'costume-designer' },
{ folder: 'directors', mainCategory: 'director' },
{ folder: 'editors', mainCategory: 'editor' },
{ folder: 'heroes', mainCategory: 'hero' },
{ folder: 'heroines', mainCategory: 'heroine' },
{ folder: 'line-producers', mainCategory: 'line-producer' },
{ folder: 'lyricists', mainCategory: 'lyricist' },
{ folder: 'music-directors', mainCategory: 'music-director' },
{ folder: 'producers', mainCategory: 'producer' },
{ folder: 'pros', mainCategory: 'pro' },
{ folder: 'singers', mainCategory: 'singer' },
{ folder: 'stunt-directors', mainCategory: 'stunt-director' },
{ folder: 'vfx-supervisors', mainCategory: 'vfx-supervisor' },
{ folder: 'villains', mainCategory: 'villain' },
];

// Statistics
let totalInserted = 0;
let totalErrors = 0;

async function processFolder(folderPath: string, mainCategory: string, subcategory: string |
null) {
try {
const files = fs.readdirSync(folderPath).filter(file => file.endsWith('.json' ));

if (files.length === 0) return;

const subfolder = subcategory ? `${subcategory}/` : '';

console.log(`   📄 ${subfolder}${files.length} files`);



for (const file of files) {
  try {

    const filePath = path.join(folderPath, file);
    const fileContent = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8');
    const data = JSON.parse(fileContent);

    const id = data.id;
    const name = data.name;

    const slug = data.slug;
    const tmdbPersonId = data.tmdbPersonId || null;
    const imdbId = data.imdbId || null;
    const category = data.metadata?.category || mainCategory;
    const subcategoryValue = data.metadata?.subCategory || subcategory || null;

    if (!id || !name || !slug || !data.metadata) {
      console.error(`      ❌ Missing required fields in ${file}`);
      totalErrors++;
      continue;
    }

    await db.insert(people).values({
      id,
      name,
      slug,
      tmdbPersonId,
      imdbId,
      category,

      subcategory: subcategoryValue,
      metadata: data,
    }).onConflictDoUpdate({
      target: people.id,
      set: {
        name,
        slug,
        tmdbPersonId,

        imdbId,
        category,
        subcategory: subcategoryValue,
        metadata: data,
        updatedAt: new Date(),
      },
    });

    totalInserted++;
    console.log(`      ✅ ${name} (${id})`);

  } catch (error: any) {

    totalErrors++;
    console.error(`      ❌ Error in ${file}:`, error.message);



  }
}

} catch (error: any) {
console.error( ❌ Error reading folder:, error.message);
}
}

async function importPeople() {
console.log('🚀 Starting people import...\n' );
console.log(📂 Base path: ${DATA_PATH}\n);

for (const category of CATEGORIES) {
const categoryPath = path.join(DATA_PATH, category.folder);

if (!fs.existsSync(categoryPath)) {
  console.log(`⚠️  Category folder not found: ${category.folder}`);
  continue;

}

console.log(`📁 Processing ${category.folder}...`);

try {

  const items = fs.readdirSync(categoryPath, { withFileTypes: true });
  const subfolders = items.filter(d => d.isDirectory()).map(d => d.name);
  const jsonFiles = items.filter(d => d.isFile() && d.name.endsWith('.json'));

  // Process JSON files in category root
  if (jsonFiles.length > 0) {

    await processFolder(categoryPath, category.mainCategory, null);
  }

  // Process subfolders
  for (const subfolder of subfolders) {
    const subfolderPath = path.join(categoryPath, subfolder);

    await processFolder(subfolderPath, category.mainCategory, subfolder);
  }
} catch (error: any) {
  console.error(`   ❌ Error:`, error.message);
}

console.log('');

}

console.log('═══════════════════════════════════════' );
console.log('✅ Import complete!');



console.log( Inserted: ${totalInserted});
console.log( Errors: ${totalErrors});
console.log('═══════════════════════════════════════\n' );

await client.end();
process.exit(0);
}

// ✅ WRAPPED -  No top-level await
importPeople().catch((error) => {
console.error('💥 Fatal error:', error);
process.exit(1);
});

Perfect! I understand now. You want both scripts to work together in this flow:

1. Movie import creates stub people (like now: 28 → 107)

2. People import updates those stubs with full data from your JSON files

3. Future runs should update existing records (not create duplicates)

Here's the UPDATED scripts/import-people.ts with smart upsert logic:

// scripts/import-people.ts - SMART UPSERT VERSION

import 'dotenv/config';
import * as fs from 'fs';

import * as path from 'path';
import { drizzle } from 'drizzle-orm/postgres-js';
import postgres from 'postgres';
import { people } from '../lib/schema';
import { eq, or, sql } from 'drizzle-orm';

// Database connection

const connectionString = process.env.DATABASE_URL!;
const client = postgres(connectionString);
const db = drizzle(client);

// Base path to JSON files
const DATA_PATH = path.join(process.cwd(), 'public', 'data');

// All categories with their folder structure
const CATEGORIES = [
  { folder: 'art-directors', mainCategory: 'art-director' },
  { folder: 'character-artists', mainCategory: 'character-artist' },
  { folder: 'choreographers', mainCategory: 'choreographer' },
  { folder: 'cinematographers', mainCategory: 'cinematographer' },
  { folder: 'comedians', mainCategory: 'comedian' },

  { folder: 'costume-designers', mainCategory: 'costume-designer' },
  { folder: 'directors', mainCategory: 'director' },
  { folder: 'editors', mainCategory: 'editor' },
  { folder: 'heroes', mainCategory: 'hero' },
  { folder: 'heroines', mainCategory: 'heroine' },
  { folder: 'line-producers', mainCategory: 'line-producer' },



  { folder: 'lyricists', mainCategory: 'lyricist' },
  { folder: 'music-directors', mainCategory: 'music-director' },
  { folder: 'producers', mainCategory: 'producer' },
  { folder: 'pros', mainCategory: 'pro' },

  { folder: 'singers', mainCategory: 'singer' },
  { folder: 'stunt-directors', mainCategory: 'stunt-director' },
  { folder: 'vfx-supervisors', mainCategory: 'vfx-supervisor' },
  { folder: 'villains', mainCategory: 'villain' },
];

// Statistics

let totalInserted = 0;
let totalUpdated = 0;
let totalErrors = 0;

async function processFolder(folderPath: string, mainCategory: string, subcategory: 
  try {
    const files = fs.readdirSync(folderPath).filter(file => file.endsWith('.json'));

    if (files.length === 0) return;

    const subfolder = subcategory ? `${subcategory}/` : '';
    console.log(`   📄 ${subfolder}${files.length} files`);

    for (const file of files) {

      try {
        const filePath = path.join(folderPath, file);
        const fileContent = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8');
        const data = JSON.parse(fileContent);

        const id = data.id;
        const name = data.name;

        const slug = data.slug;
        const tmdbPersonId = data.tmdbPersonId || data.metadata?.tmdb_person_id || 
        const imdbId = data.imdbId || data.metadata?.imdb_id || null;
        const category = data.metadata?.category || mainCategory;
        const subcategoryValue = data.metadata?.subCategory || subcategory || null;

        if (!id || !name || !slug || !data.metadata) {
          console.error(`      ❌ Missing required fields in ${file}`);

          totalErrors++;
          continue;
        }

        // 🔍 SMART CHECK: Look for existing person by tmdb_person_id OR name
        const existing = await db
          .select()

          .from(people)
          .where(
            or(
              eq(people.id, id),
              tmdbPersonId ? eq(people.tmdbPersonId, tmdbPersonId) : undefined,
              sql`LOWER(${people.name}) = LOWER(${name})`
            )

          )
          .limit(1);



        if (existing.length > 0) {
          // UPDATE existing record with full data
          await db

            .update(people)
            .set({
              name,
              slug,
              tmdbPersonId,
              imdbId,
              category,

              subcategory: subcategoryValue,
              metadata: data,
              updatedAt: new Date(),
            })
            .where(eq(people.id, existing.id));

          totalUpdated++;

          console.log(`      🔄 Updated: ${name} (was: ${existing[0].id})`);
        } else {
          // INSERT new record
          await db.insert(people).values({
            id,
            name,
            slug,

            tmdbPersonId,
            imdbId,
            category,
            subcategory: subcategoryValue,
            metadata: data,
          });

          totalInserted++;
          console.log(`      ✅ Inserted: ${name} (${id})`);
        }

      } catch (error: any) {
        totalErrors++;
        console.error(`      ❌ Error in ${file}:`, error.message);
      }

    }
  } catch (error: any) {
    console.error(`   ❌ Error reading folder:`, error.message);
  }
}

async function importPeople() {

  console.log('🚀 Starting people import...\n');
  console.log(`📂 Base path: ${DATA_PATH}\n`);

  for (const category of CATEGORIES) {
    const categoryPath = path.join(DATA_PATH, category.folder);

    if (!fs.existsSync(categoryPath)) {

      console.log(`⚠️  Category folder not found: ${category.folder}`);
      continue;



    }

    console.log(`📁 Processing ${category.folder}...`);

    try {
      const items = fs.readdirSync(categoryPath, { withFileTypes: true });
      const subfolders = items.filter(d => d.isDirectory()).map(d => d.name);
      const jsonFiles = items.filter(d => d.isFile() && d.name.endsWith('.json'));

      // Process JSON files in category root
      if (jsonFiles.length > 0) {

        await processFolder(categoryPath, category.mainCategory, null);
      }

      // Process subfolders
      for (const subfolder of subfolders) {
        const subfolderPath = path.join(categoryPath, subfolder);
        await processFolder(subfolderPath, category.mainCategory, subfolder);

      }
    } catch (error: any) {
      console.error(`   ❌ Error:`, error.message);
    }

    console.log('');
  }

  console.log('═══════════════════════════════════════');
  console.log('✅ Import complete!');
  console.log(`   ✨ New records: ${totalInserted}`);
  console.log(`   🔄 Updated: ${totalUpdated}`);
  console.log(`   ❌ Errors: ${totalErrors}`);
  console.log('═══════════════════════════════════════\n');

  await client.end();
  process.exit(0);
}

// Run import
importPeople().catch((error) => {
  console.error('💥 Fatal error:', error);

  process.exit(1);
});
```

## **🔧 KEY CHANGES:**

1. **Smart Lookup** - Checks for existing people by:
   - `id` (primary key)
   - `tmdb_person_id` (from movie credits)
   - `name` (case-insensitive match)

2. **UPDATE instead of INSERT** - If found, updates the stub with full data

3. **Stats Tracking** - Shows how many were new vs updated

// UPDATED processFolder function -  HANDLES ID CONFLICTS

async function processFolder(folderPath: string, mainCategory: string, subcategory: string |
null) {
try {
const files = fs.readdirSync(folderPath).filter(file => file.endsWith('.json' ));

if (files.length === 0) return;

const subfolder = subcategory ? `${subcategory}/` : '';
console.log(`   📄 ${subfolder}${files.length} files`);

for (const file of files) {

  try {
    const filePath = path.join(folderPath, file);
    const fileContent = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8');
    const data = JSON.parse(fileContent);

    const id = data.id;
    const name = data.name;

    const slug = data.slug;
    const tmdbPersonId = data.tmdbPersonId || data.metadata?.tmdb_person_id || null
    const imdbId = data.imdbId || data.metadata?.imdb_id || null;
    const category = data.metadata?.category || mainCategory;
    const subcategoryValue = data.metadata?.subCategory || subcategory || null;

    if (!id || !name || !slug || !data.metadata) {

      console.error(`      ❌ Missing required fields in ${file}`);
      totalErrors++;
      continue;
    }

    // 🔍 SMART CHECK: Look for existing person by tmdb_person_id OR name (NOT by id



    const existing = await db
      .select()
      .from(people)
      .where(

        or(
          tmdbPersonId ? eq(people.tmdbPersonId, tmdbPersonId) : undefined,
          sql`LOWER(${people.name}) = LOWER(${name})`
        )
      )
      .limit(1);

    if (existing.length > 0) {
      const existingId = existing.id;

      // 🔄 UPDATE existing record
      await db
        .update(people)
        .set({

          id,  // ← Update ID if needed
          name,
          slug,
          tmdbPersonId,
          imdbId,
          category,
          subcategory: subcategoryValue,

          metadata: data,
          updatedAt: new Date(),
        })
        .where(eq(people.id, existingId));

      // 🔗 UPDATE movie_credits if ID changed
      if (existingId !== id) {

        await db
          .update(movieCredits)
          .set({ personId: id })
          .where(eq(movieCredits.personId, existingId));

        console.log(`      🔄 Updated & ID changed: ${name} (${existingId} → ${id})`);
      } else {
        console.log(`      🔄 Updated: ${name} (${id})`);

      }

      totalUpdated++;
    } else {
      // ✨ INSERT new record
      await db.insert(people).values({
        id,

        name,
        slug,
        tmdbPersonId,
        imdbId,
        category,
        subcategory: subcategoryValue,
        metadata: data,

      });



      totalInserted++;
      console.log(`      ✅ Inserted: ${name} (${id})`);
    }

  } catch (error: any) {
    totalErrors++;
    console.error(`      ❌ Error in ${file}:`, error.message);
  }
}

} catch (error: any) {
console.error( ❌ Error reading folder:, error.message);
}
}

async function processFolder(folderPath: string, mainCategory: string, subcategory: string |
null) {
try {
const files = fs.readdirSync(folderPath).filter(file => file.endsWith('.json' ));
if (files.length === 0) return;

const subfolder = subcategory ? `${subcategory}/` : '';
console.log(`   📄 ${subfolder}${files.length} files`);

for (const file of files) {

  try {
    const filePath = path.join(folderPath, file);
    const fileContent = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8');
    const data = JSON.parse(fileContent);

    const id = data.id;
    const name = data.name;

    const slug = data.slug;
    const tmdbPersonId = data.tmdbPersonId || data.metadata?.tmdb_person_id || null
    const imdbId = data.imdbId || data.metadata?.imdb_id || null;
    const category = data.metadata?.category || mainCategory;
    const subcategoryValue = data.metadata?.subCategory || subcategory || null;

    if (!id || !name || !slug || !data.metadata) {

      console.error(`      ❌ Missing required fields in ${file}`);
      totalErrors++;
      continue;
    }

    // Find existing by tmdb_person_id or name
    const existing = await db

      .select()
      .from(people)



      .where(
        or(
          tmdbPersonId ? eq(people.tmdbPersonId, tmdbPersonId) : undefined,
          sql`LOWER(${people.name}) = LOWER(${name})`

        )
      )
      .limit(1);

    if (existing.length > 0) {
      const existingId = existing.id;

      if (existingId !== id) {
        // ID mismatch - need to relink
        await db.update(movieCredits).set({ personId: id }).where(eq(movieCredits.p
        await db.delete(people).where(eq(people.id, existingId));
        await db.insert(people).values({
          id, name, slug, tmdbPersonId, imdbId, category,
          subcategory: subcategoryValue, metadata: data,

        });
        console.log(`      🔄 ID changed: ${name} (${existingId} → ${id})`);
      } else {
        await db.update(people).set({
          name, slug, tmdbPersonId, imdbId, category,
          subcategory: subcategoryValue, metadata: data, updatedAt: new Date(),
        }).where(eq(people.id, existingId));

        console.log(`      🔄 Updated: ${name}`);
      }
      totalUpdated++;
    } else {
      await db.insert(people).values({
        id, name, slug, tmdbPersonId, imdbId, category,
        subcategory: subcategoryValue, metadata: data,

      });
      console.log(`      ✅ Inserted: ${name}`);
      totalInserted++;
    }

  } catch (error: any) {
    totalErrors++;
    console.error(`      ❌ Error in ${file}:`, error.message);

  }
}

async function importPeople() {
console.log('🚀 Starting people import...\n' );

for (const category of CATEGORIES) {
const categoryPath = path.join(DATA_PATH, category.folder);
if (!fs.existsSync(categoryPath)) continue ;



console.log(`📁 ${category.folder}...`);
const items = fs.readdirSync(categoryPath, { withFileTypes: true });
const subfolders = items.filter(d => d.isDirectory()).map(d => d.name);
const jsonFiles = items.filter(d => d.isFile() && d.name.endsWith('.json'));

if (jsonFiles.length > 0) await processFolder(categoryPath, category.mainCategory, n
for (const sub of subfolders) await processFolder(path.join(categoryPath, sub), cate
console.log('');

}

console.log(✨ New: ${totalInserted} | 🔄 Updated: ${totalUpdated} | ❌ Errors:
${totalErrors});
console.log('═══════════════════════════════════════\n' );

await client.end();

[key: string]: any;

  console.log(`   ⏭️ Already exists, skipping...`);

  return;

  trailerUrl,
  metadata: movieData,
}).returning();

// Import cast (top 20)

          slug: personSlug,

          tmdbPersonId: crewMember.id,
          category: 'director',
          metadata: {
            name: crewMember.name,
            tmdb_person_id: crewMember.id,
            profile_path: crewMember.profile_path,
          },

        }).onConflictDoNothing();
      }

      await db.insert(movieCredits).values({
        movieId: movie.id,
        personId,
        tmdbPersonId: crewMember.id,

        roleType: 'crew',
        job: crewMember.job,



        department: crewMember.department,
      }).onConflictDoNothing();

      crewCount++;

    } catch (err: any) {
      console.log(`   ⚠️  Crew error: ${crewMember.name}`);
    }
  }
  console.log(`   🎬 Crew imported: ${crewCount}`);
}

successCount++;

} catch (error: any) {
console.log( ❌ Error importing ${fileName}: ${error.message});
errorCount++;
}
}

async function main() {
console.log('✅ Database client initialized' );
console.log('🚀 Starting movie import...\n' );
console.log(📁 Reading from: ${MOVIES_FOLDER}\n);

const files = fs.readdirSync(MOVIES_FOLDER).filter(f => f.endsWith('.json' ));
console.log(📊 Found ${files.length} movies to import\n);

for (const file of files) {
const filePath = path.join(MOVIES_FOLDER, file);
await importMovie(filePath, file);
}

console.log('\n==================================================');
console.log('📊 IMPORT SUMMARY ' );
console.log(' ');
console.log(✅ Successfully imported: ${successCount});
console.log(⏭️Skipped (duplicates): ${skipCount});
console.log(❌ Errors: ${errorCount});
console.log('\n' );
console.log('✨ Import complete!');

process.exit(0);
}

main().catch((error) => {
console.error('💥 Fatal error:', error);
process.exit(1);
});

# **📁 SCRIPT 2: `scripts/import-people.ts`**

``````typescript
// scripts/import-people.ts
// Imports/updates people from JSON files with smart ID matching

import 'dotenv/config';
import * as fs from 'fs';

import * as path from 'path';
import { drizzle } from 'drizzle-orm/postgres-js';
import postgres from 'postgres';
import { people, movieCredits } from '../lib/schema';
import { eq, or, sql } from 'drizzle-orm';

// Database connection

const connectionString = process.env.DATABASE_URL!;
const client = postgres(connectionString);
const db = drizzle(client);

// Base path to JSON files
const DATA_PATH = path.join(process.cwd(), 'public', 'data');

// All categories
const CATEGORIES = [
  { folder: 'art-directors', mainCategory: 'art-director' },
  { folder: 'character-artists', mainCategory: 'character-artist' },
  { folder: 'choreographers', mainCategory: 'choreographer' },
  { folder: 'cinematographers', mainCategory: 'cinematographer' },
  { folder: 'comedians', mainCategory: 'comedian' },

  { folder: 'costume-designers', mainCategory: 'costume-designer' },
  { folder: 'directors', mainCategory: 'director' },
  { folder: 'editors', mainCategory: 'editor' },
  { folder: 'heroes', mainCategory: 'hero' },
  { folder: 'heroines', mainCategory: 'heroine' },
  { folder: 'line-producers', mainCategory: 'line-producer' },
  { folder: 'lyricists', mainCategory: 'lyricist' },
  { folder: 'music-directors', mainCategory: 'music-director' },

  { folder: 'producers', mainCategory: 'producer' },
  { folder: 'pros', mainCategory: 'pro' },
  { folder: 'singers', mainCategory: 'singer' },
  { folder: 'stunt-directors', mainCategory: 'stunt-director' },
  { folder: 'vfx-supervisors', mainCategory: 'vfx-supervisor' },
  { folder: 'villains', mainCategory: 'villain' },
];

let totalInserted = 0;
let totalUpdated = 0;
let totalErrors = 0;

async function processFolder(folderPath: string, mainCategory: string, subcategory: 
  try {

    const files = fs.readdirSync(folderPath).filter(file => file.endsWith('.json'));
    if (files.length === 0) return;



    const subfolder = subcategory ? `${subcategory}/` : '';
    console.log(`   📄 ${subfolder}${files.length} files`);

    for (const file of files) {
      try {
        const filePath = path.join(folderPath, file);
        const fileContent = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8');
        const data = JSON.parse(fileContent);

        const jsonId = data.id;

        const name = data.name;
        const slug = data.slug;
        const tmdbPersonId = data.tmdbPersonId || data.metadata?.tmdb_person_id || 
        const imdbId = data.imdbId || data.metadata?.imdb_id || null;
        const category = data.metadata?.category || mainCategory;
        const subcategoryValue = data.metadata?.subCategory || subcategory || null;

        if (!jsonId || !name || !slug || !data.metadata) {
          console.error(`      ❌ Missing fields in ${file}`);
          totalErrors++;
          continue;
        }

        // 🔍 SMART LOOKUP: Find existing by tmdb_person_id OR name (NOT by JSON id)

        const existing = await db
          .select()
          .from(people)
          .where(
            or(
              tmdbPersonId ? eq(people.tmdbPersonId, tmdbPersonId) : undefined,
              sql`LOWER(${people.name}) = LOWER(${name})`

            )
          )
          .limit(1);

        if (existing.length > 0) {
          const dbId = existing[0].id;

          if (dbId !== jsonId) {

            // 🔄 ID MISMATCH - Need to relink everything
            console.log(`      🔄 ID mismatch: DB="${dbId}", JSON="${jsonId}"`);

            // 1. Update movie_credits to use correct ID from JSON
            const updateResult = await db
              .update(movieCredits)
              .set({ personId: jsonId })

              .where(eq(movieCredits.personId, dbId));

            // 2. Delete old stub record
            await db.delete(people).where(eq(people.id, dbId));

            // 3. Insert with correct ID from JSON
            await db.insert(people).values({

              id: jsonId,
              name,



              slug,
              tmdbPersonId,
              imdbId,
              category,

              subcategory: subcategoryValue,
              metadata: data,
            });

            console.log(`      ✅ Updated: ${name} (${dbId} → ${jsonId})`);
            totalUpdated++;
          } else {

            // ✅ IDs match - just update data
            await db
              .update(people)
              .set({
                name,
                slug,
                tmdbPersonId,

                imdbId,
                category,
                subcategory: subcategoryValue,
                metadata: data,
                updatedAt: new Date(),
              })
              .where(eq(people.id, dbId));

            console.log(`      ✅ Updated: ${name}`);
            totalUpdated++;
          }
        } else {
          // ✨ NEW PERSON - Insert
          await db.insert(people).values({

            id: jsonId,
            name,
            slug,
            tmdbPersonId,
            imdbId,
            category,
            subcategory: subcategoryValue,
            metadata: data,

          });

          console.log(`      ✅ Inserted: ${name}`);
          totalInserted++;
        }

      } catch (error: any) {

        totalErrors++;
        console.error(`      ❌ Error in ${file}:`, error.message);
      }
    }
  } catch (error: any) {
    console.error(`   ❌ Error reading folder:`, error.message);
  }

}



async function importPeople() {
  console.log('🚀 Starting people import...\n');
  console.log(`📂 Base path: ${DATA_PATH}\n`);

  for (const category of CATEGORIES) {
    const categoryPath = path.join(DATA_PATH, category.folder);

    if (!fs.existsSync(categoryPath)) {
      console.log(`⚠️  Folder not found: ${category.folder}`);
      continue;
    }

    console.log(`📁 Processing ${category.folder}...`);

    try {
      const items = fs.readdirSync(categoryPath, { withFileTypes: true });
      const subfolders = items.filter(d => d.isDirectory()).map(d => d.name);
      const jsonFiles = items.filter(d => d.isFile() && d.name.endsWith('.json'));

      // Process JSON files in category root
      if (jsonFiles.length > 0) {
        await processFolder(categoryPath, category.mainCategory, null);
      }

      // Process subfolders

      for (const subfolder of subfolders) {
        const subfolderPath = path.join(categoryPath, subfolder);
        await processFolder(subfolderPath, category.mainCategory, subfolder);
      }
    } catch (error: any) {
      console.error(`   ❌ Error:`, error.message);
    }

    console.log('');
  }

  console.log('═══════════════════════════════════════');
  console.log('✅ Import complete!');
  console.log(`   ✨ New records: ${totalInserted}`);
  console.log(`   🔄 Updated: ${totalUpdated}`);

  console.log(`   ❌ Errors: ${totalErrors}`);
  console.log('═══════════════════════════════════════\n');

  await client.end();
  process.exit(0);
}

// Run import
importPeople().catch((error) => {
  console.error('💥 Fatal error:', error);
  process.exit(1);
});



🔥 HOW IT WORKS - NO LOOPHOLES

🎬 SCRIPT 1: Movie Import (import-movies.ts)

What It Does:

1. Reads JSON files from ./test-movies/ folder

2. Checks for duplicates using tmdb_id

3. Converts URLs (posters, backdrops, trailers)

4. Inserts movie into database

5. Smart people lookup:

Checks if person exists by tmdb_person_id OR name

If found → Reuses existing person ID

If not found → Creates minimal stub with slug

If slug exists → Adds tmdb_person_id suffix to avoid conflicts

6. Links cast & crew via movie_credits table

Zero Loopholes:

✅ Never creates duplicate people (checks tmdb_id + name)

✅ Handles slug conflicts (adds suffix if needed)

✅ Skips duplicate movies

✅ Graceful error handling (continues on errors)

✅ Works even if people don't exist yet

👥 SCRIPT 2: People Import (import-people.ts)

What It Does:

1. Reads all JSON files from public/data/ folders

2. Smart matching by tmdb_person_id OR name (NOT by JSON id)

3. Three scenarios handled:
A. Person exists with SAME ID:

Updates metadata, category, biography, etc.

Keeps all movie_credits links intact

B. Person exists with DIFFERENT ID (stub):

Updates movie_credits table: old_id → new_id

Deletes old stub record



Inserts full data with correct ID from JSON

Movie credits stay linked! ✅

C. New person (doesn't exist):

Inserts fresh record with all data

Zero Loopholes:

✅ Finds stubs even if ID is wrong (uses tmdb_id/name match)

✅ Updates movie_credits table when ID changes

✅ No orphaned credits (all links preserved)

✅ Works for both new and existing people

✅ Can be run multiple times safely (upsert logic)

### **Step 6.1: Bulk OTT Link Fetcher**

```python```
# For each movie without OTT links

for movie in movies_without_ott:
    # Try JustWatch API



    ott_data = justwatch.search(movie.title, movie.year)

    # Extract streaming links
    for platform in ott_data.streaming_providers:

        save_ott_link(movie.id, platform.name, platform.url)

    # Update JSON file
    update_movie_json(movie.id, ott_links=ott_data)
```

**✅ No Loopholes:**

- Automated OTT link fetching
- Updates JSON + DB
