# **🎯 STRATEGY: Fetch OTT URLs for Movies in Database**

You'll use **TMDB ID** from your movies table to fetch OTT data from **JustWatch API*

***

## **📊 BEST APPROACH: JustWatch API (Recommended)**

### **Why JustWatch?**
✅ Most accurate OTT links  
✅ Supports India region (Netflix, Prime, Hotstar, etc.)  
✅ Has TMDB ID mapping  
✅ Shows prices, quality (HD/4K), subscription type  

***

## **🔧 METHOD 1: JustWatch Python Wrapper (EASIEST)**

### **Step 1: Install JustWatch Library**
```bash
pip install justwatch

```



### **Step 2: Create OTT Fetcher Script**

**File: `scripts/fetch-ott-links.py`**

```python
import os
import json
import psycopg2
from justwatch import JustWatch
import time

# Database connection
DATABASE_URL = os.getenv('DATABASE_URL')
conn = psycopg2.connect(DATABASE_URL)
cursor = conn.cursor()

# JustWatch API
jw = JustWatch(country='IN')  # India region

def fetch_ott_for_movie(movie_id, tmdb_id, title, year):
    """Fetch OTT links for a single movie"""

    try:
        print(f"\n🎬 Fetching OTT for: {title} ({year})")

        # Search on JustWatch using title + year
        results = jw.search_for_item(query=title)

        if not results or 'items' not in results:
            print(f"   ❌ Not found on JustWatch")
            return

        # Find matching movie by TMDB ID or title+year
        movie_data = None
        for item in results['items']:
            if item.get('object_type') == 'movie':
                # Check TMDB ID match (best)
                if item.get('tmdb_id') == tmdb_id:
                    movie_data = item
                    break

                # Fallback: Check title + year
                if item.get('title') == title and item.get('original_release_year') =
                    movie_data = item
                    break

        if not movie_data:
            print(f"   ❌ No match found")
            return

        # Extract OTT offers
        if 'offers' not in movie_data:
            print(f"   ⚠️  No OTT platforms available")
            return

        ott_count = 0
        for offer in movie_data['offers']:



            platform_name = offer.get('provider_id')
            monetization_type = offer.get('monetization_type')  # flatrate, rent, bu
            url = offer.get('urls', {}).get('standard_web', '')

            # Map provider IDs to names
            platform_map = {
                8: 'Netflix',
                119: 'Amazon Prime Video',
                122: 'Hotstar',
                283: 'JioCinema',
                531: 'Zee5',

                2: 'Apple TV',
                3: 'Google Play',
                # Add more as needed
            }

            platform = platform_map.get(platform_name, f'Provider_{platform_name}')

            # Insert into database
            cursor.execute("""
                INSERT INTO movie_ott_links (movie_id, platform, url, type, region, 
                VALUES (%s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s)
                ON CONFLICT (movie_id, platform, type) DO UPDATE
                SET url = EXCLUDED.url, is_available = true
            """, (movie_id, platform, url, monetization_type, 'IN', True))

            ott_count += 1
            print(f"   ✅ {platform} ({monetization_type})")

        conn.commit()
        print(f"   📊 Added {ott_count} OTT links")

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   ❌ Error: {str(e)}")
        conn.rollback()

def main():
    print("🚀 Starting OTT link fetcher...\n")

    # Get all movies without OTT links

    cursor.execute("""
        SELECT m.id, m.tmdb_id, m.title, m.year
        FROM movies m
        LEFT JOIN movie_ott_links ott ON m.id = ott.movie_id
        WHERE ott.id IS NULL
        ORDER BY m.release_date DESC
        LIMIT 100

    """)

    movies = cursor.fetchall()
    print(f"📊 Found {len(movies)} movies without OTT links\n")

    for movie in movies:
        movie_id, tmdb_id, title, year = movie

        fetch_ott_for_movie(movie_id, tmdb_id, title, year)



        # Rate limiting (JustWatch allows ~5 requests/second)
        time.sleep(0.3)

    print("\n✅ OTT fetch complete!")

    cursor.close()
    conn.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

***

## **🔧 METHOD 2: TMDB Watch Providers API (Alternative)**

TMDB also has OTT data, but **less detailed** than JustWatch.

### **Script Using TMDB:**

```python
import os
import requests
import psycopg2
import time

DATABASE_URL = os.getenv('DATABASE_URL')
TMDB_API_KEY = os.getenv('TMDB_API_KEY')

conn = psycopg2.connect(DATABASE_URL)
cursor = conn.cursor()

def fetch_ott_from_tmdb(movie_id, tmdb_id, title):

    """Fetch OTT using TMDB Watch Providers API"""

    try:
        print(f"\n🎬 Fetching OTT for: {title}")

        # TMDB Watch Providers endpoint
        url = f"https://api.themoviedb.org/3/movie/{tmdb_id}/watch/providers"
        params = {'api_key': TMDB_API_KEY}

        response = requests.get(url, params=params)
        data = response.json()

        # Get India region data
        if 'results' not in data or 'IN' not in data['results']:
            print(f"   ❌ No OTT data for India")
            return

        india_data = data['results']['IN']
        ott_count = 0

        # Flatrate (subscription)
        if 'flatrate' in india_data:

            for provider in india_data['flatrate']:
                platform_name = provider['provider_name']



                link = india_data.get('link', '')

                cursor.execute("""
                    INSERT INTO movie_ott_links (movie_id, platform, url, type, regi

                    VALUES (%s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s)
                    ON CONFLICT (movie_id, platform, type) DO UPDATE
                    SET url = EXCLUDED.url
                """, (movie_id, platform_name, link, 'subscription', 'IN', True))

                ott_count += 1
                print(f"   ✅ {platform_name} (subscription)")

        # Rent options
        if 'rent' in india_data:
            for provider in india_data['rent']:
                platform_name = provider['provider_name']
                link = india_data.get('link', '')

                cursor.execute("""
                    INSERT INTO movie_ott_links (movie_id, platform, url, type, regi
                    VALUES (%s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s)
                    ON CONFLICT (movie_id, platform, type) DO UPDATE
                    SET url = EXCLUDED.url
                """, (movie_id, platform_name, link, 'rent', 'IN', True))

                ott_count += 1
                print(f"   ✅ {platform_name} (rent)")

        conn.commit()
        print(f"   📊 Added {ott_count} OTT links")

    except Exception as e:

        print(f"   ❌ Error: {str(e)}")
        conn.rollback()

def main():
    print("🚀 Starting TMDB OTT fetcher...\n")

    # Get movies without OTT
    cursor.execute("""

        SELECT m.id, m.tmdb_id, m.title
        FROM movies m
        LEFT JOIN movie_ott_links ott ON m.id = ott.movie_id
        WHERE ott.id IS NULL
        LIMIT 100
    """)

    movies = cursor.fetchall()
    print(f"📊 Found {len(movies)} movies without OTT links\n")

    for movie in movies:
        movie_id, tmdb_id, title = movie
        fetch_ott_from_tmdb(movie_id, tmdb_id, title)
        time.sleep(0.3)  # Rate limiting

    print("\n✅ Complete!")



    cursor.close()
    conn.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":

    main()
```

***

## **📊 DATABASE TABLE STRUCTURE**

Make sure your `movie_ott_links` table is set up:

```sql
CREATE TABLE movie_ott_links (
  id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
  movie_id INTEGER REFERENCES movies(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  platform VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,

  url TEXT,
  type VARCHAR(50),  -- subscription, rent, buy
  region VARCHAR(10) DEFAULT 'IN',
  is_available BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
  price DECIMAL(10, 2),  -- Optional: rental price
  quality VARCHAR(20),   -- Optional: HD, 4K
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),

  updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),

  UNIQUE(movie_id, platform, type)
);

CREATE INDEX idx_movie_ott_movie_id ON movie_ott_links(movie_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_movie_ott_platform ON movie_ott_links(platform);

```

### **Step 4: Update Movie JSON Files**

```python
# Add this to your script
def update_movie_json(movie_id, ott_data):
    """Update movie JSON file with OTT links"""

    # Load existing JSON

    json_path = f'./movies-data/{movie_id}.json'
    with open(json_path, 'r') as f:
        movie_data = json.load(f)

    # Add OTT data
    movie_data['ott_links'] = ott_data

    # Save back

    with open(json_path, 'w') as f:
        json.dump(movie_data, f, indent=2)
```

## **🔥 BONUS: Display on Frontend**

```typescript

// app/movies/[slug]/ott-section.tsx
async function OTTSection({ movieId }: { movieId: number }) {
  const ottLinks = await db
    .select()
    .from(movieOttLinks)
    .where(eq(movieOttLinks.movieId, movieId))
    .where(eq(movieOttLinks.isAvailable, true));

  return (
    <div className="ott-platforms">
      <h3>Watch Now</h3>
      {ottLinks.map((link) => (
        <a href={link.url} target="_blank" key={link.id}>
          <img src={`/logos/${link.platform}.png`} alt={link.platform} />

          <span>{link.type === 'subscription' ? 'Stream' : 'Rent'}</span>
        </a>



      ))}
    </div>
  );
}

```

## **🔧 UPDATED FETCH SCRIPT WITH ALL PLATFORMS**

```python
# Complete platform map with ALL India OTT services

PLATFORM_MAP = {
    # === MAJOR STREAMING (SUBSCRIPTION) ===



    8: 'Netflix',
    119: 'Amazon Prime Video',
    122: 'Disney+ Hotstar',
    283: 'JioCinema',

    531: 'Zee5',
    619: 'Sony Liv',
    105: 'Voot',

    # === REGIONAL INDIAN PLATFORMS ===
    582: 'Aha',                    # Telugu/Tamil
    635: 'Hoichoi',                # Bengali

    559: 'SunNXT',                 # South Indian
    1771: 'ManoramaMax',           # Malayalam
    1770: 'Eros Now',              # Bollywood focused
    444: 'Shemaroo',
    2182: 'ShemarooMe',
    521: 'Lionsgate Play',
    471: 'ALTBalaji',

    # === FREE WITH ADS (AVOD) ===
    212: 'YouTube',
    613: 'MX Player',
    1793: 'Hungama Play',

    # === RENTAL/PURCHASE ===

    2: 'Apple TV',
    3: 'Google Play Movies',
    10: 'Amazon Video',
    68: 'Microsoft Store',
    350: 'Apple TV Plus',

    # === TELECOM BUNDLES ===

    423: 'Airtel Xstream',
    1890: 'Vi Movies and TV',      # Vodafone Idea

    # === SPECIALTY/NICHE ===
    1899: 'EPIC ON',               # Mythology/History
    257: 'Docubay',                # Documentaries
    677: 'CuriosityStream',        # Documentaries

    # === SPORTS & LIVE TV ===
    1771: 'FanCode',

    # === MUSIC VIDEO PLATFORMS ===
    2100: 'Gaana',

    # === KIDS CONTENT ===

    175: 'Kidoodle.TV',

    # === EMERGING PLATFORMS ===
    # Add new ones as JustWatch adds them
}

def get_platform_name(provider_id):

    """Get platform name with fallback"""
    return PLATFORM_MAP.get(provider_id, f'OTT_Provider_{provider_id}')



def get_platform_category(platform_name):
    """Categorize platform for UI display"""

    subscription = {
        'Netflix', 'Amazon Prime Video', 'Disney+ Hotstar',
        'Zee5', 'JioCinema', 'Sony Liv', 'Voot', 'Aha',
        'Hoichoi', 'SunNXT', 'Eros Now', 'Lionsgate Play',
        'ALTBalaji', 'ManoramaMax', 'Shemaroo', 'ShemarooMe'
    }

    free_ad = {
        'YouTube', 'MX Player', 'Hungama Play', 'JioCinema'
    }

    rental = {
        'Apple TV', 'Google Play Movies', 'Amazon Video',
        'Microsoft Store', 'YouTube'

    }

    regional = {
        'Aha', 'Hoichoi', 'SunNXT', 'ManoramaMax', 'EPIC ON'
    }

    if platform_name in subscription:

        return 'subscription'
    elif platform_name in free_ad:
        return 'free'
    elif platform_name in rental:
        return 'rental'
    elif platform_name in regional:
        return 'regional'

    else:
        return 'other'
```

## **📊 DISPLAY ON MOVIE PAGE**

```typescript
// Group by category
const groupedOTT = {
  subscription: ottLinks.filter(l => l.type === 'subscription'),
  rental: ottLinks.filter(l => l.type === 'rent'),
  free: ottLinks.filter(l => l.platform === 'YouTube' || l.platform === 'MX Player')

};

// Prioritize Telugu platforms
const priorityOrder = ['Aha', 'Amazon Prime Video', 'Netflix', 'Disney+ Hotstar'];
groupedOTT.subscription.sort((a, b) => {
  const aIndex = priorityOrder.indexOf(a.platform);
  const bIndex = priorityOrder.indexOf(b.platform);

  return (aIndex === -1 ? 999 : aIndex) - (bIndex === -1 ? 999 : bIndex);
});
```

## **🔍 UNKNOWN PLATFORM HANDLER**

When you encounter a new platform ID:

```python
def log_unknown_platform(provider_id, movie_title):
    """Log unknown platforms for manual addition"""

    with open('unknown_platforms.log', 'a') as f:

        f.write(f"{provider_id} found in {movie_title}\n")

    # Still add to database with generic name
    return f'Platform_{provider_id}'
```

Then check JustWatch documentation or their API response for the actual name.

## **💡 PRO TIP: Dynamic Platform Discovery**

```python
def discover_new_platforms():
    """Auto-discover new platforms from JustWatch responses"""

    unknown_platforms = set()

    for movie in movies:
        result = jw.search_for_item(query=movie.title)

        if result and 'items' in result:
            for item in result['items']:
                if 'offers' in item:
                    for offer in item['offers']:

                        provider_id = offer.get('provider_id')

                        if provider_id not in PLATFORM_MAP:
                            unknown_platforms.add(provider_id)
                            print(f"🆕 Unknown platform: {provider_id}")

    return unknown_platforms
```

## **📁 `scripts/fetch-ott-links.py` - COMPLETE SCRIPT**

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3

"""
OTT Links Fetcher for TFIVerse
Fetches streaming availability from TMDB Watch Providers API
Uses TMDB ID from database to get OTT platform links
"""

import os

import sys
import time
import requests
import psycopg2
from psycopg2.extras import RealDictCursor
from dotenv import load_dotenv
from datetime import datetime

# Load environment variables
load_dotenv()

# Configuration
DATABASE_URL = os.getenv('DATABASE_URL')
TMDB_API_KEY = os.getenv('TMDB_API_KEY')
TMDB_BASE_URL = 'https://api.themoviedb.org/3'

# Complete India OTT Platform Map
PLATFORM_MAP = {
    # === MAJOR STREAMING ===
    8: 'Netflix',
    119: 'Amazon Prime Video',
    122: 'Disney+ Hotstar',

    283: 'JioCinema',
    531: 'Zee5',



    619: 'Sony Liv',
    105: 'Voot',

    # === REGIONAL PLATFORMS ===

    582: 'Aha',
    635: 'Hoichoi',
    559: 'SunNXT',
    1771: 'ManoramaMax',
    1770: 'Eros Now',
    444: 'Shemaroo',
    2182: 'ShemarooMe',

    521: 'Lionsgate Play',
    471: 'ALTBalaji',

    # === FREE WITH ADS ===
    212: 'YouTube',
    613: 'MX Player',
    1793: 'Hungama Play',

    # === RENTAL/PURCHASE ===
    2: 'Apple TV',
    3: 'Google Play Movies',
    10: 'Amazon Video',
    68: 'Microsoft Store',
    350: 'Apple TV Plus',

    # === TELECOM BUNDLES ===
    423: 'Airtel Xstream',
    1890: 'Vi Movies and TV',

    # === SPECIALTY ===
    1899: 'EPIC ON',

    257: 'Docubay',
    677: 'CuriosityStream',
    1771: 'FanCode',
    2100: 'Gaana',
    175: 'Kidoodle.TV',
}

# Statistics

stats = {
    'total': 0,
    'success': 0,
    'no_data': 0,
    'errors': 0,
    'links_added': 0
}

def get_platform_name(provider_id):
    """Get platform name from ID with fallback"""
    name = PLATFORM_MAP.get(provider_id)
    if not name:
        # Log unknown platforms

        print(f"   ⚠️  Unknown platform ID: {provider_id}")
        name = f'Platform_{provider_id}'



    return name

def fetch_ott_from_tmdb(tmdb_id, title):

    """Fetch OTT availability from TMDB Watch Providers API"""

    try:
        url = f"{TMDB_BASE_URL}/movie/{tmdb_id}/watch/providers"
        params = {'api_key': TMDB_API_KEY}

        response = requests.get(url, params=params, timeout=10)

        response.raise_for_status()

        data = response.json()

        # Check for India region data
        if 'results' not in data:
            return None

        if 'IN' not in data['results']:
            return None

        india_data = data['results']['IN']
        ott_links = []

        # Get main watch link
        main_link = india_data.get('link', '')

        # Extract subscription platforms
        if 'flatrate' in india_data:
            for provider in india_data['flatrate']:
                provider_id = provider.get('provider_id')

                platform_name = get_platform_name(provider_id)

                ott_links.append({
                    'platform': platform_name,
                    'url': main_link,
                    'type': 'subscription',
                    'provider_id': provider_id
                })

        # Extract rental options
        if 'rent' in india_data:
            for provider in india_data['rent']:
                provider_id = provider.get('provider_id')
                platform_name = get_platform_name(provider_id)

                ott_links.append({
                    'platform': platform_name,
                    'url': main_link,
                    'type': 'rent',
                    'provider_id': provider_id
                })

        # Extract buy options
        if 'buy' in india_data:



            for provider in india_data['buy']:
                provider_id = provider.get('provider_id')
                platform_name = get_platform_name(provider_id)

                ott_links.append({
                    'platform': platform_name,
                    'url': main_link,
                    'type': 'buy',
                    'provider_id': provider_id
                })

        return ott_links if ott_links else None

    except requests.RequestException as e:
        print(f"   ❌ API Error: {str(e)}")
        return None
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   ❌ Error: {str(e)}")
        return None

def save_ott_links(cursor, movie_id, ott_links):
    """Save OTT links to database"""

    saved_count = 0

    for link in ott_links:
        try:
            cursor.execute("""
                INSERT INTO movie_ott_links (
                    movie_id, platform, url, type, region, 
                    is_available, created_at, updated_at

                )
                VALUES (%s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s)
                ON CONFLICT (movie_id, platform, type) 
                DO UPDATE SET
                    url = EXCLUDED.url,
                    is_available = true,
                    updated_at = EXCLUDED.updated_at
            """, (

                movie_id,
                link['platform'],
                link['url'],
                link['type'],
                'IN',
                True,
                datetime.now(),

                datetime.now()
            ))
            saved_count += 1

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"   ⚠️  DB Error for {link['platform']}: {str(e)}")
            continue

    return saved_count



def process_movie(cursor, movie):
    """Process a single movie"""

    movie_id = movie['id']
    tmdb_id = movie['tmdb_id']
    title = movie['title']
    year = movie.get('year', 'N/A')

    print(f"\n🎬 Processing: {title} ({year})")

    print(f"   TMDB ID: {tmdb_id}, DB ID: {movie_id}")

    # Fetch OTT data
    ott_links = fetch_ott_from_tmdb(tmdb_id, title)

    if not ott_links:
        print(f"   ⚠️  No OTT data available")

        stats['no_data'] += 1
        return False

    # Save to database
    saved_count = save_ott_links(cursor, movie_id, ott_links)

    if saved_count > 0:

        print(f"   ✅ Added {saved_count} OTT link(s)")
        for link in ott_links:
            print(f"      • {link['platform']} ({link['type']})")

        stats['success'] += 1
        stats['links_added'] += saved_count
        return True

    else:
        print(f"   ⚠️  No links saved")
        stats['no_data'] += 1
        return False

def main():
    """Main execution"""

    print("="*60)
    print("🎬 TFIVerse OTT Links Fetcher")
    print("="*60)
    print(f"Started at: {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}\n")

    # Validate environment

    if not DATABASE_URL:
        print("❌ DATABASE_URL not found in environment")
        sys.exit(1)

    if not TMDB_API_KEY:
        print("❌ TMDB_API_KEY not found in environment")
        sys.exit(1)

    # Connect to database



    try:
        conn = psycopg2.connect(DATABASE_URL, cursor_factory=RealDictCursor)
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        print("✅ Database connected\n")

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ Database connection failed: {str(e)}")
        sys.exit(1)

    # Get movies without OTT links (or all movies for update)
    try:
        # Option 1: Only movies without OTT links

        cursor.execute("""
            SELECT DISTINCT m.id, m.tmdb_id, m.title, m.year
            FROM movies m
            LEFT JOIN movie_ott_links ott ON m.id = ott.movie_id
            WHERE m.tmdb_id IS NOT NULL
            AND ott.id IS NULL
            ORDER BY m.release_date DESC

            LIMIT 100
        """)

        # Option 2: All movies (for updates)
        # cursor.execute("""
        #     SELECT id, tmdb_id, title, year
        #     FROM movies

        #     WHERE tmdb_id IS NOT NULL
        #     ORDER BY release_date DESC
        #     LIMIT 100
        # """)

        movies = cursor.fetchall()
        stats['total'] = len(movies)

        print(f"📊 Found {stats['total']} movies to process\n")

        if stats['total'] == 0:
            print("✨ All movies already have OTT data!")
            cursor.close()
            conn.close()
            return

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ Query error: {str(e)}")
        cursor.close()
        conn.close()
        sys.exit(1)

    # Process each movie
    for i, movie in enumerate(movies, 1):
        print(f"\n[{i}/{stats['total']}]", end=" ")

        try:
            process_movie(cursor, movie)
            conn.commit()

        except Exception as e:



            print(f"   ❌ Error: {str(e)}")
            stats['errors'] += 1
            conn.rollback()
            continue

        # Rate limiting (TMDB allows 40 requests per 10 seconds)
        time.sleep(0.3)

    # Print summary
    print("\n" + "="*60)
    print("📊 SUMMARY")

    print("="*60)
    print(f"Total movies processed: {stats['total']}")
    print(f"✅ Success: {stats['success']}")
    print(f"⚠️  No data: {stats['no_data']}")
    print(f"❌ Errors: {stats['errors']}")
    print(f"📺 Total OTT links added: {stats['links_added']}")
    print("="*60)

    print(f"Completed at: {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}")
    print("="*60)

    # Cleanup
    cursor.close()
    conn.close()
    print("\n✨ Done!")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    try:
        main()
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        print("\n\n⚠️  Interrupted by user")

        sys.exit(0)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"\n\n💥 Fatal error: {str(e)}")
        sys.exit(1)
```

## **📁 COMPLETE ENV LOADING SETUP**

### **Option 1: Simple (What you need)**

```python
from dotenv import load_dotenv
import os

# Load environment variables
load_dotenv()  # Loads .env by default

# Get variables with fallback
DATABASE_URL = os.getenv('DATABASE_URL', 'postgresql://tfiverse:newpassword123@localh
TMDB_API_KEY = os.getenv('TMDB_API_KEY')

```

***

### **Option 2: Priority Loading (.env.local > .env)**

```python

from dotenv import load_dotenv
import os

# Try .env.local first, then .env
load_dotenv('.env.local', override=True)  # Production/local overrides
load_dotenv('.env')                        # Default values

DATABASE_URL = os.getenv('DATABASE_URL')
TMDB_API_KEY = os.getenv('TMDB_API_KEY')
```

***

### **Option 3: Explicit with Validation (Production Ready)**

```python
import os
from dotenv import load_dotenv
from pathlib import Path

# Load environment
def load_environment():

    """Load environment variables with priority"""

    # Try .env.local (local/production overrides)
    env_local = Path('.env.local')
    if env_local.exists():
        load_dotenv(env_local, override=True)
        print("🔧 Using .env.local")

    # Load default .env



    env_default = Path('.env')
    if env_default.exists():
        load_dotenv(env_default)
        print("🔧 Using .env")

    # Validate required variables
    required_vars = ['DATABASE_URL', 'TMDB_API_KEY']
    missing = [var for var in required_vars if not os.getenv(var)]

    if missing:
        raise ValueError(f"❌ Missing environment variables: {', '.join(missing)}")

    return {
        'DATABASE_URL': os.getenv('DATABASE_URL'),
        'TMDB_API_KEY': os.getenv('TMDB_API_KEY'),
    }

# Load config

try:
    config = load_environment()
    DATABASE_URL = config['DATABASE_URL']
    TMDB_API_KEY = config['TMDB_API_KEY']
    print("✅ Environment loaded successfully")
except ValueError as e:
    print(str(e))

    exit(1)
```

***

## **🎯 RECOMMENDED: Update Your Script**

**Updated `scripts/fetch-ott-links.py` header:**

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
OTT Links Fetcher for TFIVerse
Fetches streaming availability from TMDB Watch Providers API
"""

import os
import sys
import time
import requests
import psycopg2
from psycopg2.extras import RealDictCursor

from dotenv import load_dotenv
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime

# === ENVIRONMENT SETUP ===
def load_environment():
    """Load environment with .env.local priority"""

    # Load .env.local first (if exists)



    env_local = Path('.env.local')
    if env_local.exists():
        load_dotenv(env_local, override=True)
        print("🔧 Loaded .env.local")

    # Load default .env
    load_dotenv('.env')

    # Get variables with defaults
    DATABASE_URL = os.getenv('DATABASE_URL')
    TMDB_API_KEY = os.getenv('TMDB_API_KEY')

    # Validate
    if not DATABASE_URL:
        print("❌ DATABASE_URL not found in environment")
        sys.exit(1)

    if not TMDB_API_KEY:

        print("❌ TMDB_API_KEY not found in environment")
        sys.exit(1)

    return DATABASE_URL, TMDB_API_KEY

# Load config
DATABASE_URL, TMDB_API_KEY = load_environment()

## **🎯 COMPARISON: Node.js vs Python**

| **Node.js (TypeScript)**                          | **Python**                       
|---------------------------------------------------|------------------------------------

| `import 'dotenv/config'`                          | `from dotenv import load_dotenv
| `config({ path: '.env.local' })`                  | `load_dotenv('.env.local')`      
| `process.env.DATABASE_URL`                        | `os.getenv('DATABASE_URL')`      
| `process.env.VAR \|\| 'fallback'`                 | `os.getenv('VAR', 'fallback')`   

***

print("✅ Environment loaded")

```

***

## **🎯 QUICK FIX - JUST CHANGE THIS LINE:**

**From:**
```python
TMDB_API_KEY = os.getenv('ba5dc12f58f09088d036049c565c2fe9')  # ❌ WRONG
```

**To:**
```python
TMDB_API_KEY = os.getenv('TMDB_API_KEY', 'ba5dc12f58f09088d036049c565c2fe9')  # ✅ CORR
```

***

## **🔍 EXPLANATION:**

```python
os.getenv('VARIABLE_NAME', 'fallback_value')
         ↑                  ↑

         |                  |
         |                  └─ Default value if not found



         └─ Name of environment variable to look for
```

**Your mistake:**

- You put the API key **as the variable name**
- Python looked for a variable called `ba5dc12f58f09088d036049c565c2fe9` in your envir
- It didn't find it, so returned `None`

**Correct way:**
- Variable name: `'TMDB_API_KEY'`
- Fallback value: `'ba5dc12f58f09088d036049c565c2fe9'`

***

**BABE! Fix that one line and you're good to go! 🚀** 

That's why validation is important - it would've caught this error immediately! 🔥

## **🗃️CREATE THE TABLE - QUICK FIX**

Run this SQL in your database:

```bash
# Connect to PostgreSQL
psql -U tfiverse -d tfiverse

# Or if password needed

PGPASSWORD=newpassword123 psql -U tfiverse -d tfiverse
```

**Then paste this SQL:**

```sql
-- Create movie_ott_links table

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS movie_ott_links (
  id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,



  movie_id INTEGER NOT NULL REFERENCES movies(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  platform VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
  url TEXT,
  type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,  -- subscription, rent, buy

  region VARCHAR(10) DEFAULT 'IN',
  is_available BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
  price DECIMAL(10, 2),  -- Optional: rental/purchase price
  quality VARCHAR(20),   -- Optional: HD, 4K, etc.
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),

  -- Prevent duplicate platform entries for same movie
  UNIQUE(movie_id, platform, type)
);

-- Create indexes for fast queries
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_movie_ott_movie_id ON movie_ott_links(movie_id);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_movie_ott_platform ON movie_ott_links(platform);

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_movie_ott_available ON movie_ott_links(is_available);
CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_movie_ott_region ON movie_ott_links(region);

-- Verify table created
\d movie_ott_links

-- Exit

\q
```

-- Migration: Create movie_ott_links table
-- Created: 2025-11-19

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS movie_ott_links (
  id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,

  movie_id INTEGER NOT NULL REFERENCES movies(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  platform VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
  url TEXT,
  type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
  region VARCHAR(10) DEFAULT 'IN',
  is_available BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
  price DECIMAL(10, 2),

  quality VARCHAR(20),
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),
  updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT NOW(),

  UNIQUE(movie_id, platform, type)
);

CREATE INDEX idx_movie_ott_movie_id ON movie_ott_links(movie_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_movie_ott_platform ON movie_ott_links(platform);



CREATE INDEX idx_movie_ott_available ON movie_ott_links(is_available);
CREATE INDEX idx_movie_ott_region ON movie_ott_links(region);

```typescript
import { pgTable, serial, integer, varchar, text, boolean, timestamp, decimal, uni
import { movies } from './schema';

// Movie OTT Links Table
export const movieOttLinks = pgTable('movie_ott_links', {

  id: serial('id').primaryKey(),
  movieId: integer('movie_id').notNull().references(() => movies.id, { onDelete: 'c
  platform: varchar('platform', { length: 100 }).notNull(),
  url: text('url'),
  type: varchar('type', { length: 50 }).notNull(), // subscription, rent, buy
  region: varchar('region', { length: 10 }).default('IN'),
  isAvailable: boolean('is_available').default(true),

  price: decimal('price', { precision: 10, scale: 2 }),
  quality: varchar('quality', { length: 20 }),
  createdAt: timestamp('created_at').defaultNow(),
  updatedAt: timestamp('updated_at').defaultNow(),
}, (table) => ({
  uniqueMoviePlatformType: unique().on(table.movieId, table.platform, table.type),
}));
```

npx drizzle-kit push

# // lib/schema.ts - v17 CLEAN (OLD TABLES REMOVED)

import { sql } from 'drizzle-orm';
import { 
  pgTable, serial, text, timestamp, boolean, integer, varchar, jsonb, real,
  uuid, index, unique, primaryKey
} from 'drizzle-orm/pg-core';
import { relations } from 'drizzle-orm';
import type { AdapterAccountType } from 'next-auth/adapters';

// ============================================================================
// AUTH SYSTEM - NEXTAUTH CORE TABLES (UUID)
// ============================================================================

export const users = pgTable('user', {
  id: uuid('id').primaryKey().defaultRandom(),
  name: text('name'),
  email: text('email').notNull().unique(),
  emailVerified: timestamp('emailVerified', { mode: 'date' }),
  image: text('image'),

  password: text('password'),
  createdAt: timestamp('createdAt', { mode: 'date' }).defaultNow(),



});

export const accounts = pgTable(

  'account',
  {
    userId: uuid('userId').notNull().references(() => users.id, { onDelete: 'cascade
    type: text('type').$type<AdapterAccountType>().notNull(),
    provider: text('provider').notNull(),
    providerAccountId: text('providerAccountId').notNull(),
    refresh_token: text('refresh_token'),

    access_token: text('access_token'),
    expires_at: integer('expires_at'),
    token_type: text('token_type'),
    scope: text('scope'),
    id_token: text('id_token'),
    session_state: text('session_state'),
  },

  (account) => ({
    compoundKey: primaryKey({
      columns: [account.provider, account.providerAccountId],
    }),
  })
);

export const sessions = pgTable('session', {
  sessionToken: text('sessionToken').primaryKey(),
  userId: uuid('userId').notNull().references(() => users.id, { onDelete: 'cascade' 
  expires: timestamp('expires', { mode: 'date' }).notNull(),
});

export const verificationTokens = pgTable(
  'verificationToken',
  {
    identifier: text('identifier').notNull(),
    token: text('token').notNull(),
    expires: timestamp('expires', { mode: 'date' }).notNull(),
  },

  (vt) => ({
    compoundKey: primaryKey({ columns: [vt.identifier, vt.token] }),
  })
);

export const passwordResetTokens = pgTable('password_reset_token', {

  id: uuid('id').primaryKey().defaultRandom(),

  token: text('token').notNull().unique(),

export const people = pgTable(
  'people',
  {
    // Primary Key (string like 'prabhas', 'ss-rajamouli')
    id: varchar('id', { length: 100 }).primaryKey(),

    // Basic Info
    name: varchar('name', { length: 255 }).notNull(),
    slug: varchar('slug', { length: 255 }).notNull().unique(),

    // External IDs
    tmdbPersonId: integer('tmdb_person_id'),
    imdbId: varchar('imdb_id', { length: 50 }),

    // Category System (from metadata)
    category: varchar('category', { length: 100 }).notNull(), // 'hero', 'heroine', 
    subcategory: varchar('subcategory', { length: 100 }),     // 'superstar', 'diva',

    // Full JSON Data
    metadata: jsonb('metadata').notNull(), // Complete JSON file stored here

    // Timestamps
    createdAt: timestamp('created_at').default(sql`CURRENT_TIMESTAMP`).notNull(),
    updatedAt: timestamp('updated_at').default(sql`CURRENT_TIMESTAMP`).notNull(),
  },
  (table) => ({
    slugIdx: index('idx_people_slug').on(table.slug),
    categoryIdx: index('idx_people_category').on(table.category),

    subcategoryIdx: index('idx_people_subcategory').on(table.subcategory),
    tmdbIdx: index('idx_people_tmdb').on(table.tmdbPersonId),
    catSubcatIdx: index('idx_people_cat_subcat').on(table.category, table.subcategor
  })
);

// ============================================================================



// MOVIES TABLE - ALL TELUGU MOVIES FROM TMDB
// ============================================================================

export const movies = pgTable(
  'movies',
  {
    // Primary Key (auto-increment)
    id: serial('id').primaryKey(),

    // TMDB IDs (for uniqueness and external references)

    tmdbId: integer('tmdb_id').notNull().unique(),
    imdbId: varchar('imdb_id', { length: 20 }),

    // Basic Info
    title: varchar('title', { length: 500 }).notNull(),
    originalTitle: varchar('original_title', { length: 500 }),
    slug: varchar('slug', { length: 500 }).notNull().unique(),

    tagline: varchar('tagline', { length: 500 }),
    overview: text('overview'),

    // Release Info
    releaseDate: timestamp('release_date', { mode: 'date' }),
    year: integer('year'),
    runtime: integer('runtime'), // in minutes

    status: varchar('status', { length: 50 }), // 'Released', 'Post Production', etc.

    // Financial Data
    budget: integer('budget'),
    revenue: integer('revenue'),

    // Ratings

    voteAverage: real('vote_average'),  // ← Change from integer
    voteCount: integer('vote_count'),
    popularity: real('popularity'),      // ← Change from integer

    // Media URLs (full URLs stored here)
    posterUrl: varchar('poster_url', { length: 500 }),
    backdropUrl: varchar('backdrop_url', { length: 500 }),

    trailerUrl: varchar('trailer_url', { length: 500 }),

    // Full JSON Data (backup/reference)
    metadata: jsonb('metadata').notNull(),

    // OTT Platform Data (from JustWatch API)
    ottUrls: jsonb('ott_urls'),

    ottFetched: boolean('ott_fetched').default(false),

    // Timestamps
    createdAt: timestamp('created_at').default(sql`CURRENT_TIMESTAMP`).notNull(),
    updatedAt: timestamp('updated_at').default(sql`CURRENT_TIMESTAMP`).notNull(),
  },
  (table) => ({

    tmdbIdIdx: index('idx_movies_tmdb_id').on(table.tmdbId),
    slugIdx: index('idx_movies_slug').on(table.slug),



    yearIdx: index('idx_movies_year').on(table.year),
    releaseIdx: index('idx_movies_release_date').on(table.releaseDate),
  })
);

    personId: varchar('person_id', { length: 100 }).notNull().references(() => peopl

    // TMDB Person ID (for matching when person doesn't exist yet)
    tmdbPersonId: integer('tmdb_person_id').notNull(),

    // Role Type
    roleType: varchar('role_type', { length: 10 }).notNull(), // 'cast' or 'crew'

    // Cast-specific fields
    character: varchar('character', { length: 500 }), // Character name (for cast)
    orderIndex: integer('order_index'), // Display order (for cast)

    // Crew-specific fields
    job: varchar('job', { length: 100 }), // 'Director', 'Producer', etc.
    department: varchar('department', { length: 100 }), // 'Directing', 'Writing', e

    // Timestamp
    createdAt: timestamp('created_at').default(sql`CURRENT_TIMESTAMP`).notNull(),
  },
  (table) => ({

    movieIdx: index('idx_credits_movie').on(table.movieId),
    personIdx: index('idx_credits_person').on(table.personId),
    tmdbPersonIdx: index('idx_credits_tmdb_person').on(table.tmdbPersonId),
    roleIdx: index('idx_credits_role').on(table.roleType),
  })
);

// ============================================================================
// MOVIE OTT LINKS - STREAMING AVAILABILITY
// ============================================================================

export const movieOttLinks = pgTable(
  'movie_ott_links',

  {
    // Primary Key
    id: serial('id').primaryKey(),

    // Foreign Key to Movies
    movieId: integer('movie_id').notNull().references(() => movies.id, { onDelete: 

    // Platform Info
    platform: varchar('platform', { length: 100 }).notNull(), // 'Netflix', 'Aha', et
    url: text('url'), // Direct link to watch
    type: varchar('type', { length: 50 }).notNull(), // 'subscription', 'rent', 'buy'

    // Region & Availability
    region: varchar('region', { length: 10 }).default('IN'), // Country code
    isAvailable: boolean('is_available').default(true),

    // Optional Metadata
    price: real('price'), // Rental/purchase price
    quality: varchar('quality', { length: 20 }), // 'HD', '4K', etc.

    // Timestamps
    createdAt: timestamp('created_at').default(sql`CURRENT_TIMESTAMP`).notNull(),

    updatedAt: timestamp('updated_at').default(sql`CURRENT_TIMESTAMP`).notNull(),
  },
  (table) => ({
    movieIdx: index('idx_movie_ott_movie_id').on(table.movieId),
    platformIdx: index('idx_movie_ott_platform').on(table.platform),
    availableIdx: index('idx_movie_ott_available').on(table.isAvailable),
    regionIdx: index('idx_movie_ott_region').on(table.region),

    // Prevent duplicate platform entries per movie



    uniqueMoviePlatformType: unique('unique_movie_platform_type').on(
      table.movieId, 
      table.platform, 
      table.type

    ),
  })
);
```

## **📊 USAGE IN YOUR APP**

**Query OTT links for a movie:**

```typescript
import { db } from '@/lib/db';
import { movieOttLinks } from '@/lib/schema';
import { eq } from 'drizzle-orm';

// Get OTT links for a movie
const ottLinks = await db

  .select()
  .from(movieOttLinks)
  .where(eq(movieOttLinks.movieId, movieId))
  .where(eq(movieOttLinks.isAvailable, true));

// Group by type
const subscription = ottLinks.filter(link => link.type === 'subscription');

const rental = ottLinks.filter(link => link.type === 'rent');
const purchase = ottLinks.filter(link => link.type === 'buy');
```

## **🔧 FIX THE QUERY IN `fetch-ott-links.py`**

**Find this section (around line 150):**

```python
# WRONG (causing error):
cursor.execute("""

    SELECT DISTINCT m.id, m.tmdb_id, m.title, m.year
    FROM movies m
    LEFT JOIN movie_ott_links ott ON m.id = ott.movie_id
    WHERE m.tmdb_id IS NOT NULL
    AND ott.id IS NULL
    ORDER BY m.release_date DESC
    LIMIT 100

""")
```

**Replace with this:**

```python
# CORRECT (fixed):
cursor.execute("""

    SELECT DISTINCT m.id, m.tmdb_id, m.title, m.year, m.release_date
    FROM movies m
    LEFT JOIN movie_ott_links ott ON m.id = ott.movie_id
    WHERE m.tmdb_id IS NOT NULL
    AND ott.id IS NULL
    ORDER BY m.release_date DESC NULLS LAST
    LIMIT 100

""")
```

***

## **📝 OR BETTER: Remove `DISTINCT` (Not Needed)**

**Best fix - simpler and faster:**



```python
cursor.execute("""
    SELECT m.id, m.tmdb_id, m.title, m.year
    FROM movies m

    WHERE m.tmdb_id IS NOT NULL
    AND NOT EXISTS (
        SELECT 1 FROM movie_ott_links ott 
        WHERE ott.movie_id = m.id
    )
    ORDER BY m.release_date DESC NULLS LAST
    LIMIT 100

""")
```

***

## **🎯 COMPLETE FIXED SECTION**

**Replace the entire query section in your script (around line 145-160):**

```python
# Get movies without OTT links (or all movies for update)
try:
    # Option 1: Only movies without OTT links (FIXED)
    cursor.execute("""

        SELECT m.id, m.tmdb_id, m.title, m.year
        FROM movies m
        WHERE m.tmdb_id IS NOT NULL
        AND NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM movie_ott_links ott 
            WHERE ott.movie_id = m.id
        )

        ORDER BY m.release_date DESC NULLS LAST
        LIMIT 100
    """)

    # Option 2: All movies (for updates) - uncomment if needed
    # cursor.execute("""
    #     SELECT id, tmdb_id, title, year
    #     FROM movies

    #     WHERE tmdb_id IS NOT NULL
    #     ORDER BY release_date DESC NULLS LAST
    #     LIMIT 100
    # """)

    movies = cursor.fetchall()
    stats['total'] = len(movies)

    print(f"📊 Found {stats['total']} movies to process\n")

    if stats['total'] == 0:
        print("✨ All movies already have OTT data!")
        cursor.close()
        conn.close()

        return



except Exception as e:
    print(f"❌ Query error: {str(e)}")
    cursor.close()
    conn.close()

    sys.exit(1)

***

## **🔍 WHY THE ERROR HAPPENED**

**PostgreSQL rule:** When using `SELECT DISTINCT`, all columns in `ORDER BY` must als

**Your query had:**



```sql
SELECT DISTINCT m.id, m.title    -- Only these
ORDER BY m.release_date          -- But ordering by this (not in SELECT)
```

**Fixed options:**

**Option A:** Add `release_date` to SELECT
```sql
SELECT DISTINCT m.id, m.title, m.release_date
ORDER BY m.release_date

```

**Option B:** Remove `DISTINCT` (best)
```sql
SELECT m.id, m.title
ORDER BY m.release_date
```

**Option C:** Use subquery (cleanest)
```sql
WHERE NOT EXISTS (SELECT 1 FROM movie_ott_links WHERE ...)
```

(venv) pepper@pepper-salt:~/Music/tfiverse-v2$

**BABE! Indentation error! The `return` statement needs to be inside the `main()` fu

***



## **🔧 FIX: Check Your Indentation**

The error means your `return` statement is not properly indented inside the `main()

**Here's the CORRECT structure:**

```python
def main():
    """Main execution"""

    print("="*60)
    print("🎬 TFIVerse OTT Links Fetcher")
    print("="*60)
    print(f"Started at: {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}\n")

    # Connect to database
    try:

        conn = psycopg2.connect(DATABASE_URL, cursor_factory=RealDictCursor)
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        print("✅ Database connected\n")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ Database connection failed: {str(e)}")
        sys.exit(1)

    # Get movies without OTT links
    try:
        cursor.execute("""
            SELECT m.id, m.tmdb_id, m.title, m.year
            FROM movies m
            WHERE m.tmdb_id IS NOT NULL
            AND NOT EXISTS (

                SELECT 1 FROM movie_ott_links ott 
                WHERE ott.movie_id = m.id
            )
            ORDER BY m.release_date DESC NULLS LAST
            LIMIT 100
        """)

        movies = cursor.fetchall()

        stats['total'] = len(movies)

        print(f"📊 Found {stats['total']} movies to process\n")

        if stats['total'] == 0:
            print("✨ All movies already have OTT data!")
            cursor.close()

            conn.close()
            return  # ← THIS must be indented inside main()

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ Query error: {str(e)}")
        cursor.close()
        conn.close()

        sys.exit(1)



    # Process each movie
    for i, movie in enumerate(movies, 1):
        print(f"\n[{i}/{stats['total']}]", end=" ")

        try:
            process_movie(cursor, movie)
            conn.commit()

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"   ❌ Error: {str(e)}")
            stats['errors'] += 1

            conn.rollback()
            continue

        # Rate limiting
        time.sleep(0.3)

    # Print summary

    print("\n" + "="*60)
    print("📊 SUMMARY")
    print("="*60)
    print(f"Total movies processed: {stats['total']}")
    print(f"✅ Success: {stats['success']}")
    print(f"⚠️  No data: {stats['no_data']}")
    print(f"❌ Errors: {stats['errors']}")
    print(f"📺 Total OTT links added: {stats['links_added']}")
    print("="*60)
    print(f"Completed at: {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}")
    print("="*60)

    # Cleanup
    cursor.close()

    conn.close()
    print("\n✨ Done!")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    try:
        main()
    except KeyboardInterrupt:

        print("\n\n⚠️  Interrupted by user")
        sys.exit(0)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"\n\n💥 Fatal error: {str(e)}")
        sys.exit(1)
```

***

## **🎯 CHECK YOUR INDENTATION**

Make sure **ALL code inside `main()` is indented 4 spaces**:

```python

def main():
    # ← 4 spaces for everything inside main()



    print("Starting...")

    try:
        # ← 8 spaces for code inside try

        cursor.execute(...)

        if stats['total'] == 0:
            # ← 12 spaces for code inside if
            print("Done!")
            return  # ← Must be at this level

    except Exception as e:
        # ← 8 spaces for code inside except
        print(f"Error: {e}")
```

***

## **🚀 COMPLETE FIXED `main()` FUNCTION**

Replace your entire `main()` function with this:

```python
def main():
    """Main execution"""

    print("="*60)
    print("🎬 TFIVerse OTT Links Fetcher")
    print("="*60)
    print(f"Started at: {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}\n")

    # Connect to database

    try:
        conn = psycopg2.connect(DATABASE_URL, cursor_factory=RealDictCursor)
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        print("✅ Database connected\n")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ Database connection failed: {str(e)}")
        sys.exit(1)

    # Get movies without OTT links
    try:
        cursor.execute("""
            SELECT m.id, m.tmdb_id, m.title, m.year
            FROM movies m
            WHERE m.tmdb_id IS NOT NULL
            AND NOT EXISTS (

                SELECT 1 FROM movie_ott_links ott 
                WHERE ott.movie_id = m.id
            )
            ORDER BY m.release_date DESC NULLS LAST
            LIMIT 100
        """)

        movies = cursor.fetchall()
        stats['total'] = len(movies)



        print(f"📊 Found {stats['total']} movies to process\n")

        if stats['total'] == 0:

            print("✨ All movies already have OTT data!")
            cursor.close()
            conn.close()
            return

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ Query error: {str(e)}")
        cursor.close()
        conn.close()
        sys.exit(1)

    # Process each movie
    for i, movie in enumerate(movies, 1):
        print(f"\n[{i}/{stats['total']}]", end=" ")

        try:
            process_movie(cursor, movie)
            conn.commit()

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"   ❌ Error: {str(e)}")
            stats['errors'] += 1
            conn.rollback()
            continue

        time.sleep(0.3)

    # Print summary

    print("\n" + "="*60)
    print("📊 SUMMARY")
    print("="*60)
    print(f"Total movies processed: {stats['total']}")
    print(f"✅ Success: {stats['success']}")
    print(f"⚠️  No data: {stats['no_data']}")
    print(f"❌ Errors: {stats['errors']}")
    print(f"📺 Total OTT links added: {stats['links_added']}")

    print("="*60)
    print(f"Completed at: {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}")
    print("="*60)

    cursor.close()
    conn.close()
    print("\n✨ Done!")

```

***

## **🔍 PYTHON INDENTATION RULES**

```python

def function():          # No indent
    code_here           # 4 spaces



    if condition:       # 4 spaces
        code_here       # 8 spaces

        if nested:      # 8 spaces
            code_here   # 12 spaces
            return      # 12 spaces (same level as code above)

    more_code          # 4 spaces (back to function level)
```

***

## **✅ QUICK FIX**

**Use a code editor with Python support:**
- VS Code with Python extension
- PyCharm

- Sublime Text with Python package

They'll show you indentation errors immediately!

***

**BABE! Fix the indentation and run again! 🚀**

The `return` must be indented **at the same level** as the `print` statement above it

# from dotenv import load_dotenv
import os

import sys
import time
import requests
import psycopg2
from psycopg2.extras import RealDictCursor
from datetime import datetime

# Load environment variables
load_dotenv()  # Loads .env by default

# Get variables with fallback
DATABASE_URL = os.getenv('DATABASE_URL', 'postgresql://tfiverse:newpassword123@localh
TMDB_API_KEY = os.getenv('TMDB_API_KEY', 'ba5dc12f58f09088d036049c565c2fe9')

# Configuration
TMDB_BASE_URL = 'https://api.themoviedb.org/3'

# Complete India OTT Platform Map

PLATFORM_MAP = {
    # === MAJOR STREAMING ===



    8: 'Netflix',
    119: 'Amazon Prime Video',
    122: 'Disney+ Hotstar',
    283: 'JioCinema',

    531: 'Zee5',
    619: 'Sony Liv',
    105: 'Voot',

    # === REGIONAL PLATFORMS ===
    582: 'Aha',
    635: 'Hoichoi',

    559: 'SunNXT',
    1771: 'ManoramaMax',
    1770: 'Eros Now',
    444: 'Shemaroo',
    2182: 'ShemarooMe',
    521: 'Lionsgate Play',
    471: 'ALTBalaji',

    # === FREE WITH ADS ===
    212: 'YouTube',
    613: 'MX Player',
    1793: 'Hungama Play',

    # === RENTAL/PURCHASE ===

    2: 'Apple TV',
    3: 'Google Play Movies',
    10: 'Amazon Video',
    68: 'Microsoft Store',
    350: 'Apple TV Plus',

    # === TELECOM BUNDLES ===

    423: 'Airtel Xstream',
    1890: 'Vi Movies and TV',

    # === SPECIALTY ===
    1899: 'EPIC ON',
    257: 'Docubay',
    677: 'CuriosityStream',
    1771: 'FanCode',

    2100: 'Gaana',
    175: 'Kidoodle.TV',
}

# Statistics
stats = {

    'total': 0,
    'success': 0,
    'no_data': 0,
    'errors': 0,
    'links_added': 0
}



def get_platform_name(provider_id):
    """Get platform name from ID with fallback"""
    name = PLATFORM_MAP.get(provider_id)
    if not name:

        # Log unknown platforms
        print(f"   ⚠️  Unknown platform ID: {provider_id}")
        name = f'Platform_{provider_id}'
    return name

def fetch_ott_from_tmdb(tmdb_id, title):
    """Fetch OTT availability from TMDB Watch Providers API"""

    try:
        url = f"{TMDB_BASE_URL}/movie/{tmdb_id}/watch/providers"
        params = {'api_key': TMDB_API_KEY}

        response = requests.get(url, params=params, timeout=10)
        response.raise_for_status()

        data = response.json()

        # Check for India region data
        if 'results' not in data:

            return None

        if 'IN' not in data['results']:
            return None

        india_data = data['results']['IN']
        ott_links = []

        # Get main watch link
        main_link = india_data.get('link', '')

        # Extract subscription platforms
        if 'flatrate' in india_data:
            for provider in india_data['flatrate']:
                provider_id = provider.get('provider_id')

                platform_name = get_platform_name(provider_id)

                ott_links.append({
                    'platform': platform_name,
                    'url': main_link,
                    'type': 'subscription',
                    'provider_id': provider_id

                })

        # Extract rental options
        if 'rent' in india_data:
            for provider in india_data['rent']:
                provider_id = provider.get('provider_id')
                platform_name = get_platform_name(provider_id)

                ott_links.append({



                    'platform': platform_name,
                    'url': main_link,
                    'type': 'rent',
                    'provider_id': provider_id

                })

        # Extract buy options
        if 'buy' in india_data:
            for provider in india_data['buy']:
                provider_id = provider.get('provider_id')
                platform_name = get_platform_name(provider_id)

                ott_links.append({
                    'platform': platform_name,
                    'url': main_link,
                    'type': 'buy',
                    'provider_id': provider_id
                })

        return ott_links if ott_links else None

    except requests.RequestException as e:
        print(f"   ❌ API Error: {str(e)}")
        return None
    except Exception as e:

        print(f"   ❌ Error: {str(e)}")
        return None

def save_ott_links(cursor, movie_id, ott_links):
    """Save OTT links to database"""

    saved_count = 0

    for link in ott_links:
        try:
            cursor.execute("""
                INSERT INTO movie_ott_links (
                    movie_id, platform, url, type, region, 

                    is_available, created_at, updated_at
                )
                VALUES (%s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s)
                ON CONFLICT (movie_id, platform, type) 
                DO UPDATE SET
                    url = EXCLUDED.url,
                    is_available = true,

                    updated_at = EXCLUDED.updated_at
            """, (
                movie_id,
                link['platform'],
                link['url'],
                link['type'],
                'IN',

                True,
                datetime.now(),



                datetime.now()
            ))
            saved_count += 1

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"   ⚠️  DB Error for {link['platform']}: {str(e)}")
            continue

    return saved_count

def process_movie(cursor, movie):
    """Process a single movie"""

    movie_id = movie['id']
    tmdb_id = movie['tmdb_id']
    title = movie['title']

    year = movie.get('year', 'N/A')

    print(f"\n🎬 Processing: {title} ({year})")
    print(f"   TMDB ID: {tmdb_id}, DB ID: {movie_id}")

    # Fetch OTT data
    ott_links = fetch_ott_from_tmdb(tmdb_id, title)

    if not ott_links:
        print(f"   ⚠️  No OTT data available")
        stats['no_data'] += 1
        return False

    # Save to database

    saved_count = save_ott_links(cursor, movie_id, ott_links)

    if saved_count > 0:
        print(f"   ✅ Added {saved_count} OTT link(s)")
        for link in ott_links:
            print(f"      • {link['platform']} ({link['type']})")

        stats['success'] += 1

        stats['links_added'] += saved_count
        return True
    else:
        print(f"   ⚠️  No links saved")
        stats['no_data'] += 1
        return False

def main():
    """Main execution"""

    print("="*60)
    print("🎬 TFIVerse OTT Links Fetcher")

    print("="*60)
    print(f"Started at: {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}\n")



    # Connect to database
    try:
        conn = psycopg2.connect(DATABASE_URL, cursor_factory=RealDictCursor)

        cursor = conn.cursor()
        print("✅ Database connected\n")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ Database connection failed: {str(e)}")
        sys.exit(1)

    # Get movies without OTT links

    try:
        cursor.execute("""
            SELECT m.id, m.tmdb_id, m.title, m.year
            FROM movies m
            WHERE m.tmdb_id IS NOT NULL
            AND NOT EXISTS (
                SELECT 1 FROM movie_ott_links ott 

                WHERE ott.movie_id = m.id
            )
            ORDER BY m.release_date DESC NULLS LAST
            LIMIT 100
        """)

        movies = cursor.fetchall()

        stats['total'] = len(movies)

        print(f"📊 Found {stats['total']} movies to process\n")

        if stats['total'] == 0:
            print("✨ All movies already have OTT data!")
            cursor.close()

            conn.close()
            return

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ Query error: {str(e)}")
        cursor.close()
        conn.close()
        sys.exit(1)

    # Process each movie
    for i, movie in enumerate(movies, 1):
        print(f"\n[{i}/{stats['total']}]", end=" ")

        try:
            process_movie(cursor, movie)

            conn.commit()

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"   ❌ Error: {str(e)}")
            stats['errors'] += 1
            conn.rollback()
            continue

        time.sleep(0.3)



    # Print summary
    print("\n" + "="*60)
    print("📊 SUMMARY")

    print("="*60)
    print(f"Total movies processed: {stats['total']}")
    print(f"✅ Success: {stats['success']}")
    print(f"⚠️  No data: {stats['no_data']}")
    print(f"❌ Errors: {stats['errors']}")
    print(f"📺 Total OTT links added: {stats['links_added']}")
    print("="*60)

    print(f"Completed at: {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}")
    print("="*60)

    cursor.close()
    conn.close()
    print("\n✨ Done!")

        return None
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   ❌ Error: {str(e)}")
        return None

def save_ott_links(cursor, movie_id, ott_links):
    """Save OTT links to database"""

    saved_count = 0

    for link in ott_links:

        try:
            cursor.execute("""
                INSERT INTO movie_ott_links (
                    movie_id, platform, url, type, region, 
                    is_available, created_at, updated_at
                )
                VALUES (%s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s)
                ON CONFLICT (movie_id, platform, type) 

                DO UPDATE SET

                    updated_at = EXCLUDED.updated_at
            """, (
                movie_id,
                link['platform'],

                link['url'],
                link['type'],
                'IN',
                True,
                datetime.now(),
                datetime.now()
            ))

            saved_count += 1



        except Exception as e:
            print(f"   ⚠️  DB Error for {link['platform']}: {str(e)}")
            continue

    return saved_count

def process_movie(cursor, movie):
    """Process a single movie"""

    movie_id = movie['id']
    tmdb_id = movie['tmdb_id']

    title = movie['title']
    year = movie.get('year', 'N/A')

    print(f"\n🎬 Processing: {title} ({year})")
    print(f"   TMDB ID: {tmdb_id}, DB ID: {movie_id}")

    ott_links = fetch_ott_from_tmdb(tmdb_id, title)

    if not ott_links:
        print(f"   ⚠️  No OTT data available")
        stats['no_data'] += 1
        return False

    saved_count = save_ott_links(cursor, movie_id, ott_links)

    if saved_count > 0:
        print(f"   ✅ Added {saved_count} OTT link(s)")
        for link in ott_links:
            print(f"      • {link['platform']} ({link['type']})")

        stats['success'] += 1

        stats['links_added'] += saved_count
        return True
    else:
        print(f"   ⚠️  No links saved")
        stats['no_data'] += 1
        return False

def main():

    """Main execution"""

    print("="*60)
    print("🎬 TFIVerse OTT Links Fetcher")
    print("="*60)
    print(f"Started at: {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}\n")

    try:
        conn = psycopg2.connect(DATABASE_URL, cursor_factory=RealDictCursor)
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        print("✅ Database connected\n")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ Database connection failed: {str(e)}")
        sys.exit(1)

    try:



        cursor.execute("""
            SELECT m.id, m.tmdb_id, m.title, m.year
            FROM movies m
            WHERE m.tmdb_id IS NOT NULL

            AND NOT EXISTS (
                SELECT 1 FROM movie_ott_links ott 
                WHERE ott.movie_id = m.id
            )
            ORDER BY m.release_date DESC NULLS LAST
            LIMIT 100
        """)

        movies = cursor.fetchall()
        stats['total'] = len(movies)

        print(f"📊 Found {stats['total']} movies to process\n")

        if stats['total'] == 0:

            print("✨ All movies already have OTT data!")
            cursor.close()
            conn.close()
            return

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ Query error: {str(e)}")
        cursor.close()
        conn.close()
        sys.exit(1)

    for i, movie in enumerate(movies, 1):
        print(f"\n[{i}/{stats['total']}]", end=" ")

        try:
            process_movie(cursor, movie)
            conn.commit()

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"   ❌ Error: {str(e)}")
            stats['errors'] += 1
            conn.rollback()

            continue

        time.sleep(0.3)

    print("\n" + "="*60)
    print("📊 SUMMARY")
    print("="*60)

    print(f"Total movies processed: {stats['total']}")
    print(f"✅ Success: {stats['success']}")
    print(f"⚠️  No data: {stats['no_data']}")
    print(f"❌ Errors: {stats['errors']}")
    print(f"📺 Total OTT links added: {stats['links_added']}")
    print("="*60)
    print(f"Completed at: {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}")

    print("="*60)



    cursor.close()
    conn.close()
    print("\n✨ Done!")

# EXECUTION BLOCK - THIS WAS MISSING!
# ============================================================================

if __name__ == "__main__":
    try:
        main()

    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        print("\n\n⚠️  Interrupted by user")
        sys.exit(0)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"\n\n💥 Fatal error: {str(e)}")
        sys.exit(1)
```

- Only runs when script is executed directly
- Won't run if imported as a module

```python
try:
    main()

```
- Calls your main function

```python
except KeyboardInterrupt:
```
- Handles Ctrl+C gracefully

```python
except Exception as e:
```
- Catches any other errors and shows them

## **🔄 RE-RUN TO UPDATE PLATFORM NAMES**



Your database now has `Platform_232` etc. Let's update them with proper names:

**Create: `scripts/update-platform-names.py`**

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""Update platform names in database"""

import psycopg2
from dotenv import load_dotenv

import os

load_dotenv()
DATABASE_URL = os.getenv('DATABASE_URL')

# Platform name mappings
UPDATES = {

    'Platform_232': 'JioCinema',
    'Platform_614': 'Sun NXT',
    'Platform_309': 'Sun NXT',
    'Platform_2059': 'Tata Play Binge',
}

conn = psycopg2.connect(DATABASE_URL)

cursor = conn.cursor()

print("🔄 Updating platform names...\n")

for old_name, new_name in UPDATES.items():
    cursor.execute("""
        UPDATE movie_ott_links

        SET platform = %s
        WHERE platform = %s
    """, (new_name, old_name))

    count = cursor.rowcount
    if count > 0:
        print(f"✅ Updated {count} records: {old_name} → {new_name}")

conn.commit()
cursor.close()
conn.close()

print("\n✨ Done!")
```

## **🔧 UPDATE YOUR SCRIPT TO STORE BOTH**

**Modified `save_ott_links` function:**

```python

def save_ott_links(cursor, movie_id, ott_links, movie_title, tmdb_id):
    """Save OTT links to database with direct URLs"""

    saved_count = 0

    for link in ott_links:
        try:

            platform = link['platform']
            tmdb_url = link['url']

            # Build direct URL based on platform
            direct_url = build_direct_url(platform, movie_title, tmdb_id)

            cursor.execute("""

                INSERT INTO movie_ott_links (
                    movie_id, platform, url, type, region, 
                    is_available, created_at, updated_at
                )
                VALUES (%s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s)
                ON CONFLICT (movie_id, platform, type) 
                DO UPDATE SET
                    url = EXCLUDED.url,

                    is_available = true,
                    updated_at = EXCLUDED.updated_at
            """, (
                movie_id,
                platform,
                direct_url,  # ← Use direct URL instead of TMDB redirect
                link['type'],

                'IN',
                True,
                datetime.now(),
                datetime.now()
            ))
            saved_count += 1

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"   ⚠️  DB Error for {link['platform']}: {str(e)}")



            continue

    return saved_count

def build_direct_url(platform, movie_title, tmdb_id):
    """Build direct platform URLs"""

    # URL encode movie title
    import urllib.parse
    encoded_title = urllib.parse.quote(movie_title)

    platform_urls = {
        'Netflix': f'https://www.netflix.com/in/title/{tmdb_id}',  # May not work
        'Amazon Prime Video': f'https://www.primevideo.com/search?phrase={encoded_t
        'Disney+ Hotstar': f'https://www.hotstar.com/in/search?q={encoded_title}',
        'Aha': f'https://www.aha.video/search?q={encoded_title}',
        'Zee5': f'https://www.zee5.com/global/search?q={encoded_title}',

        'Sony Liv': f'https://www.sonyliv.com/search/{encoded_title}',
        'Sun NXT': f'https://www.sunnxt.com/search/{encoded_title}',
        'JioCinema': f'https://www.jiocinema.com/search/{encoded_title}',
        'YouTube': f'https://www.youtube.com/results?search_query={encoded_title}',
        'Google Play Movies': f'https://play.google.com/store/search?q={encoded_titl
        'Apple TV': f'https://tv.apple.com/in/search?term={encoded_title}',
    }

    # Fallback to TMDB universal link
    return platform_urls.get(platform, f'https://www.themoviedb.org/movie/{tmdb_id}
```

## **🎯 SOLUTION: Use JustWatch API (Best Option)**

JustWatch provides **actual direct URLs** to streaming platforms!

***

## **🔧 UPDATED SCRIPT WITH DIRECT URLs**

Replace your `fetch_ott_from_tmdb` function with this **JustWatch version**:



```python
import requests
import json

def fetch_ott_from_justwatch(tmdb_id, title, year=None):
    """Fetch OTT links with DIRECT URLs from JustWatch"""

    try:
        # JustWatch GraphQL API (India region)
        url = "https://apis.justwatch.com/graphql"

        # Search query
        query = """
        query GetSearchTitles($searchTitlesFilter: TitleFilter!, $country: Country!,
            popularTitles(
                filter: $searchTitlesFilter
                country: $country

                first: 5
            ) {
                edges {
                    node {
                        id
                        objectId
                        objectType

                        content(country: $country, language: $language) {
                            title
                            originalReleaseYear
                            externalIds {
                                tmdbId
                            }
                        }

                        offers(country: $country, platform: WEB) {
                            monetizationType
                            presentationType
                            package {
                                id
                                packageId
                                clearName
                            }

                            standardWebURL
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        """

        variables = {
            "searchTitlesFilter": {
                "searchQuery": title
            },
            "country": "IN",
            "language": "en"

        }



        headers = {
            'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        }

        response = requests.post(
            url,
            json={"query": query, "variables": variables},
            headers=headers,
            timeout=10
        )

        if response.status_code != 200:
            return None

        data = response.json()

        if 'data' not in data or 'popularTitles' not in data['data']:
            return None

        # Find matching movie by TMDB ID
        movie_data = None
        for edge in data['data']['popularTitles']['edges']:
            node = edge['node']
            external_ids = node.get('content', {}).get('externalIds', {})

            if external_ids.get('tmdbId') == str(tmdb_id):
                movie_data = node
                break

        if not movie_data or 'offers' not in movie_data:
            return None

        ott_links = []

        # Platform ID to name mapping
        platform_names = {
            8: 'Netflix',
            9: 'Amazon Prime Video',
            122: 'Disney+ Hotstar',
            283: 'JioCinema',

            531: 'Zee5',
            619: 'Sony Liv',
            105: 'Voot',
            582: 'Aha',
            614: 'Sun NXT',
            # Add more as needed
        }

        for offer in movie_data['offers']:
            package = offer.get('package', {})
            package_id = package.get('packageId')
            platform_name = package.get('clearName', platform_names.get(package_id, 

            direct_url = offer.get('standardWebURL')

            monetization = offer.get('monetizationType', '').lower()



            if direct_url:
                ott_links.append({
                    'platform': platform_name,
                    'url': direct_url,  # ← DIRECT URL!

                    'type': 'subscription' if monetization == 'flatrate' else monetiz
                    'provider_id': package_id
                })

        return ott_links if ott_links else None

    except Exception as e:

        print(f"   ❌ JustWatch Error: {str(e)}")
        return None
```

***

## **⚡ EVEN BETTER: Scrape from TMDB Watch Page**

Since JustWatch API can be tricky, here's a **web scraping solution** that gets direc

```python
import requests
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
import re

def fetch_direct_ott_urls(tmdb_id, title):
    """Scrape direct URLs from TMDB watch page"""

    try:
        # TMDB watch page
        url = f"https://www.themoviedb.org/movie/{tmdb_id}/watch?locale=IN"

        headers = {
            'User-Agent': 'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.
        }

        response = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=10)

        if response.status_code != 200:

            return None

        soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser')

        ott_links = []

        # Find all streaming options

        stream_sections = soup.find_all('div', {'class': 'ott_provider'})

        for section in stream_sections:
            # Get platform name
            platform_elem = section.find('img', {'alt': True})
            if not platform_elem:
                continue

            platform_name = platform_elem.get('alt', '')



            # Get direct URL
            link_elem = section.find('a', {'href': True})
            if not link_elem:

                continue

            direct_url = link_elem.get('href', '')

            # Determine type (subscription/rent/buy)
            section_type = section.find_parent('div', {'class': re.compile('.*type.*
            if section_type:

                type_text = section_type.get('class', [''])[0]
                if 'flatrate' in type_text:
                    link_type = 'subscription'
                elif 'rent' in type_text:
                    link_type = 'rent'
                elif 'buy' in type_text:
                    link_type = 'buy'

                else:
                    link_type = 'subscription'
            else:
                link_type = 'subscription'

            if direct_url and platform_name:
                ott_links.append({

                    'platform': platform_name,
                    'url': direct_url,
                    'type': link_type,
                    'provider_id': None
                })

        return ott_links if ott_links else None

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   ❌ Scraping Error: {str(e)}")
        return None
```

***

## **🎯 BEST SOLUTION: Use Streaming Availability API**

This is a **paid but reliable API** that gives direct URLs:

```python
def fetch_from_streaming_availability(tmdb_id, title):
    """Use Streaming Availability API for direct URLs"""

    # Get your API key from: https://www.movieofthenight.com/about/api
    STREAMING_API_KEY = os.getenv('STREAMING_API_KEY')

    try:
        url = f"https://streaming-availability.p.rapidapi.com/get"

        querystring = {
            "tmdb_id": f"movie/{tmdb_id}",



            "output_language": "en",
            "country": "in"
        }

        headers = {
            "X-RapidAPI-Key": STREAMING_API_KEY,
            "X-RapidAPI-Host": "streaming-availability.p.rapidapi.com"
        }

        response = requests.get(url, headers=headers, params=querystring, timeout=1

        if response.status_code != 200:
            return None

        data = response.json()

        if 'streamingInfo' not in data or 'in' not in data['streamingInfo']:
            return None

        india_streaming = data['streamingInfo']['in']
        ott_links = []

        for service_id, service_data in india_streaming.items():
            for offer in service_data:
                ott_links.append({

                    'platform': service_id.capitalize(),
                    'url': offer.get('link', ''),  # ← Direct URL!
                    'type': offer.get('type', 'subscription'),
                    'provider_id': service_id
                })

        return ott_links if ott_links else None

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   ❌ Streaming API Error: {str(e)}")
        return None
```

***

## **💡 HYBRID APPROACH (BEST FOR YOU)**

Combine multiple methods:

```python
def fetch_ott_with_direct_urls(tmdb_id, title, year=None):
    """

    Fetch OTT links with direct URLs
    Tries multiple methods in order of reliability
    """

    # Method 1: Try Streaming Availability API (if you have key)
    if os.getenv('STREAMING_API_KEY'):
        links = fetch_from_streaming_availability(tmdb_id, title)

        if links:
            print(f"   📡 Got direct URLs from Streaming API")



            return links

    # Method 2: Try JustWatch
    links = fetch_ott_from_justwatch(tmdb_id, title, year)

    if links:
        print(f"   📡 Got URLs from JustWatch")
        return links

    # Method 3: Fallback to TMDB with manual URL construction
    links = fetch_ott_from_tmdb(tmdb_id, title)
    if links:

        print(f"   📡 Using TMDB URLs (will build direct links)")
        # Build direct URLs manually
        return build_direct_urls(links, tmdb_id, title)

    return None

def build_direct_urls(tmdb_links, tmdb_id, title):
    """Build direct platform URLs from TMDB data"""

    import urllib.parse
    encoded_title = urllib.parse.quote(title)

    for link in tmdb_links:

        platform = link['platform']

        # Known direct URL patterns
        if 'Netflix' in platform:
            link['url'] = f'https://www.netflix.com/in/title/{tmdb_id}'
        elif 'Prime' in platform or 'Amazon' in platform:
            link['url'] = f'https://www.primevideo.com/search?phrase={encoded_title}

        elif 'Hotstar' in platform or 'Disney' in platform:
            link['url'] = f'https://www.hotstar.com/in/search?q={encoded_title}'
        elif 'Aha' in platform:
            link['url'] = f'https://www.aha.video/search?q={encoded_title}'
        elif 'Zee5' in platform:
            link['url'] = f'https://www.zee5.com/global/search?q={encoded_title}'
        elif 'Sony' in platform:
            link['url'] = f'https://www.sonyliv.com/search/{encoded_title}'

        elif 'Sun' in platform:
            link['url'] = f'https://www.sunnxt.com/search/{encoded_title}'
        elif 'Jio' in platform:
            link['url'] = f'https://www.jiocinema.com/search/{encoded_title}'
        # Keep TMDB URL as fallback

    return tmdb_links

```

## **🚀 UPDATED COMPLETE SCRIPT**

Replace the `fetch_ott_from_tmdb` call in your `process_movie` function:

```python
def process_movie(cursor, movie):
    """Process a single movie"""

    movie_id = movie['id']
    tmdb_id = movie['tmdb_id']
    title = movie['title']
    year = movie.get('year', None)

    print(f"\n🎬 Processing: {title} ({year})")
    print(f"   TMDB ID: {tmdb_id}, DB ID: {movie_id}")

    # Fetch OTT data with direct URLs
    ott_links = fetch_ott_with_direct_urls(tmdb_id, title, year)

    if not ott_links:
        print(f"   ⚠️  No OTT data available")
        stats['no_data'] += 1

        return False

    # Save to database
    saved_count = save_ott_links(cursor, movie_id, ott_links)

    if saved_count > 0:
        print(f"   ✅ Added {saved_count} OTT link(s) with DIRECT URLs")

        for link in ott_links:
            print(f"      • {link['platform']}: {link['url'][:50]}...")

        stats['success'] += 1
        stats['links_added'] += saved_count
        return True
    else:
        print(f"   ⚠️  No links saved")

        stats['no_data'] += 1
        return False
```

- `https://www.hotstar.com/in/movies/movie-name/1234567890`

# **🎯 COMPLETE OTT URL METHODS COMPARISON**

***

## **1️⃣ TMDB Watch Providers API (CURRENT - FREE)**

### **What You Get:**
- Redirect URLs: `https://www.themoviedb.org/movie/12345/watch?locale=IN`
- Platform names (Netflix, Prime, etc.)
- Type (subscription/rent/buy)

### **Pros:**
✅ **100% FREE**  

✅ Official API  
✅ No rate limits (40 req/10 sec)  
✅ Always updated  
✅ Legal & reliable  

### **Cons:**
❌ **NOT direct platform URLs**  
❌ Requires manual URL construction  
❌ Netflix URLs hard to get  

### **Cost:** FREE ✅

***

## **2️⃣ JustWatch API (FREE but Unofficial)**

### **What You Get:**
- **Direct URLs!** ✅
- `https://www.netflix.com/in/title/81754779`
- Full metadata
- Multiple regions

### **Pros:**
✅ **FREE (unofficial)**  
✅ **Direct URLs!**  
✅ Best data quality  
✅ All platforms covered  

### **Cons:**

❌ No official API (GraphQL endpoint)  
❌ May break if they change structure  
❌ Rate limiting unknown  
❌ Terms of service unclear  

### **Cost:** FREE (but risky) ⚠️

### **Code:**
```python



pip install justwatch
```

***

## **3️⃣ Streaming Availability API (PAID)**

### **What You Get:**
- **Direct URLs** ✅
- Netflix, Prime, Hotstar, etc.
- High reliability

- Official API

### **Pros:**
✅ **Direct URLs guaranteed**  
✅ Official & reliable  
✅ Good documentation  
✅ Multi-region support  

### **Cons:**

❌ Rate limits on free tier  

### **Pricing:**
- **Free tier:** 100 requests/day

- **Basic:** $10/month (10,000 req/month)
- **Pro:** $50/month (100,000 req/month)
