### **My Recommendation:**

```python
def get_ott_urls(tmdb_id, title, imdb_id=None):
    """
    Hybrid approach:
    1. Get platforms from TMDB (free)
    2. Construct direct URLs where possible
    3. Fallback to search URLs

    """

    # Step 1: Get platforms from TMDB (FREE)
    platforms = fetch_from_tmdb(tmdb_id)

    # Step 2: Build direct URLs
    direct_urls = []

    for platform in platforms:
        if platform == 'Netflix':
            # Try to get Netflix ID from IMDB
            if imdb_id:
                netflix_id = lookup_netflix_id(imdb_id)
                if netflix_id:

                    url = f'https://www.netflix.com/in/title/{netflix_id}'
                else:



                    url = f'https://www.netflix.com/search?q={title}'
            else:
                url = f'https://www.netflix.com/search?q={title}'

        elif platform == 'Amazon Prime Video':
            # Prime uses ASIN, hard to get
            url = f'https://www.primevideo.com/search?phrase={title}'

        elif platform == 'Disney+ Hotstar':
            url = f'https://www.hotstar.com/in/search?q={title}'

        elif platform == 'Aha':
            url = f'https://www.aha.video/search?q={title}'

        # Add more platforms...

        direct_urls.append({
            'platform': platform,

            'url': url,
            'type': 'subscription'
        })

    return direct_urls
```

# **🏆 MY RECOMMENDATION: BEST FREE METHOD**

## **HYBRID TMDB + Manual Construction**

```python

def fetch_ott_urls_free(tmdb_id, title, year=None):
    """
    100% FREE method - Best balance of quality and reliability
    """

    # Step 1: Get platforms from TMDB API (FREE)
    tmdb_data = fetch_from_tmdb_api(tmdb_id)

    if not tmdb_data:
        return None

    # Step 2: Build direct URLs
    import urllib.parse
    encoded_title = urllib.parse.quote(title)

    ott_links = []

    for platform_data in tmdb_data:
        platform = platform_data['platform']

        # Platform-specific URL patterns
        url_patterns = {

            'Netflix': f'https://www.netflix.com/search?q={encoded_title}',
            'Amazon Prime Video': f'https://www.primevideo.com/search?phrase={encod



            'Disney+ Hotstar': f'https://www.hotstar.com/in/search?q={encoded_title}'
            'Aha': f'https://www.aha.video/search?q={encoded_title}',
            'Zee5': f'https://www.zee5.com/global/search?q={encoded_title}',
            'Sony Liv': f'https://www.sonyliv.com/search?q={encoded_title}',

            'Sun NXT': f'https://www.sunnxt.com/search/{encoded_title}',
            'JioCinema': f'https://www.jiocinema.com/search?q={encoded_title}',
            'Voot': f'https://www.voot.com/search?q={encoded_title}',
            'MX Player': f'https://www.mxplayer.in/search?q={encoded_title}',
            'YouTube': f'https://www.youtube.com/results?search_query={encoded_title}
            'Google Play Movies': f'https://play.google.com/store/search?q={encoded_
            'Apple TV': f'https://tv.apple.com/in/search?term={encoded_title}',

        }

        ott_links.append({
            'platform': platform,
            'url': url_patterns.get(platform, f'https://www.google.com/search?q={enc
            'type': platform_data['type']
        })

    return ott_links
```

## **📝 STEP 2: COMPLETE UPDATED SCRIPT**

**File: `scripts/fetch-ott-links-justwatch.py`**

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
OTT Links Fetcher using JustWatch API
Gets DIRECT platform URLs (Netflix, Prime, etc.)
"""

from dotenv import load_dotenv



import os
import sys
import time
import psycopg2

from psycopg2.extras import RealDictCursor
from datetime import datetime
from simplejustwatchapi.justwatch import search, details

# Load environment
load_dotenv()

DATABASE_URL = os.getenv('DATABASE_URL', 'postgresql://tfiverse:newpassword123@localh

# Platform mapping (JustWatch uses different names sometimes)
PLATFORM_MAPPING = {
    'Netflix': 'Netflix',
    'Amazon Prime Video': 'Amazon Prime Video',
    'Prime Video': 'Amazon Prime Video',

    'Disney Plus': 'Disney+ Hotstar',
    'Disney+': 'Disney+ Hotstar',
    'Hotstar': 'Disney+ Hotstar',
    'JioCinema': 'JioCinema',
    'Zee5': 'Zee5',
    'Sony Liv': 'Sony Liv',
    'SonyLIV': 'Sony Liv',

    'Voot': 'Voot',
    'Aha': 'Aha',
    'Sun Nxt': 'Sun NXT',
    'SunNXT': 'Sun NXT',
    'YouTube': 'YouTube',
    'Google Play Movies': 'Google Play Movies',
    'Apple TV': 'Apple TV',

    'MX Player': 'MX Player',
}

# Statistics
stats = {
    'total': 0,
    'success': 0,
    'no_data': 0,

    'errors': 0,
    'links_added': 0
}

def fetch_ott_from_justwatch(title, year=None):
    """Fetch OTT links with DIRECT URLs from JustWatch"""

    try:
        # Search for the movie in India
        results = search(
            title=title,
            country="IN",  # India
            language="en",

            count=5,
            best_only=True



        )

        if not results:
            return None

        # Find best match (first result usually correct)
        movie = None
        for result in results:
            # Match by year if available
            if year and result.release_year:
                if abs(result.release_year - year) <= 1:  # Allow 1 year difference

                    movie = result
                    break
            else:
                movie = result
                break

        if not movie:

            return None

        # Get offers (streaming availability)
        if not movie.offers:
            return None

        ott_links = []

        for offer in movie.offers:
            # Get platform name
            platform_name = offer.provider_name

            # Normalize platform name
            platform_name = PLATFORM_MAPPING.get(platform_name, platform_name)

            # Get direct URL
            direct_url = offer.url

            # Determine type
            if offer.monetization_type == 'FLATRATE':
                offer_type = 'subscription'
            elif offer.monetization_type == 'RENT':

                offer_type = 'rent'
            elif offer.monetization_type == 'BUY':
                offer_type = 'buy'
            else:
                offer_type = 'subscription'

            ott_links.append({

                'platform': platform_name,
                'url': direct_url,  # ← DIRECT URL!
                'type': offer_type,
                'quality': offer.presentation_type if hasattr(offer, 'presentation_ty
            })

        return ott_links if ott_links else None

    except Exception as e:



        print(f"   ❌ JustWatch Error: {str(e)}")
        return None

def save_ott_links(cursor, movie_id, ott_links):
    """Save OTT links to database"""

    saved_count = 0

    for link in ott_links:
        try:

            cursor.execute("""
                INSERT INTO movie_ott_links (
                    movie_id, platform, url, type, region, 
                    is_available, quality, created_at, updated_at
                )
                VALUES (%s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s)
                ON CONFLICT (movie_id, platform, type) 

                DO UPDATE SET
                    url = EXCLUDED.url,
                    is_available = true,
                    quality = EXCLUDED.quality,
                    updated_at = EXCLUDED.updated_at
            """, (
                movie_id,

                link['platform'],
                link['url'],
                link['type'],
                'IN',
                True,
                link.get('quality'),
                datetime.now(),

                datetime.now()
            ))
            saved_count += 1

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"   ⚠️  DB Error for {link['platform']}: {str(e)}")
            continue

    return saved_count

def process_movie(cursor, movie):
    """Process a single movie"""

    movie_id = movie['id']

    title = movie['title']
    year = movie.get('year')

    print(f"\n🎬 Processing: {title} ({year or 'N/A'})")
    print(f"   DB ID: {movie_id}")

    # Fetch OTT data from JustWatch

    ott_links = fetch_ott_from_justwatch(title, year)



    if not ott_links:
        print(f"   ⚠️  No OTT data available on JustWatch")
        stats['no_data'] += 1
        return False

    # Save to database
    saved_count = save_ott_links(cursor, movie_id, ott_links)

    if saved_count > 0:
        print(f"   ✅ Added {saved_count} DIRECT OTT link(s)")
        for link in ott_links:

            # Show first 60 chars of URL
            url_preview = link['url'][:60] + "..." if len(link['url']) > 60 else link[
            quality = f" [{link['quality']}]" if link.get('quality') else ""
            print(f"      • {link['platform']} ({link['type']}){quality}")
            print(f"        {url_preview}")

        stats['success'] += 1

        stats['links_added'] += saved_count
        return True
    else:
        print(f"   ⚠️  No links saved")
        stats['no_data'] += 1
        return False

def main():
    """Main execution"""

    print("="*70)
    print("🎬 TFIVerse OTT Links Fetcher (JustWatch - DIRECT URLs)")
    print("="*70)

    print(f"Started at: {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}\n")

    # Connect to database
    try:
        conn = psycopg2.connect(DATABASE_URL, cursor_factory=RealDictCursor)
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        print("✅ Database connected\n")
    except Exception as e:

        print(f"❌ Database connection failed: {str(e)}")
        sys.exit(1)

    # Get movies without OTT links
    try:
        cursor.execute("""
            SELECT m.id, m.title, m.year

            FROM movies m
            WHERE NOT EXISTS (
                SELECT 1 FROM movie_ott_links ott 
                WHERE ott.movie_id = m.id
            )
            ORDER BY m.release_date DESC NULLS LAST
            LIMIT 100

        """)



        movies = cursor.fetchall()
        stats['total'] = len(movies)

        print(f"📊 Found {stats['total']} movies to process\n")

        if stats['total'] == 0:
            print("✨ All movies already have OTT data!")
            cursor.close()
            conn.close()
            return

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ Query error: {str(e)}")
        cursor.close()
        conn.close()
        sys.exit(1)

    # Process each movie

    for i, movie in enumerate(movies, 1):
        print(f"\n[{i}/{stats['total']}]", end=" ")

        try:
            process_movie(cursor, movie)
            conn.commit()

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"   ❌ Error: {str(e)}")
            stats['errors'] += 1
            conn.rollback()
            continue

        # Rate limiting (be nice to JustWatch)

        time.sleep(1)  # 1 second delay between requests

    # Print summary
    print("\n" + "="*70)
    print("📊 SUMMARY")
    print("="*70)
    print(f"Total movies processed: {stats['total']}")
    print(f"✅ Success: {stats['success']}")

    print(f"⚠️  No data: {stats['no_data']}")
    print(f"❌ Errors: {stats['errors']}")
    print(f"📺 Total DIRECT OTT links added: {stats['links_added']}")
    print("="*70)
    print(f"Completed at: {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}")
    print("="*70)

    cursor.close()
    conn.close()
    print("\n✨ Done!")

if __name__ == "__main__":
    try:

        main()
    except KeyboardInterrupt:



        print("\n\n⚠️  Interrupted by user")
        sys.exit(0)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"\n\n💥 Fatal error: {str(e)}")

        sys.exit(1)
```

## **🔄 HYBRID APPROACH (BEST)**

Combine JustWatch + TMDB for best results:

```python
def fetch_ott_hybrid(title, year, tmdb_id):
    """Try JustWatch first, fallback to TMDB"""

    # Try JustWatch (direct URLs)
    links = fetch_ott_from_justwatch(title, year)

    if links:
        print(f"   📡 Got DIRECT URLs from JustWatch")



        return links

    # Fallback to TMDB (redirect URLs)
    links = fetch_ott_from_tmdb(tmdb_id)

    if links:
        print(f"   📡 Fallback to TMDB URLs")
        return links

    return None
```

## **🔧 FIXED SCRIPT - Correct JustWatch Attributes**

Replace the `fetch_ott_from_justwatch` function:



```python
def fetch_ott_from_justwatch(title, year=None):
    """Fetch OTT links with DIRECT URLs from JustWatch"""

    try:
        # Search for the movie in India
        results = search(
            title=title,
            country="IN",  # India
            language="en",

            count=5,
            best_only=True
        )

        if not results:
            return None

        # Find best match (first result usually correct)
        movie = None
        for result in results:
            # Match by year if available
            if year and hasattr(result, 'release_year') and result.release_year:
                if abs(result.release_year - year) <= 1:
                    movie = result

                    break
            else:
                movie = result
                break

        if not movie:
            return None

        # Get offers (streaming availability)
        if not hasattr(movie, 'offers') or not movie.offers:
            return None

        ott_links = []

        for offer in movie.offers:

            try:
                # DEBUG: Print offer attributes
                # print(f"   DEBUG: Offer attributes: {dir(offer)}")

                # Get platform name (correct attribute)
                platform_name = offer.package.name if hasattr(offer, 'package') else 

                # Normalize platform name
                platform_name = PLATFORM_MAPPING.get(platform_name, platform_name)

                # Get direct URL (correct attribute)
                direct_url = offer.url if hasattr(offer, 'url') else None

                if not direct_url:

                    continue



                # Determine type (correct attribute)
                monetization = offer.monetization_type if hasattr(offer, 'monetizati

                if monetization == 'FLATRATE':

                    offer_type = 'subscription'
                elif monetization == 'RENT':
                    offer_type = 'rent'
                elif monetization == 'BUY':
                    offer_type = 'buy'
                else:
                    offer_type = 'subscription'

                # Get quality
                quality = offer.presentation_type if hasattr(offer, 'presentation_typ

                ott_links.append({
                    'platform': platform_name,
                    'url': direct_url,

                    'type': offer_type,
                    'quality': quality
                })

            except Exception as e:
                print(f"   ⚠️  Error processing offer: {str(e)}")
                continue

        return ott_links if ott_links else None

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   ❌ JustWatch Error: {str(e)}")
        import traceback
        traceback.print_exc()  # Print full error for debugging

        return None
```

## **📝 COMPLETE FIXED SCRIPT**

**File: `scripts/fetch-ott-links-justwatch.py`** (Updated)

```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
OTT Links Fetcher using JustWatch API
Gets DIRECT platform URLs (Netflix, Prime, etc.)
"""

from dotenv import load_dotenv
import os
import sys
import time
import psycopg2
from psycopg2.extras import RealDictCursor

from datetime import datetime
from simplejustwatchapi.justwatch import search



# Load environment
load_dotenv()

DATABASE_URL = os.getenv('DATABASE_URL', 'postgresql://tfiverse:newpassword123@localh

# Platform mapping
PLATFORM_MAPPING = {
    'Netflix': 'Netflix',
    'Amazon Prime Video': 'Amazon Prime Video',
    'Prime Video': 'Amazon Prime Video',

    'Disney Plus': 'Disney+ Hotstar',
    'Disney+': 'Disney+ Hotstar',
    'Hotstar': 'Disney+ Hotstar',
    'JioCinema': 'JioCinema',
    'Zee5': 'Zee5',
    'Sony Liv': 'Sony Liv',
    'SonyLIV': 'Sony Liv',

    'Voot': 'Voot',
    'Aha': 'Aha',
    'Sun Nxt': 'Sun NXT',
    'SunNXT': 'Sun NXT',
    'YouTube': 'YouTube',
    'Google Play Movies': 'Google Play Movies',
    'Apple TV': 'Apple TV',

    'MX Player': 'MX Player',
}

# Statistics
stats = {
    'total': 0,
    'success': 0,

    'no_data': 0,
    'errors': 0,
    'links_added': 0
}

def fetch_ott_from_justwatch(title, year=None):
    """Fetch OTT links with DIRECT URLs from JustWatch"""

    try:
        print(f"   🔍 Searching JustWatch for: {title}")

        # Search for the movie in India
        results = search(
            title=title,

            country="IN",
            language="en",
            count=5,
            best_only=True
        )

        if not results:

            print(f"   ⚠️  No results from JustWatch")
            return None



        print(f"   📊 Found {len(results)} results")

        # Find best match

        movie = None
        for idx, result in enumerate(results):
            print(f"   → Result {idx+1}: {result.title} ({getattr(result, 'release_yea

            # Match by year if available
            if year and hasattr(result, 'release_year') and result.release_year:
                if abs(result.release_year - year) <= 1:

                    movie = result
                    print(f"   ✓ Matched by year!")
                    break
            elif idx == 0:  # First result as fallback
                movie = result
                print(f"   ✓ Using first result")
                break

        if not movie:
            print(f"   ⚠️  No suitable match found")
            return None

        # Get offers
        if not hasattr(movie, 'offers') or not movie.offers:

            print(f"   ⚠️  No offers available")
            return None

        print(f"   📺 Found {len(movie.offers)} offers")

        ott_links = []

        for idx, offer in enumerate(movie.offers):
            try:
                # Get platform name from package
                if hasattr(offer, 'package') and offer.package:
                    platform_name = offer.package.name
                else:
                    print(f"   ⚠️  Offer {idx+1}: No package info")
                    continue

                # Get URL
                if hasattr(offer, 'url') and offer.url:
                    direct_url = offer.url
                else:
                    print(f"   ⚠️  Offer {idx+1}: No URL")
                    continue

                # Normalize platform name
                platform_name = PLATFORM_MAPPING.get(platform_name, platform_name)

                # Get monetization type
                monetization = getattr(offer, 'monetization_type', 'FLATRATE')

                if monetization == 'FLATRATE':
                    offer_type = 'subscription'



                elif monetization == 'RENT':
                    offer_type = 'rent'
                elif monetization == 'BUY':
                    offer_type = 'buy'

                else:
                    offer_type = 'subscription'

                # Get quality
                quality = getattr(offer, 'presentation_type', None)

                ott_links.append({

                    'platform': platform_name,
                    'url': direct_url,
                    'type': offer_type,
                    'quality': quality
                })

                print(f"   ✓ {platform_name} ({offer_type})")

            except Exception as e:
                print(f"   ⚠️  Error processing offer {idx+1}: {str(e)}")
                continue

        return ott_links if ott_links else None

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"   ❌ JustWatch Error: {str(e)}")
        return None

def save_ott_links(cursor, movie_id, ott_links):
    """Save OTT links to database"""

    saved_count = 0

    for link in ott_links:
        try:
            cursor.execute("""
                INSERT INTO movie_ott_links (
                    movie_id, platform, url, type, region, 

                    is_available, quality, created_at, updated_at
                )
                VALUES (%s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s, %s)
                ON CONFLICT (movie_id, platform, type) 
                DO UPDATE SET
                    url = EXCLUDED.url,
                    is_available = true,

                    quality = EXCLUDED.quality,
                    updated_at = EXCLUDED.updated_at
            """, (
                movie_id,
                link['platform'],
                link['url'],
                link['type'],

                'IN',
                True,



                link.get('quality'),
                datetime.now(),
                datetime.now()
            ))

            saved_count += 1

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"   ⚠️  DB Error for {link['platform']}: {str(e)}")
            continue

    return saved_count

def process_movie(cursor, movie):
    """Process a single movie"""

    movie_id = movie['id']
    title = movie['title']

    year = movie.get('year')

    print(f"\n🎬 Processing: {title} ({year or 'N/A'})")
    print(f"   DB ID: {movie_id}")

    # Fetch OTT data from JustWatch
    ott_links = fetch_ott_from_justwatch(title, year)

    if not ott_links:
        print(f"   ⚠️  No OTT data available")
        stats['no_data'] += 1
        return False

    # Save to database

    saved_count = save_ott_links(cursor, movie_id, ott_links)

    if saved_count > 0:
        print(f"   ✅ Added {saved_count} DIRECT OTT link(s)")
        for link in ott_links:
            url_preview = link['url'][:60] + "..." if len(link['url']) > 60 else link[
            quality = f" [{link['quality']}]" if link.get('quality') else ""
            print(f"      • {link['platform']} ({link['type']}){quality}")

            print(f"        {url_preview}")

        stats['success'] += 1
        stats['links_added'] += saved_count
        return True
    else:
        print(f"   ⚠️  No links saved")

        stats['no_data'] += 1
        return False

def main():
    """Main execution"""

    print("="*70)
    print("🎬 TFIVerse OTT Links Fetcher (JustWatch - DIRECT URLs)")



    print("="*70)
    print(f"Started at: {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}\n")

    try:

        conn = psycopg2.connect(DATABASE_URL, cursor_factory=RealDictCursor)
        cursor = conn.cursor()
        print("✅ Database connected\n")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ Database connection failed: {str(e)}")
        sys.exit(1)

    try:
        cursor.execute("""
            SELECT m.id, m.title, m.year
            FROM movies m
            WHERE NOT EXISTS (
                SELECT 1 FROM movie_ott_links ott 
                WHERE ott.movie_id = m.id

            )
            ORDER BY m.release_date DESC NULLS LAST
            LIMIT 5
        """)

        movies = cursor.fetchall()
        stats['total'] = len(movies)

        print(f"📊 Found {stats['total']} movies to process\n")

        if stats['total'] == 0:
            print("✨ All movies already have OTT data!")
            cursor.close()
            conn.close()

            return

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"❌ Query error: {str(e)}")
        cursor.close()
        conn.close()
        sys.exit(1)

    for i, movie in enumerate(movies, 1):
        print(f"\n{'='*70}")
        print(f"[{i}/{stats['total']}]")

        try:
            process_movie(cursor, movie)
            conn.commit()

        except Exception as e:
            print(f"   ❌ Error: {str(e)}")
            stats['errors'] += 1
            conn.rollback()
            continue

        time.sleep(2)  # Be nice to JustWatch



    print("\n" + "="*70)
    print("📊 SUMMARY")
    print("="*70)
    print(f"Total movies processed: {stats['total']}")

    print(f"✅ Success: {stats['success']}")
    print(f"⚠️  No data: {stats['no_data']}")
    print(f"❌ Errors: {stats['errors']}")
    print(f"📺 Total DIRECT OTT links added: {stats['links_added']}")
    print("="*70)
    print(f"Completed at: {datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')}")
    print("="*70)

    cursor.close()
    conn.close()
    print("\n✨ Done!")

if __name__ == "__main__":

    try:
        main()
    except KeyboardInterrupt:
        print("\n\n⚠️  Interrupted by user")
        sys.exit(0)
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"\n\n💥 Fatal error: {str(e)}")

        import traceback
        traceback.print_exc()
        sys.exit(1)
```

# **⚡ JUSTWATCH API LIMITS & BEST PRACTICES**

## **📊 Rate Limits (Unofficial API)**

Since JustWatch is **unofficial**, there are no published limits, but here's what's s

### **🔒 Conservative Limits (RECOMMENDED):**
- **Max:** 100-200 requests/hour

- **Delay:** 2-3 seconds between requests
- **Daily:** 1,000-2,000 requests max

### **⚠️ If You Go Too Fast:**
- IP ban (temporary, usually 1-24 hours)
- Empty responses
- Connection timeouts

### **✅ Safe Usage Strategy:**

```python
# Current script: 2 second delay ✅
time.sleep(2)

# For bulk processing:
if i % 50 == 0:  # Every 50 movies
    print("   ⏸️ Taking a 5-minute break...")
    time.sleep(300)  # 5 min cooldown
```

```typescript

import { db } from '@/lib/db';
import { movieOttLinks } from '@/lib/schema';
import { eq } from 'drizzle-orm';

export async function OTTSection({ movieId }: { movieId: number }) {
  const links = await db
    .select()

    .from(movieOttLinks)
    .where(eq(movieOttLinks.movieId, movieId))
    .where(eq(movieOttLinks.isAvailable, true));

  if (links.length === 0) {
    ```
    return <div>Not available for streaming</div>;

    ```
  }

  // Group by type
  const subscription = links.filter(l => l.type === 'subscription');
  const rental = links.filter(l => l.type === 'rent');
  const purchase = links.filter(l => l.type === 'buy');

  return (
    <div className="ott-section">
      ```
      <h3>Where to Watch</h3>
      ```

      {subscription.length > 0 && (
        <div className="ott-group">
          <h4>Stream</h4>
          {subscription.map(link => (
            <a 
              key={link.id} 
              href={link.url} 
              target="_blank"

              className="ott-button"
            >
              <img src={`/ott-logos/${link.platform}.png`} alt={link.platform} />
              <span>{link.platform}</span>
              {link.quality && <span className="quality">{link.quality}</span>}
            </a>
          ))}

        </div>
      )}

      {rental.length > 0 && (
        <div className="ott-group">
          <h4>Rent</h4>
          {rental.map(link => (

            <a key={link.id} href={link.url} target="_blank" className="ott-button">
              <img src={`/ott-logos/${link.platform}.png`} alt={link.platform} />



              <span>{link.platform}</span>
            </a>
          ))}
        </div>

      )}
    </div>
  );
}

```python
import argparse

parser = argparse.ArgumentParser()
parser.add_argument('--recent', action='store_true', help='Only fetch for recent mov
args = parser.parse_args()

if args.recent:
    cursor.execute("""
        SELECT m.id, m.title, m.year

        FROM movies m
        WHERE m.created_at > NOW() - INTERVAL '7 days'
        AND NOT EXISTS (
            SELECT 1 FROM movie_ott_links ott 
            WHERE ott.movie_id = m.id
        )
        ORDER BY m.created_at DESC

    """)

### **7. Build Analytics Dashboard**

```sql
-- See coverage by platform
SELECT 

    platform,
    COUNT(*) as movie_count,
    type
FROM movie_ott_links
GROUP BY platform, type
ORDER BY movie_count DESC;

-- Movies without OTT
SELECT COUNT(*) 
FROM movies m
WHERE NOT EXISTS (
    SELECT 1 FROM movie_ott_links ott WHERE ott.movie_id = m.id
);

### **9. Build "New on OTT" Feature**

```sql
SELECT m.*, ott.platform, ott.created_at as added_to_ott
FROM movies m
JOIN movie_ott_links ott ON m.id = ott.movie_id

WHERE ott.created_at > NOW() - INTERVAL '7 days'
ORDER BY ott.created_at DESC;
```
